/ /yepAdanakhaMbidhurmakurYaumUrdhenyastamadhiShThitairidAnIM/ / /gang gi zhabs sen zla ba'i me long dag /spyi bor bkod pa'i mod la byin rlabs kyi/ /nUtnAmr-itahAradAnadhIrairAbodhiShwadhibhUttareNapAletra/
bdud rtsi'i do shal gsar pa sbyin mkhas pa/ /khyab bdag bla mas byang chub bar du skyongs/ /

byams dang snying rje'i sprin dkar g.yos pa las/ /'gro kun dga' byed sdom gsum nor bu'i char/ /phab pas bdag blo'i shing rta 'gengs mdzad pa/ /bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho'i gtsug
rgyan phyag gi yul/ /e ma srid pa'i gdung ba kun sel zhing / /bde ba'i dpal skyed snang ba'i mchog sbyin pa/ /sngon med 'dren pa bdud rtsi'i 'byung gnas dang / /mtshungs
pa 'jig rten 'dir ni byung bar gyur/ /de yi yon tan mtha' ni kun gsal gyis/ /rang lus sngon por ma song de srid du/ /btsal yang de yi nges pa ma rnyed rung / /da dung 'tshol
ba'i ngal ba 'dzin pa 'dra/ /'on kyang nor bu'i gling nas ded dpon gyis/ /rin chen mtha' dag len par mi nus mod/ /cung zad res kyang 'dod rgu sbyin pa ltar/ /skal bzang
dga' ba bskyed phyir cha tsam brjod/ /spyi don gnyis pa dus gsum gyi rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa rnams kyi gsang gsum gcig tu bsdus pa'i ngo bo/ /lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig
rten thams cad kyi ral pa'i thor tshugs indra nI la'i mdog lta bus lan cig ma yin par yang nas yang du btud pa'i skyabs kyi mchog tu gyur pa/ shes bya'i chos thams cad
la thogs pa med pa'i mkhyen rab kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu rgyas pa/ 'gro ba rnams la rjes su chags pa'i snying rje'i 'od zer ring por 'phro ba/ sgrib gnyis kyi mun pa stug
po thams cad yongs su 'jil ba/ 'khor ba'i chu gter mtha' dag skem par byed pa/ mngon mtho dang nges legs kyi lam gsal bar byed pa/ gsol ba btab na mchog dang thun mong gi
dngos grub kyi snang ba bde blag tu ster bar byed pa/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'dren mchog smra ba'i nyi ma mtshan brjod par dka' ba/ don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na/
dpal e waM chos ldan gyi mkhan rabs zhe drug pa mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin

bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes yongs su grags pa'i mtshan snyan gyi rgyal rngas phyogs kyi khor yug kun tu khyab par gyur pa gang de'i rnam par thar pa
skye bo tha mal pa rnams kyi blo ngor snang ba de mdor tsam zhig brjod par bya ste/ de la bdun/ thog mar sems can gyi don du sku'i skye ba bzhes nas gzhon nu rol rtsed
mdzad pa'i tshul/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che'i sgor zhugs nas rgyud sdom pa gsum ldan du mdzad pa'i tshul/ zhugs pa'i rten des thos bsam sgom gsum ji ltar mdzad pa'i
tshul/ phrin las kyi gtso bo bstan pa dang sems can gyi don rlabs po che ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i grub 'bras bstan 'dzin gyi slob ma ji tsam
byung ba'i tshul/ sdom pa gsum la gces spras su mdzad cing nyams rtogs ji ltar 'khrungs pa'i tshul bye brag tu bshad pa/ mthar gdul bya rtag 'dzin can rnams chos la bskul
ba'i ched du gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos kyi dbyings su bsdus pa'i tshul bshad pa'o/ /de la dang po sems can gyi don du sku'i skye ba bzhes nas gzhon nu rol rtsed mdzad pa'i
tshul ni/ bdag gi bla ma 'phags pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mi rnams kyi bla mar gyur pa/ 'jig rten na 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po zhes yongs su grags pa de'i zhal snga
nas mdzad pa'i mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po 'di'i rnam thar gsol 'debs byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i sprin mdzes zhes bya ba las/ rdo rje 'chang dbang ye shes las byung
ba'i/ /byams pa'i thugs rjes 'gro rnams sgrol ba'i slad/ /kun dga'i mtshan dper shar ba'i sgyu 'phrul gyis/ /bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin la gsol ba 'debs/ /mgon khyod
gdod nas zhi ba mchog brnyes kyang / /rmad byung snying rje'i bdud rtsi'i dpyid dpal gyis/ /dam pas bsngags pa'i rigs kyi dga' tshal du/ /gzugs sku'i ljon bzang 'khrungs
la gsol ba

'debs/ /thog ma nyid nas nges par 'byung ba dang / /rig dang brtse ba'i me tog mdzes 'bar bas/ /phyogs bral dpyod ldan 'dus pa'i tshogs rnams kyi/ /brtan pa gcig car 'phrog
la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po 'di ni bskal pa dpag tu med pa'i sngon rol nas mngon par
rdzogs par sangs rgyas su zin na'ang sngon gyi smon lam dang snying rje'i dbang gis 'khor ba ji srid gnas pa de srid du sprul pa sna tshogs pa'i sgo nas sems can gyi don
rgyun mi 'chad par mdzad pa las/ re zhig kha ba can gyi gdul bya rnams la thugs lhag par brtse bas so so skye bo'i rdo rje slob dpon gyi rnam rol tu ston par bzhed de/
de la 'di'i 'khrungs pa'i yul ni/ snyigs dus kyi rdo rje 'chang gnyis pa ngor chen kun dga' bzang pos phyag btab pa'i gnas mchog /yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal
e wa~M chos ldan dang nye ba'i sa'i cha/ rin po che marga ta'i kha dog 'dzin pa'i ljon shing gi ra bas mdzes par spud pa'i khrod na bya dang bung ba mang pos snyan pa'i
ngag gi gling bu sgyur ba/ gtsang zhing bsil ba'i chu rgyun du ma phyogs tha dad du babs pa las lhung lhung gi sgra snyan par sgrogs pa sogs mdor na sngon bsags legs byas
kyi mthu phun sum tshogs pa'i bdag po'i 'bras bu yongs su smin pa'i gnas/ bkra shis shing dge mtshan du mas legs par gtams pa'i rtse na rgya mtsho gling zhes par/ rje
'di'i yab ni mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med dang yab yum gcig pa'i sku mched padma don grub ces bya ba/ rigs gzugs phun sum tshogs shing stobs
dang dpa' rtsal gyi phul du son pa/ 'jig rten lugs kyi bstan bcos mtha' dag la mkhas pa de dang / yum ni gnas grongs la sgang zhes pa sger ba rta rkyang zhig gi rigs las

byon pa'i lugs gnyis kyi shes bya thams cad la blo gros gsal zhing / ngo tsha dang khrel yod kyis brgyan pa/ dad pa dang phan sems che ba la sogs pa ya rabs kyi yon tan mang
pos mdzes par spud pa padma bu khrid ces bya ba de yin la/ de la sras drug dang sras mo lnga ste bcu gcig tsam yod pa las/ sras thams cad kyi thog mar gyur pa ni bdag cag
gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa yon tan rin po che'i phung por gyur pa 'di yin la/ de'i 'og ma ni khyim la gnas shing phan sems kyi me tog bkra ba padma sum legs zhes bya ba
dang / de'i 'og ma ni bdag cag gi bla ma mkhas dang grub pa yongs kyi gtsug rgyan rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang / de'i 'og ma ni bsod nams dang dbang
thang gi ljon pa rgyas shing / mkhyen rab kyi lo 'dab yongs su grol ba mdzod pa nor ldan shes rab bzang po pa dang / de'i 'og ma ni khyim pa'i brtul zhugs 'dzin pa rgyal
po tshe ring zhes bya ba dang / de 'og sras thams cad kyi tha chung du gyur pa ni dran dbang gi me long rab tu gsal ba rje drung bzang po blo gros su grags pa'o/ /de lta
bu'i sras rnams kyi thog mar gyur pa bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po 'di ni dang po yum gyi lhums su zhugs pa'i tshe'ang ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas mang du byung zhing / de nas ji srid phyir ma btsas kyi bar du yum la rmi ltas bzang zhing / lus shing bal gyi 'dab ma ltar yang ba dang / zo mdog rgyas
pa dang / khyim gyi 'byor pa 'phel ba la sogs pa dge zhing bkra shis pa'i ltas mang po mngon sum du byung bar gyur la/ de nas zla grangs rdzogs te rab byung bcu gsum pa'i
nang gses 'phags pa'i yul na du rmu kha zhes pa bod skad du gdong ngan te ljongs 'dir dbang thang dang bstun pa'i ming me pho spre'u'i lor/ yum la gnod pa med cing ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas mang po dang bcas

te bde bar sku bltams par gyur to/ /de ltar bltams pa'i khye'u de ni gzugs mdzes shing lta na sdug la brjid chags pa/ ston ka'i zla ba dri ma med pa ltar kha dog dkar zhing
snum pa skyes bu chen po'i mtshan dang ldan pas skye bo mtha' dag gi yid kyi brtan pa dbang med du 'phrog pa zhig yod la/ yab yum rnams kyis mtshan padma rdo rje zhes bya
bar gsol to/ /de lta bu'i gzhon nu de ni bskal pa dpag tu med pa nas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rlabs po che la goms pa brtas pa'i shugs kyis gsung sgros smra mi mkhyen
pa'i dus su'ang ma Ni sgra dag par rtag tu gsung ba dang / dgung grangs bzhi lnga tsam bzhes pa'i tshe/ yab yum gyi mdzo mo zhig brlag pa ji tsam btsal kyang ma rnyed
pa la/ rje 'dis phyag mdzub gtad de ri pha ki'i rgyab na yod gsungs pa bzhin du rnyed pa sogs mngon shes kyang gsal bar mnga' ba dang / khyad par du yang mgon po byams
pas/ sbyor ba'i sngon du snying rje dang / /mos pa dang ni bzod pa dang / /dge ba yang dag spyod pa ni/ /rigs kyi rtags su shes par bya/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar theg pa chen
po'i rigs sad pa'i stobs kyis nye ring med pa'i sems can thams cad la tshad med pa'i snying rje mnga' zhing / mgon med pa dang / skyabs med pa dang / dpung gnyen med pa'i
'gro ba nyam thag pa gzigs pa'am gsan pa'i tshe rang dbang med par spyan chab ldang ba dang / sems can gsod pa sogs kyi gtam gsan pa'am/ yang na de dag gi sha khrag sogs
gzigs pa'i tshe mi bzod pa'i snying rje shugs drag po skyes pa'i stobs kyis spyan chab lhung zhing / nyin grangs mang po'i bar du gsol chas kyi dwang ga'ang 'gags 'gro
ba zhig yod pa yin te/ nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po 'di'i zhal snga nas/ nged na so shin tu phra ba'i skabs su'ang

sems can gsod pa'i gtam thos pa tsam gyis mig nas mchi ma rang dbang med par shor zhing / nyin grangs mang po'i bar du zas la dwang ga 'gags 'gro ba zhig yod pa yin/ de la
brten nas byis pa gzhan rnams kyis rtsed mo'i phyir du 'bu dang sbrang ma la sogs pa gsod par byed kyang / nged nas de 'dra bsad pa ye mi dran/ 'di la bltas nas tshe snga
ma'ang ston mchog shAkya'i rgyal po'i bstan pa rin po che'i sgor zhugs nas byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa la goms 'dris cung zad byas pa 'dra zhes bka' stsal pa bdag nyid
kyis thos la/ gzhan yang bla ma dang sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa'i sku gzugs 'jim pa las grub pa sogs rnyed tshad bsdus te gnas dben par stegs gtsang ma'i steng du bzhugs
su gsol zhing / de la mgron bu la sogs pa'i dngos po byung tshad thams cad 'bul ba dang / dar gos rnyed tshad kyi na bza' gsol ba dang / phyag dang yon chab 'bul ba
la sogs pa chos dang mthun pa'i bya ba 'ba' zhig gis dus 'da' bar mdzad pa dang / mngon par rtogs pa rgyan las/ gos la sogs pa gtsang ba dang / /lus la srin bu rnams mi
'byung / /zhes sbyor lam rtse mo la gnas pa'i rtags su bshad pa dang mthun par gtsang sbra che zhing / sku lus la srin bu med pa sogs dam pa'i yon tan du ma dang ldan zhing
/ rgan pa la gus pa dang / gzhon pa la byams pa sogs ya rabs kyi spyod pa dang ldan pas skye rgu thams cad shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i gnas la bkod par gyur to zhes thos so/
/skabs shig bar chad kyi rnam pas yul der gzhung gi rnga mo mgo ba sleb pa na/ byis pa thams cad ri bong cal rgyug gi tshul du rnga mo sleb yong zhes sgrogs shing phyogs
thams cad du bros pa na/ rje 'dis kyang de bzhin du mdzad pas/ khang pa thog tshad gcig tsam gyi g.yang du sku lhung ba'i rkyen gyis snyan gyi dbang por

cung zad skyon shor ba lta bus de phyin chad snyan gyis cher mi gsan par gyur pa yin zhes thos la/ de dag ni shin tu snyigs ma'i dus 'dir dkar phyogs rnams pham/ nag phyogs
rnams rgyal ba'i skabs su song gshis bdud kyi rigs kyis bar chad byed par brtsams kyang / rje 'di ni bskal pa dpag tu med pa nas gzhan la sman pa'i thugs bskyed kyi g.yar
dam brtan pa'i stobs kyis snyan la skyon cung zad byung ba tsam las/ gzhan pa'i bar chad kyis glags ma rnyed par sems so/ /dgung lo lnga pa kun ldan gyi lor bdag chen 'jam
pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros yab sras rnams dbus phebs mdzad pa'i yar lam ngor du phebs/ dgon pa'i phyi rol du tshe dbang zhig stsal ba rje 'di yab yum dang
bcas pa gsan du byon pas sku tshe la mnga' brnyes pa'i rten 'brel gyi thog ma'ang 'di dus nas 'grig par mngon no/ /rgyal rnams dgongs pa'i snying po ni/ /'gro kun srid
las sgrol ba ste/ /nyi zla'i 'od kyi byed las kyang / /mun pa'i smag rum kho na sel/ /de slad sprul pa sna tshogs kyis/ /'gro ba'i re 'dod skong ba ni/ /dpag bsam shing
dang bum pa bzang / /bsam 'phel nor bus mtshon ma gyur/ /khyad par bsil ldan ljongs kyi 'gro/ /thar pa'i grong du dbugs dbyung slad/ /skyob pa rnams kyi ye shes kyang /
/mtshan dpe'i gzugs su sprul la chas/ /e ma dge mtshan rgya mtsho yis/ /mdzes par 'khyud pa'i gling 'di ni/ /sprul pa'i sku de 'khrungs yul du/ /byed pos gsar du bskrun min
nam/ /shin tu ngo mtshar ltas rnams kyis/ /yongs su bskor te smin legs ma'i/ /lus kyi gzhal med khang pa ru/ /'jug pa'i dus ston gsar pa shar/ /'phags rnams dman pa'i
lto ba na/ /gzhar yang gnas pa ma yin te/ /seng ge'i 'o ma rin chen las/ /gzhan pa'i snod du

chags nus sam/ /de phyir mi yi cha byad las/ /rab 'das lha mo'i dpal 'dzin ma/ /bzhin bzang ma khyod rgyal ba'i sras/ /bskyed phyir 'phags ma'i sprul par nges/ /de nas dus
la bab pa na/ /mdzes pa'i cha shas kun rdzogs shing / /snang bas mun 'phrog gdung sel zla/ /'gro 'di'i bsod nams skal bas rnyed/ /rab mdzes me tog padma dkar/ /mtshan dang
dpe byad kyis spras shing / /chos kyi bag chags dang ldan na/ /gzhon nu 'di yi dpe zlar 'os/ /rgyal la bsnyen bsrid mi mnga' yang / /gangs ljongs lha ni 'di'o zhes/ /ston
phyir gsung gi thog ma ru/ /yi ge drug pa dbyangs su len/ /bskal pa dpag tu med pa nas/ /tshogs gnyis rdzogs pa'i mthar son kyang / /da dung rgyal ba'i sku brnyan la/
/mchod pa'i ltad mo ci yang ston/ /sgrib gnyis g.ya' yis ma gos pa'i/ /ye shes me long dag pa'i ngos/ /shes bya'i gzugs kun shar ba la/ /mngon par shes pa'i grags pa dkar/
/rang gi ma la su yang brtse/ /'byor ldan rnams la kun kyang dga'/ /rgyal po la ni thams cad btud/ /dman la byams pa khyod kho na/ /na tshod phra mo'i dus 'dir yang / /mgon
med rnams kyi mgon gyur na/ /da gzod dar la babs pa'i tshe/ /kun gyi skyabs su 'gyur bar nges/ /khyod ni ris med lus can la/ /phan bde'i bdud rtsi rab stsol yang / /yid
srubs dpung dang bcas pa yi/ /snying la mya ngan zug rngu sbyin/ /de slad bar du gcod brtsams kyang / /glags rnyed 'gyur ba ga la nus/ /de bas 'di la skyabs song na/
/khyed rnams bde la 'god par nges/ /brtan par btsugs so 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ /'chi med mgon po'i skur bzhengs te/ /gzhon nu'i tshe yi ka ba ni/ /'gyur du med pa'i rang bzhin
du'o// //spyi don gnyis pa rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che'i sgor

zhugs nas rgyud sdom pa gsum ldan du mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ rtsod dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i rje 'di'i rnam
thar gsol 'debs byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i sprin mdzes zhes bya ba las/ rdo rje 'chang dngos nam mkha'i mtshan can las/ /sdom pa gsum gyi bka' drin legs nos shing / /zab
rgyas sde snod rgyud sde rgya mtsho yi/ /smin grol lam bzang gsan la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs shing / de'ang 'di ltar rjes su thos te/ bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam
pa gzhal du med pa'i yon tan du ma la dbang bsgyur ba 'di ni gzhon nu'i dus nas chos kyi bag chags shin tu mthug pa'i stobs kyis/ skye bo phal che bas kyang nges par bstan
pa 'dzin pa'i khyu mchog chen po nyid du 'gyur bar gdon mi za bar sems la/ khyad par mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med kyi zhal snga nas/ gzhon nu
'di chos byas na nges par bstan pa la phan thogs shin tu che bar 'ong ba'i bka' mchid dbyangs kyi rgyal mo'i rgyud mangs nas drangs pa lta bu rna ba'i bcud du stsal bas rkyen
byas te/ dgung lo drug pa lcags mo glang gi lor/ dper na skyes bu skom pas gdung ba 'ga' zhig shin tu gtsang zhing bsil ba'i chu rgyun yid la byed cing 'gro ba bzhin
du/ yab dang lhan cig snga na med pa'i dga' ba dang spro ba'i 'dzum rlabs gsar pa khong nas dgod bzhin pa'i ngang nas yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal e wa~M
chos ldan gyi bla brang thar pa rtser phebs/ de'i tshe gzhan dag gis gser zangs kyi ganydzir dang / rgyal mtshan rnams bstan te 'di rnams ci yin zhes dris pa na/ sngon nas
gsan ma myong yang 'di dag ni gser zangs las grub pa'i ganydzi ra dang / rgyal mtshan no gsungs pas/ thams cad kyis na tshod phra mo 'di lta bus 'di 'dra shes pa

zer zhing ngo mtshar du 'dzin pa byung / de nas mi 'phrogs pa'i mkhyen rab phul du phyin pa'i me tog bkra zhing / thugs rje'i yal ga ring por rkyong pas skye rgu thams cad
kyi re ba yongs su 'gengs pa'i rnam 'dren dpag bsam gyi ljon pa mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med kyi zhabs pad legs par bsten cing / gus pa'i kun spyod
kyis mnyes par byas te/ yi ge'i phyi mo nas bzung 'bri klog sogs bka' khrid zhus pa tsam gyis tshegs med du mkhyen/ de nas dgung lo bco lnga'i bar la e wa~M pa'i 'don
chog yongs su rdzogs pa thugs 'dzin dang / de dag gi go don dang cho ga'i phyag len tha na gdangs dbyangs tshun chad dpyis phyin par mdzad/ khyad par sa paNDita chen pos
mdzad pa'i bstan bcos sdom gsum rab dbye/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i rgyud bshad kyi sngon 'gro tshul gsum mdzes rgyan dang / rgyud kyi mngon par rtogs pa ljon
shing mdzes rgyan/ dpal kye rdo rje'i rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa ste ngor pa'i gzhung chung bzhir grags pa dang / rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i gsung
ngag lam 'bras kyi sngon 'gro snang gsum mdzes rgyan/ dngos gzhi rgyud gsum mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan bcas thugs 'dzin gnang ste e wa~M bla brang du rgyugs 'bul bar mdzad/
e wa~M du lo dar bzhin bde kye gsang gsum gyi rgyud nas bstan pa'i bla med kyi dkyil 'khor chen po lnga'i sgrub mchod mdzad pa'i nang tshan bde mchog lU nag gi cho ga'ang
lo bzhi tsam gyi bar du gtong bar mdzad/ de nas dgung grangs bco lngar son pa lcags khyi lor/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med sa skyar khri mjal
la phebs pa dang lhan cig /rje 'di'ang bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen por phebs te/ der bzhugs pa'i bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku ngo

khag dang / rten gsum thams cad zhib par mjal/ khyad par khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos 'jam mgon dbang sdud snying por rje 'di la mtshan zhig stsal dgos pa'i snyan
sgron phul ba na/ des kyang thugs dgyes pa'i 'dzum dkar g.yo bzhin pa'i ngang nas mtshan byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin zhes bya bar 'dogs par mdzad do/ /de nas rang gnas
e wa~M chos ldan du phebs shing khyim gyi bde 'byor la chags pa ni thar pa'i go skabs med pa'i me 'obs stug po'i nang na gnas pa lta bu dang / rab tu byung ba rnams ni
bsil khang na gnas pa lta bu'i 'du shes 'khrungs shing / khyad par du'ang 'phags mchog klu sgrub kyis/ khrims ni rgyu dang mi rgyu'i sa bzhin du/ /yon tan kun gyi gzhi
rten lags par gsungs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar yon tan kun gyi gzhir gyur pa ni tshul khrims kyi bslab pa nyid yin par dgongs te/ mdor na nges par 'byung ba'i thugs kyi kun slong
rnam par dag pas kun nas bslangs te lo der de dus gangs khrod kyi 'dul ba 'dzin pa rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu lta bur gyur pa khu bo mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa chen
por mkhan po zhus shing / gzhan yang las byed pa'i dge slong grangs tshang pa'i dbus su yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa dang / khyim pa'i rtags thams cad mchil ma'i
thal ba ltar bor te rab tu byung ba'i rtags dang cha lugs la sogs pa yang dag par len pa bar ma rab byung sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas dngos gzhi dge tshul gyi sdom pa rnam
par dag pa legs par bzhes par mdzad do/ /de phyin chad 'di snang srid pa'i bsam sbyor mtha' dag dug can gyi kha zas bzhin du rgyang ring du dor nas/ rang gzhan gyi don
du rnam par grol ba'i yon tan kho na don du gnyer ba'i sgo nas/ ji skad du kA ri ka sum brgya pa las/ gang zhig srog

gcod gzhan gyi nor 'phrog dang / /mi tshangs spyod rdzun bcos pa'i chang la sogs/ /gar sogs phreng sogs mal che mtho ba dang / /phyi dro'i kha zas dngul nyid spong ba ni/ /nyon
mongs dgra g.yul rgyal byed tshul khrims te/ /dge tshul brtul zhugs chu lon brtsigs pa dang / /'chi ba'i mche ba 'byin par byed pa'i thabs/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub dpal
nod dbang bskur yin/ /zhes pa ltar gyi dge tshul gyi bslab pa'i gzhi bcu char gtogs dang bcas pa mtha' dag phra zhing phra ba nas mig 'bras bzhin du srung bar mdzad do/
/byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa ni khu bo mkhan chen byang chub sems dpa' de nyid kyi drung nas kyang brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed gsan cing / gzhan
yang rgyal ba'i sras po ngag dbang bstan pa rin chen sogs las brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed gsan te/ de phyin chad nag po'i chos bzhi spong zhing de'i
gnyen por dkar po'i chos bzhi sgrub pa dang / gzhan yang pham pa lta bu'i chos bzhi dang / nyes byas bzhi bcu zhe drug dang / nam mkha'i snying po'i mdo las gsungs pa'i
byang chub sems dpa' rgyal po la 'byung ba'i ltung ba gcig /blon po la 'byung ba'i ltung ba gcig /rgyal blon thun mong du 'byung ba bzhi/ byang chub sems dpa' las dang po
pa la 'byung ba brgyad dang bcas pa thams cad kyang srung sdom gyi ra ba las nam yang mi 'da' bar mdzad pa yin no/ /gsang ba sngags kyi sdom pa ni/ gnas skabs de nyid du
rigs dang dkyil 'khor kun gyi khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa' dang dbyer ma mchis pa khu bo mkhan chen de nyid kyi drung nas/ rgyud ma smin pa smin par byed pa dpal kye rdo
rje man ngag lugs kyi dbang bskur ba legs par gsan cing / gzhir gnas pa'i rdo rje bzhi la sku bzhi'i sa bon btab ste/ dbang gis mtshon

pa'i ye shes mngon du gyur pa'i tshul gyis brjod bral lhan cig skyes pa nang gi sdom pa thob par mdzad la/ de phyin chad dbang bzhi po re re la'ang mnyam rjes bza' bsrung mi
'bral ba'i dam tshig lnga lnga ste nyi shu dang / khyad par bum dbang gi bsrung ba'i dam tshig rtsa ba'i ltung ba bcu bzhi/ yan lag gi ltung ba brgyad dang bcas pa rnams
la srung sdom rnam par dag pa'i sgo nas dam tshig phra zhing phra ba'ang nyams pa'i go skabs mi srid pa yin no/ /gzhan yang mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi drung
nas/ dpal kye rdo rje'i lus dkyil gyi dbang bskur ba dang / grub chen dze tA ris bkral ba'i bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi gtso bo tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang
bskur ba dang / ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i rgyud nas bstan zhing grub chen kun snying gis bkral ba'i rjes su 'brang ba kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor lha so
bdun mgron thabs kyi lha dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / 'phags mchog klu sgrub zhabs kyis bkral ba'i gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje lha so gnyis
kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / slob dpon nag po spyod pas mngal skyes sbyong byed du bkral ba'i 'khor lo bde mchog lha drug cu rtsa gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang
bskur ba dang / grub chen thang stong pa'i lugs kyi tshe rta zung 'brel gyi dbang dang / de'i yig cha sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis kyis mdzad pa'i lung la sogs pa
nyer mkho 'ga' zhig dang / ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i lam 'bras tshogs bshad kyi khrid yig gi lung la sogs pa gsan pa yin no/ /de lo bal bod dmag 'khrugs
kyi rkyen gyis dbus gtsang thams cad du 'brum nad byung bar brten/ rje 'di yang sku 'brum gyis sku brnyel tshul bzhes kyang / slar rim gyis zla ba sprin las grol

ba bzhin du je dwangs su gyur cing / mthar sku gzugs kyi 'phrod bzhes su skyid mkhar du chu tshan zhig la phebs pa yin no zhes thos so/ /de nas khu bo mkhan chen mchog gis
rje 'di la kun tu dgos pa'i gzhung bdun gzigs dgos tshul gyi bka' stsal phebs shing / de'i do dam slob dpon du byams pa bsod nams dpal 'byor bsko bzhag bskyangs pa ltar thugs
brtson chen po'i sgo nas legs par gzigs te/ dgung lo bcu bdun yan chad du rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i 'grel pa dag ldan gyi mjug tu/ rgyud sde'i dum bu rnam gzhag
mngon rtogs dang / stong thun rnams kyi don bsdus bstod pa gnyis/ /bdag med bstod pa'i rnam 'grel dang bcas pa/ /kun tu dgos pa'i gzhung bdun 'thor mi bya/ /zhes gsungs
pa ltar gyi rgyud spyi la dgos pa'i gzhung bdun po thugs la bzung nas e wa~M bla brang du rgyugs 'bul ba sogs mdzad do/ /spyir rje 'di ni skuu na chung ngu'i dus nas gzhan
stobs kyi skul ma sogs la rag ma las par/ rang stobs kyi brtson 'grus thang lhod med pa zhig dang / thugs rab kyang 'jam mgon sa paNDi ta chen pos mdzad pa'i mgon po
'jam pa'i rdo rje la mchod par brjod pa/ dpal ldan blo gros dhIHlas byung ba tshar bdun bsgrags pas thugs la zin pa sogs gang ci nas phun sum tshogs pa zhig mnga' ba yin
no zhes thos so/ /de nas dgung grangs bco brgyad pa chu mo glang gi lor/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa la zhugs kyang yongs suu ma rdzogs pa ni so thar gyi las bsgrub pa dang las kyi
cho ga la mi dbang zhing / de la mi dbang bas gsang sngags kyi rgyud ston pa dang dbang bskur ba sogs kyi rdo rje slob dpon khyad par can du mi 'gyur bar dgongs nas/ so
thar rigs brgyad kyi nang nas mchog tu gyur pa dge slong gi dngos por bsgrub par bzhed nas/ dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi

bla brang gzhung du mtshan brjod par dka' ba don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na/ mkhan po brtan mkhas kyi yon tan du ma la dbang bsgyur ba byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med bkra
shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po dang / las kyi slob dpon legs par gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba la mkhas shing / de'i bslab pa'i gnas mtha' dag ston pa la rnam dpyod
kyi mgrin pa yangs pa dpon slob rin po che ngag dbang dam chos pa dang / gsang ste ston pa'i slob dpon gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa bsod nams tshul khrims la sogs pa dad
pa'i dge 'dun bcu'i dbus su rje 'di dang phan khang zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang bstan pa rin chen gnyis kyis bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi sdom pa rnam par dag
pa legs par bzhes par mdzad do/ /de'i tshe skyes bu dam pa 'di rab tu byung bas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang lha'i phyogs ni zla ba yar gyi ngo bzhin du 'phel bar gyur
la/ nag po'i phyogs dang lha ma yin rnams ni mar gyi ngo bzhin du 'grib par gyur to/ /de lta bu'i snyan pa'i grags pas sa'i steng thams cad khyab par gyur cing / sa bla'i
lha rnams kyis rgyal chen ris bzhi pa'i lha rnams dang / rgyal chen ris bzhi pa rnams kyis sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams la bsgrags shing / de bzhin du 'og min gyi bar du bsgrags
par gyur te/ mdo dran pa nye bar gzhag pa las skyes bu dam pa rnams rab tu byung ba'i tshe 'di lta bu 'byung bar bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /dus de nyid nas bzung ste bsnyen
par rdzogs nas lo brgya lon pa'i dge slong gi dngos po dang 'dra bar gyur te zhi zhing dul la bag yod pa'i sgo nas ltung ba sde lnga char gtogs dang bcas pa'i dri ma
mtha' dag dang bral zhing / gnyen po'i khrims nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa gsum char gtogs dang bcas pa las nam

yang mi 'da' bar bzhugs pa yin no/ /gzhon nu nyid nas byang sems kyi/ /rlabs chen spyod pas 'khyud pa yi/ /snyan grags utpal dkar po'i phreng / /phyogs kyi bu mo'i rgyan du
byin/ /de mthong skye bo phal mo che'i/ /ngag la dbyangs can zhugs pa bzhin/ /bstod pa'i rol mo 'bum 'khrol ba/ /dri za'i phang 'gro'i glu las snyan/ /shes bya nam mkha'
dang mnyam pa/ /thugs chud 'chi med sar 'dzegs des/ /lung bstan gling bu bsgyur ba'i mod/ /phan bde'i 'dod pa 'grub la nye/ /gangs ljongs 'gro ba'i bsod nams kyi/ /rin chen
rdul mang las grub pa'i/ /e wa~M chos kyi pho brang ni/ /sa la 'og min 'phos pa bzhin/ /rgyal ba las kyang rnyed dka' ba'i/ /gsang sngags chos kyi mdzod gyur pa/ /gang
der son pa tsam gyis kyang / /'khor ba'i nad kun zhi bar byed/ /de lta'i longs spyod rdzogs zhing der/ /padma'i mtsho la ngang mo bzhin/ /zhugs pas srid pa hrul po ru/
/byed pa'i sta gon thog mar brtsams/ /gzod nas thams cad mkhyen zin kyang / /'gro 'di'i don slad yi ge nas/ /rgyud kyi rgyal po gnyis med bar/ /rnam dpyod blo yi mdzod du
bcug /mthong ba tsam gyi chu klung gis/ /sgrib pa'i dri ma kun 'khrud pa/ /dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa che/ /dad pa'i spyan gyi bdud rtsir byas/ /khyad par srid pa'i bde
ba la/ /chags pa'i mdud pa rab bkrol nas/ /rnam grol gling du bgrod pa'i phyir/ /so thar sdom pa'i shing rtar zhugs/ /yang cig theg chen sems bskyed kyi/ /sdom pa'i go
cha rab gyon nas/ /byang chub sems kyi mtshon rnon pos/ /bdag tu 'dzin pa'i dgra tshogs bcom/ /des kyang blo gros ma tshim par/ /gsang sngags sdom pa'i rkang mgyogs kyis/
/bcu gsum rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sar/ /tshe 'dir bgrod pa'i mthu ldan byas/ /chu bo'i rgyun las me lce dang / /zla ba'i zer las dug bzhin du/ /khyod

las sdom gsum dang 'gal ba'i/ /nyes byas phra mo'ang 'byung mi srid/ /e ma bsnyen par rdzogs pa yi/ /nor bu'i khri 'phang la 'khod pa'i/ /grags pa'i gdugs dkar g.yo ba des/
/srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar du khyab// //spyi don gsum pa zhugs pa'i rten des thos bsam sgom gsum ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ bdag gi bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i rje 'di'i rnam thar gsol 'debs byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i sprin mdzes las/ gzhan yang ris med dge ba'i bshes gnyen mchog /nyi shu rtsa
bzhi gus pas nyer bsten nas/ /mang du thos dang bsam pa'i shes rab kyis/ /mkhas rnams dgyes pa bskyed der gsol ba 'debs/ /dam pas byin rlabs dben pa'i sgrub gnas su/ /thun
mong lam gyi rim pas rgyud sbyangs nas/ /bskyed rdzogs rnal 'byor zab mos lhan skyes kyi/ /ye shes rgyas par mdzad la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar rgyal ba'i bstan
pa la zhugs pa rnams kyi mngon par rtogs pa ni/ rgyal ba'i sras po ma pham pas mdo sde'i rgyan las/ 'di na dang por thos pa la brten tshul bzhin yid la byed pa 'byung
/ tshul bzhin yid la byed pa la yang yang dag don yul ye shes 'byung / zhes gsungs pa ltar tshogs lam gyi skabs su gzhung lugs rnams la thos bsam sgom gsum byas pa la brten
nas/ de nyid goms pa'i tshul gyis bsam byung dang 'jig rten pa'i bsgoms byung gi shes rab sbyor lam nges 'byed cha mthun bzhi la rim gyis 'byung zhing / de la brten nas
mthong lam sa dang po'i rtogs pa mngon du gyur pa'i tshe/ yang dag pa'i ye shes kyi cha shas tshes gcig zla ba lta bu mthong bar 'gyur la/ de nyid sgom lam gyi gnas skabs
rnams su rim

gyis je gsal du song nas/ mthar thug spang bya las grol zhing chos dang chos can gyi gnas lugs ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs pa'i so so rang gis rig pa'i ye shes zla ba'i dkyil
'khor nya gang ba lta bu rtogs pa la sangs rgyas su 'jog pa'i phyir ro/ /der ma zad da ltar gyi gnas skabs su'ang thos pa la ma brten par bsam pa mi 'byung zhing / de gnyis
med par sgom pas nyams su len mi shes pa yin no/ /khyad par gsang sngags kyi dbang bskur ba rnams ni thob pa tsam gyis bskal pa dpag tu med pa nas bsags pa'i sdig sgrib
mang po 'dag nus pas 'di la nan tan du bya dgos pa yin no zhes shes pa'i ched du rang nyid kyang de'i rjes su slob par bzhed nas/ thog mar bstan pa'i snang byed dam pa
'dam thog chos rje bla ma rin chen grags pa las/ jo bo nas brgyud pa'i man ngag phra mo rnams snar thang gi mkhan chen mchims nam mkha' grags kyis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs
pa'i mngon rtogs brgya rtsar grags pa las byung ba'i rjes gnang sum cu so bzhi dang / de'i yig cha zhu chen gyis mdzad pa'i lung / rnal 'byor gyi rgyud ngan song sbyong ba'i
brtag pa las gsungs pa'i phyag rdor 'chi bdag 'joms pa lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba bcas dang / mkhas grub rgya mtsho'i gtsug rgyan mkhan chen ngag dbang
dam chos las/ kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi dbang dang / gser chos 'jam dpal nag po'i rjes su gnang ba bcas dang / rgya chen chos kyi spyan ldan spang shar bla ma ngag dbang
dpal bzang las/ grwa mngon lugs kyi dzaM dmar gyi las tshogs a rA gas mdzad pa dang / des mdzad pa'i mi 'gyur rdo rje'i gter ka nas byung ba'i dzaM lha nyer gcig gi g.yang
skyabs la sogs pa'i lung bcas gsan/ rje 'di dgung lo bco brgyad du son pa'i lo mjug der/ khu bo mkhan chen mchog gis e waM bla brang gzhung gi mkhan

sa bla brang phun tshogs khang sar la rtsis gnang nas/ rje 'di dgung lo bcu dgur son pa shing stag lor khu bo mkhan chen dam pa mdo khams su bstan 'gro'i don la chibs bskyod
bskyangs par brten/ de skor gyi thugs brel rnams bcad de rim gyis phyag dpe'i skor la gzigs rtog rgya cher bskyangs/ de skabs gong du byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med kyi rnam
thar du gsal ba ltar e waM pa'i mkhan sa bla khag rnams res bskor gyis mdzad pas/ rje 'di dgung grangs nyer gcig tu son pa me pho 'brug gi lor e wa~M bla brang gzhung
phan khang nas rtsis bzhes te/ bka' chos rnams mdo sngags smra ba'i khyu mchog ngag dbang bstan pa rin chen pas stsal ba rnams rje 'dis gsan par mdzad de/ de'ang sgrub thabs
brgya rtsa nas byung ba'i lo gyon ma'i rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas/ mkhas pa'i dbang po ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rje'i yig steng nas/ 'phags yul gyi grub pa'i
'khor los sgyur ba 'jigs bral bi rU pa'i thugs bcud gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras tshogs bshad du grags pa'i sngon 'gro snang ba gsum gyi khrid dang / de'i skabs kyi
snga chos su e wa~M pa'i chos spyod dum bu gsum kha skong dang bcas pa'i lung / de rjes brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed/ de nas slob ma rjes 'dzin sogs
dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad dang ldan pa'i sgo nas dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por bcug ste dbang bzhi rdzogs par bskur ba
dang / de nas lam gyi dngos gzhi rgyud gsum gyi khrid la/ thog mar lta bas spros pa gcod pa'i phyir kun gzhi rgyu rgyud la 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi lta ba bsgom pa/ bar du
lam gyi nyams bskyed pa'i phyir lus thabs rgyud la dbang bzhi dang rjes su 'brel ba'i lam gyi nang

nas bum dbang gi khrid yongs su rdzogs pa/ de'i nang tshan nang bskyed rim gyi mgor slob dpon gyi zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang bcas pa/ de rnams kyi snga
chos su rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi mngon rtogs/ lus dkyil dbang chu/ gtor chog rnams dang / ngag dbang brtan rdor gyis mdzad pa'i
lam 'bras kyi khrid yig gi lung dang bcas pa gsan pa'i skabs/ gsang dbang gi mgor rje 'di snyun gzhi zas dug gi rnam pa lta bus tshabs cher bsnyun par brten/ de man chad
kyi khrid rnams gsan ma thub/ de nas zhal dkar bla sman la sogs bsten te sman dpyad dang dug bcos la sogs pa mang du mdzad/ snying ri nas mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug khri
chen padma bdud 'dul mthu stobs rgyal mtshan pa'ang ngor du spyan drangs te/ smin gling pa'i sgrub thabs 'dod bum las byung ba'i chos dbang lugs kyi drang srong loktri'i
rig gtad dang / gnubs lugs kyi legs ldan stag zhon nag po'i rjes su gnang ba/ las 'brel lugs kyi gza' bdud kyi srog dbang / de dang 'brel bar gza'i byad 'grol dug dbyung
dang bcas pa/ rta mgrin yang gsang khros pa lha dgu'i dbang / pad gling lugs kyi phyag rdor dregs 'dul dang / tshe dbang rdo rje phreng ba/ zhang khrom gter byon byad
'grol gser gyi lde mig dang / tshar chen gyi yig steng nas gnod sbyin bektse 'khor mang gi rjes gnang bcas gsan/ gzhan yang gza' bcos dang dug bcos kyi rigs mang du zhu
bar mdzad/ yang skabs shig snying rir phebs te/ khri chen de nyid las gza' bcos dang dug bcos la sogs pa'i rim gro'i rigs mang du zhu ba sogs mdzad kyang lo bzhi tsam gyi
bar la snyun gzhi de sel ma thub/ de'i rkyen gyis sku gzugs kyi shed shor zhing sku sha'ang ha cang srab par song / thugs rab kyang de

phyin chad sngar dang mi 'dra bar cung zad 'grib pa yin gsungs/ dgung lo nyer gnyis pa'i nang snyun gzhi cung zad dwangs pa'i skabs shig bskyed rdzogs kyi bsgom bya'i don rnams
byams pa bsod nams dpal 'byor las bka' khrid dpyis phyin par zhu bar mdzad de/ 'byung 'dul gyi bsnyen pa bcu cha'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa dang / khyad par lo de'i hor
zla dgu pa nas bzung ste zla ba bdun gyi bar la/ dpal kye rdo rje'i gzhi'i bsnyen pa bcu cha'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa stan thog gcig tu tshang bar mdzad/ dgung grangs
nyer gsum pa'i ston mjug der/ khams nas khu bo mkhan chen mchog gi phyag mdzod yon tan rgya mtsho dpon 'khor rnams kyang 'bul skyel dang dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur stob pa'i
ched du bar chad med par ngor du 'byor/ lo de'i hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i nang rje 'di dbus phyogs kyi gnas khyad par can rnams mjal ba'i ched du ngor nas chibs bteg /mar
lam paN chen dge 'dun grub pas phyags btab pa'i chos grwa chen po bkra shis lhun po'i rten gsum rnams zhib mjal dang / de nas rim gyis lam bar gyi dgon khag rnams mjal bzhin
pa'i sgo nas lha ldan du phebs te 'jig rten kun gyi mchod sdong bla na med pa jo shAka rnam gnyis kyi gtsos pa'i rten gsum yongs su rdzogs pa zhib mjal dang / yer pa/
dga' ldan/ bsam yas/ gdan sa mthil/ zangs ri mkhar dmar/ rtse thang / yar klungs skor/ 'phyong rgyas ri bo bde chen sogs brgyud yar 'brog mtsho skor mdzad de yar 'brog skor
gyi dgon sde khag la sogs pa mdor na dbus phyogs kyi gnas khyad par can rnams dang / dgon sde khag la sogs pa'i rten gsum thams cad dad pa'i spyan gyis legs par mjal
te/ me tog bdug spos mar me dri mchog zhal zas la sogs pa'i mchod pa dang / snyan dar phon

che ba/ rten gtso che ba 'ga' zhig la zhal gser gsol ba la sogs pa mchod pa'i sprin phung rgyas par dkrigs pa'i sgo nas bsod nams kyi myu gu skyed bsrings shing / khyad par
bstan 'gro yongs la sman pa'i smon lam rnam par dag pa'i sa bon rma med pa yang nas yang du 'debs par mdzad do/ /de nas rim gyis rgyal rtse dang zhwa lu sogs su phebs nas/
de dag tu yod pa'i dgon khag so so'i rten gsum rnams zhib mjal dang / mchod 'bul sogs rgyas par mdzad de e wa~M du phebs/ de nas skabs 'gar gzhis rtse/ chu mig /srad rnams
su khrom dbang stsal du tshar kha shas byon pa dang / sku gzugs kyi 'phrod bzhes su rta nag /tsha rong / mang mkhar rnams su chu tshan la tshar kha shas phebs pa ma
gtogs ngor rang du bzhugs/ mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan du ma la dbang bsgyur ba'i phan khang zhabs drung rin po che dpal ldan rin chen chos mdzod kyi drung nas/ kha
che paN chen nas brgyud pa'i 'jam dkar ma ti lugs kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / bya rgyud rdo rje'i rigs kyi gtso bo slob dpon dze tA ris bkral ba'i rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa
la bkra shis lha mo brgyad kyis bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ sa lugs kyi dme brtsegs dud ka'i rjes su gnang ba/ khams gsum dbang du sdud pa'i rigs byed ma ngor
lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba/ pha rgyud zhe sdang can 'dul bar byed pa dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang /
'chi bdag las kyi gshin rje dam can chos kyi rgyal po lha bcu gsum gyi rjes su gnang ba/ ba ri lugs kyi sgrub thabs brgya rtsar grags pa'i rjes gnang rigs mthun phyogs gcig
tu bsdebs pa'i rjes su gnang ba bdun cu don brgyad dang / de'i rjes

gnang gi yi ge dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i lung dang bcas pa dang / mkhas pa'i dbang po rab dkar bla ma lhun grub ting 'dzin gyi drung nas/ 'phags yul gyi paN grub
rgya mtsho'i gtsug rgyan slob dpon a bha yA ka ra gupta ste 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pa zhes yongs su grags pa'i zhal snga nas legs par bkral ba'i rdo rje phreng ba nas
byung ba'i dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe gnyis dang / de'i steng du paNDi ta dArpa Na A tsarYa zhes pa 'gro ba'i me long du grags pas mdzad pa'i kri ya sa mutstsha ste rdo rje
slob dpon gyi bya ba kun las btus pa'i bstan bcos nas byung ba'i dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum bsnan te/ mdor na dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu rtsa lnga'i ras bris kyi
dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bskur ba rnams legs par gsan/ gzhan yang de skabs rnams su kun rig gi bsnyen pa zla ba gsum bcu cha'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa dang / 'jigs byed
kyi bsnyen pa zla ba gsum kha skong gi sbyin sreg dang bcas pa/ mgon dkar gyi sku mtshams zla ba gcig dang bcas pa bzhugs/ sambu Ta'i cho ga thugs 'dzin bskyangs te gtsug
lag tu sgrub mchod gsung du tshar gcig tsam byon/ e wa~M pa'i sgrub mchod chen mo'i skabs bde mchog gi tshon blugs pa'ang lo kha shas mdzad/ dgung lo nyer bdun pa rnga
chen gyi lor sa skya nas bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs mthu stobs nus pa'i dbang phyug 'gro mgon dbang sdud snying po dbus phebs mdzad pa'i mar lam ngor du phebs/ snga phyir
phebs bsu'i tshogs mang po dang / dge 'dun gyi ser sbreng gi bkod pa mtshar zhing yid du 'ong ba dang bcas pas mdun bdar te spyan drangs/ e wa~M pa'i zur bzhi bla khag
rnams kyis rang rang gi 'byor stobs dang bstun pa'i bsnyen bkur dang 'bul ba rgya chen bstabs shing chos kyi 'brel pa re'ang

zhus/ gtsug lag tu grwa mang la gnas brtan bcu drug gi rjes su gnang ba stsal te skal ba bzang po'i me tog rgyas par mdzad/ rje 'di sku mched nas kyang thar rtser gdan zhus
thog zhag gcig bzhugs par zhus te dpon 'khor tshang mar bsnyen bkur gya nom pa dang / dngos 'bul gyi tshogs shin tu gtos che bar phul/ de skabs bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs
des so so'i mos pa'i yol go dang 'tshams par chos kyi bdud rtsi stsal ba thams cad rje 'dis gsan par mdzad de/ bya rgyud de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bo thub pa
gnas brtan bcu drug gi rjes su gnang ba dang / ma gcig grub pa'i rgyal mos dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i rgyud mngon brjod 'bum pa la brten nas bkral ba'i tshe dpag med lha gcig
bum gcig gi byin rlabs dbang bzhi'i tshul du bskur ba/ grub chen thang stong pa nas brgyud pa'i tshe rta zung 'brel gyi dbang bskur ba/ gu ru chos dbang gis zab gter nas
spyan drangs pa'i phyag rdor gtum po khyung lnga'i rjes su gnang ba/ mnga' bdag nyang nyi ma 'od zer gyis zab gter nas spyan drangs pa'i gu ru drag dmar gyi dbang yongs
su rdzogs pa/ rig 'dzin rgod kyi ldem 'phru can gyis zab gter nas spyan drangs pa'i tshe sgrub 'chi med lcags kyi sdong po'i dbang bskur ba/ rgya zhang khrom rdo rje 'od
'bar gyi gter byon byad 'grol gser gyi lde mig tu grags pa rnams gsan/ bdag chen chos kyi rgyal po de e wa~M du zhag brgyad tsam bzhugs nas/ slar yang phebs skyel gyi tshogs
dang bcas te dbus phyogs su chibs kyi gdong bsgyur/ dgung lo nyer dgu pa shing byi lor mkhan chen ngag dbang dam chos byang du 'gro don la khyug tsam phebs skabs/ rje
'dis mkhan tshab mdzad de sgrub mchod kyi dbu bzhugs sogs mdzad/ slar mkhan chen de nyid byang nas tshur phebs bstun lo de'i hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bcu

gnyis nyin gangs ljongs bsod nams kyis ma zin par mkhan rin po che ngag dbang dam chos pa gang nyid glo bur du gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos kyi dbyings su bsdus/ de la brten nas
e wa~M pa'i bla khag khang tshan dang bcas pa thams cad kyis dpon slob rin po che byams pa bsod nams dpal 'byor mkhan por mnga' gsol/ rje 'dis de skabs kun tu spyir thar
rtse rang yang bla brang shin tu nyag phra ba'i 'o brgyal gang che la brten nas de'i thugs 'gan gyi khur yang lhur bzhes mdzad dgos pa yin mod/ 'on kyang gtso bor yang
na phyag dpe'i gzigs rtog /yang na de dag gi don la bsam byung gi rig pas dpyad pa/ yang na thos bsam gyis sgro 'dogs chod pa'i don rnams sgom pas nyams su bzhes pa/ der
ma zad bshad ma thag pa ltar gyi sku mtshams sogs bzhugs pa/ sku mtshams ma bzhugs kyang lam dus kyi dbang gi chu bo ma nub pas gtso byas pa'i dpal ldan sa skya pa'i chag
med rnam pa bzhi dang / gong du yi dam lha'i ljags bsnyen song rigs kyi bdag bskyed bzlas pa dang bcas pa/ yi dam dang chos srung nor lha'i rigs mang po la gtor ma 'bul
ba sogs mdor na chos brgyad kyis bran bzhin du bkol ba'i mtshams par ming btags pa phal mo ches 'gran du mi bzod pa'i thugs dam kho na la bzhugs pa sogs chos mthun gyi bya
ba 'ba' zhig las dus skad cig kyang g.yel ba mi mnga'/ gzhan yang gdul bya so so'i bsam pa dang mthun par rje rang gis gang gsan pa'i chos thams cad kyang lan grangs mang
po'i bar du stsal zhing / de dag kyang las sla dang rtsing spyod du ma song bar phyag len phro mo tshun chad kyang ma 'dres par mdzad do/ /de nas rje 'di dgung lo sum
cu pa shing glang hor zla dgu pa'i nang khu bo mkhan chen dam pa'ang mdo khams

sde dge'i phyogs nas yar phebs te/ e wa~M pa spyi dang bye brag rje 'di sku mched nas snga phyir phebs bsu'i rigs mang po dang / dgon pa'i ser sbreng gi tshogs dang bcas pas
spyan drangs te e wa~M du phebs/ gong du rje de nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal ba ltar gyi lha dang bla ma'i tshogs la mchod 'bul dang / dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur sogs rgya che
bar mdzad/ de skor gyi thugs brel chod bstun khu bo mkhan chen mchog dang rje 'di lhan rgyas nas thar rtse rang gi lha khang khag thams cad la rab gnas rgyas par mdzad/
dgung grangs so gcig pa me stag hor zla bdun pa'i nang khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang mang mkhar chu tshan du chibs bskyod bskyangs/ rje 'dis de bar la 'jam dkar ma ti
lugs kyi sku mtshams zla ba gcig bzhugs/ de nas lo de'i hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i yar tshes nas bzung ste khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi drung nas dbang
lung phal che ba bum pa gang byo'i tshul du rje 'di sku mched gnyis char gyis gsan par mdzad ces thos so/ /de'ang mdo sngags gnyis kyi nang nas ches mchog tu gyur pa
gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa la rgyud sde rin po che rnam pa bzhir bzhugs pa'i nang nas/ dang po bya rgyud kyi skor la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bo sman bla mched
bdun gyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i lung / sangs rgyas klu dbang rgyal po lha lnga'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub skor 'phags
pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs bcom ldan ral gris mdzad pa/ bstod pa rong ston gyis mdzad pa/ sgrub rjes ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rjes mdzad pa/ char 'bebs dpal
ldan chos skyong gis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / jo bo rje nas brgyud pa'i thub pa gnas brtan bcu drug gi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen
gyis

mdzad pa'i lung / gsang ba spyi rgyud nas gsungs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi bdag po rigs gsum spyi'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i yig cha thar rtse pan
chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i lung / 'jam dpal dkar po ma ti lugs kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i bstod pa paNDi ta ma tis mdzad pa/ sgrub skor rgya ston kun
dga' brtson 'grus kyis mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang gi yi ge thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ smon lam paNDi ta rig pa'i khu byug gis mdzad par grags pa/ sbyin sreg sangs
rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / 'jam dbyangs dang sa paN sbags te sgrub pa'i byin rlabs dang / de'i yig cha ngag dbang chos grags dang / tshogs bsag pa
kun dga' tshul khrims kyis mdzad pa'i lung / 'jam pa'i dbyangs la bstod pa gang blo ma la brten pa'i 'jam dpal ye shes yon tan bzang po'i rig gtad/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
rigs kyi yum 'phags ma rig pa chen mo'am gza' rnams kyi yum du grags pa gtso 'khor rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rjes mdzad pa/
bstod pa bstan 'dzin rdo rjes mdzad pa bcas kyi lung / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma lha dgu'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i bstod pa ngor chen
rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ sgrub rjes dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ brgyud 'debs mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa kha skong dang bcas pa/ sbyin sreg
dpal ldan don grub kyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / gtsug tor gdugs dkar gyi byad 'grol rmor chen pa'i yig cha'i steng nas lung dang bcas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi
khro bo gtsug tor 'bar ba'i rjes gnang byad 'grol

dang bcas pa/ de'i yig cha zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i lung / khro rgyal mi g.yo ba dkar po'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis
mdzad pa'i lung / bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi gtso bo tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa/
thar rtse paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor dang / rab gnas bya tshul/ sbyin sreg sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa/ tshe sgrub kyi gdams pa zab mo thun
mong ma yin pa sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / tshe dpag med 'chi med rnga sgra lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i yig cha
thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ de'i lhan thabs sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa bcas kyi lung / grub chen mi tra dzo kis bkral ba'i tshe dpag med dkar po'i rjes su gnang
ba dang / de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub dang zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ khro phu lo tsA bas mdzad pa'i 'chi ba bslu ba'i man ngag dang / zhu chen gyis
mdzad pa'i kha 'bar ma dkar mo'i 'chi bslu dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung / padma'i rigs kyi bdag po 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal gtso rkyang gi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i
yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ smyung gnas kyi cho ga zhu chen gyis mdzad pa bcas kyi lung / skyer sgang lugs kyi thugs rje chen po gtso 'khor gsum pa'i rjes
su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ las kha tshar sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa/ thugs rje chen po dang phyag rgya chen po zung 'jug tu nyams
su len tshul dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / 'jig rten dbang

phyug seng ge sgra'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ gdon sgrol gyi cho ga thar paN dang / sngags 'chang kun dga' bsod nams kyis mdzad
pa/ seng ge sgra'i char 'bebs 'dam thog bstan 'dzin rdo rjes mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / padma'i rigs kyi yum sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo thun mong dang / thun mong ma
yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba/ /tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i tshe khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun gyi snying po dang / de'i lhan thabs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad
pa'i yig cha bcas kyi steng nas nyams khrid zab mo yongs su rdzogs pa/ sgrol dkar sgrub thabs slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa'i 'chi bdag bslu ba'i rtog
pa nas phyung ba paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba ba ri'i 'gyur/ sgrol dkar sgrub thabs/ gtor ma/ bum chog /srung 'khor bcas kyi yi ge /bris pa'i srung 'khor
gyi yi ge /bar chad zhi bar byed pa/ ltas ngan g.yang du blang ba'i man ngag /ngag gi byang 'grol gyi yi ge slob dpon padma nag pos mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i sprul pa ce spyang
sngon mo'i srung ba/ ce spyang sngon mo'i lam srung gi gsal byed/ rjes gnang gi skabs su nye bar mkho ba'i lo rgyus mdzad byang med pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad
pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang bstod pa dang bcas pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i sgrol dkar rjes gnang dang / de'i dmigs rim skyabs yul zhing
khams ma/ sbyin sreg bklags chog tu bkod pa/ dbang phyug rab brtan gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang / sgrol dkar sbyin sreg mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad
pa dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung / jo bo nas brgyud pa'i sgrol ma nyi shu rtsa gcig gi

rjes su gnang ba dang / sgrol ma'i phyag 'tshal nyer gcig gi sgrub thabs yig rnying dang / de'i rjes gnang gi chings mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas
phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa'i sgrol ma maNDal bzhi chog dang bcas pa'i lung / bla med du gtogs kyang 'dir mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad kyi lung blang dgos pa dang sde tshan
gcig pa'i phyir bya rgyud kyi gras su bzhag pa gnyan sgrol yan lag drug pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i man ngag
rmi lam brtag thabs shin tu zab pa lha mo shra ma Na'i sgrub thabs kun mkhyen bkra shis rnam rgyal dang / sa chen kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa bcas kyi lung / padma'i
rigs kyi khro bo rta mgrin lcags ral can zla rgyal lugs su grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub thabs zla ba rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ nad gso ba/ steng gdon
gzir ba/ lus srung ba/ ser ba srung ba/ phyir zlog pa/ rjes gnang yi ge rnying pa/ thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub rjes rnams kyi lung / padma'i rigs kyi pho nya mo dbyangs
can ma dkar mo'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub rjes thar paN gyis mdzad pa kha skong dang bcas pa'i lung / rdo rje'i rigs kyi gtso bo slob dpon dze tA ris bkral ba'i
mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ de'i zur 'debs zhu chen gyis mdzad pa/ sbyin sreg gi

lha gcig bum gcig gi rjes gnang khrus dang bcas pa dang / de'i yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i lung / rdo rje'i rigs kyi pho nyar gtogs pa khro bo dme

brtsegs sa lugs su grags pa dud ka'i rjes gnang khrus dang bcas pa dang / de'i zhal gdams zab mo sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ rmor chen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs khrus chog bcas
dang / bsod nams lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i grib mdos bcas kyi lung / jo bo'i lugs kyi dme brtsegs ljang nag gi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa/
las tshogs la grib srung ba/ ser ba srung ba/ rims nad srung ba/ phyugs nad srung ba/ mi lo nad can srung ba/ ra lugs la spyang ki srung ba/ 'bras phol lhog pa gso ba/
nad pa'i sngas srung ba/ zhing gi 'bu srung ba/ bang mdzod srung ba/ 'gong po sreg pa/ dme grib srung thabs dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung / rdo rje'i rigs kyi pho nya mo khro
mo dme brtsegs kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha 'jam mgon kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i lung / bya rgyud nor can gyi rigs dzaM dkar 'brug zhon lha lnga jo
bo lugs kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha she'u lo tsA ba kun dga' chos grags dang / 'jam mgon kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i lung / phyag rdor gos sngon can gyi

bskur ba dang / kun rig gi cho ga gzhan phan mtha' yas/ bsnyen rgyas sgrib pa

rnam sel/ cha gsum gyi cho ga rnams ngor chen gyis mdzad pa/ dbang gi mtshams sbyor dang / sbyin sreg ro sreg sAtstsha rab gnas dang bcas pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad
pa/ bsnyen rgyas lhan thabs thar paN gyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / phyag rdor 'chi bdag 'joms pa lha bcu gsum gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ rgyud sde bzhi pa rnal

shAkya'i ming can gyis mdzad pa/ char 'bebs mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub kyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / las gshin lha bcu gsum gyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub rjes

pa/ las sbyor la/ khyad par gyi las sbyor ser ba dang char gcod pa/ mid 'byar bcos pa/ dug srung ba/ dug 'dred pa/ sri'u gso ba/ gdon bgegs skrod pa/ smyo ba 'dul ba/

bcud len/ mdze gso ba/ spyi 'gro'i las sbyor dang bcas pa dang / rjes gnang gi yi ge mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa rnams kyi lung / rdo rje gur las gsungs
pa'i phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub rjes dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ brgyud 'debs dpal ldan don grub kyis mdzad pa kha

gser chos kyi skor la/ rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul gyi mkhas dang grub pa yongs kyi gtsug gi nor bu'i cod paN la zhabs sen gyi padmo rnam par bkod pa grub chen birWa pa
chen pos rgyal yum rdo rje bdag med ma las dngos su gsan pa'i gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i skor la tshogs bshad dang / slob bshad gnyis su grags pa'i
dang po tshogs bshad tu grags pa'i skor la/ thog mar bla ma tshad mar bya ba'i phyir bla ma la gsol ba 'dabs pa e wa~M pa'i chos spyod dum bu gsum dang / dum bu dang po'i
kha skong mkhan chen nam mkha' bsam 'grub la gsol ba 'debs pa nas/ rje rang gi gsol 'debs dmigs med byams ldan ma'i bar dang / mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas
mdzad pa'i e waM pa'i gdan rabs rnam thar nor bu'i phreng ba bcas kyi lung / nyams myong tshad ma rgyud la skyed par byed pa'i khrid dngos la/ khrid kyi gzhung shing chen
po bzhi'i nang tshan gzhung shing rgyas pa gzhung ji ltar ba bzhin du bkri ba'i khrid yig ngag dbang brtan pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i gzhan phan phrin las rgyas byed kyi steng
nas/ lam gyi sngon 'gro snang ba gsum gyi khrid sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas brgyud

pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed pa dang / de las byung ba'i dam tshig rnams la srung sdom shes pa'i ched du byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa nyi shu pa'i 'grel pa rje
btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i lung / de nas slob ma rjes 'dzin sogs dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad dang ldan pa'i sgo nas dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi dkyil 'khor
du dbang bskur ba dang / de las byung ba'i dam tshig dang sdom pa rnams mi nyams par bsrung ba'i tshul gsal bar ston pa rtsa ltung 'khrul spong rje btsun rin po che grags
pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i lung / de ltar smin zin grol ba'i slad du lta bas spros pa gcad pa'i phyir kun gzhi rgyu rgyud la 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi lta ba bsgom pa/
lam gyi nyams bskyed pa'i phyir lus thabs rgyud la dbang bzhi dang rjes su 'brel ba'i lam bsgom pa/ 'bras bu sku lnga mngon du 'gyur ba'i tshul dang / nges shes bskyed
cing ting nge 'dzin ngo shes pa'i phyir lam gyi sa mtshams gzhag pa/ 'bras bu mthar thug sangs rgyas kyi sa bshad pa/ de ltar nyams su len pa'i slob ma la gsang ba bcu'i
rgyas gdab cing skal ldan gyi slob ma la phan par gdams pa'i bar gyis nyams khrid zab mo yongs su rdzogs pa dang / de dag gi skabs su bum dbang gi lam gyi nang tshan nang
bskyed rim gyi thog mar slob dpon gyi zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ gzhan yang sbyor ba don yod pa bzhis bla ma mnyes par byed pa'i khrid sngon du 'gro ba'i
lam zab phyi ma'i byin rlabs dang / de'i yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ lam zab phyi ma'i ngag 'don dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ brgyud 'debs ngor chen gyis mdzad
pa kha skong dang bcas pa'i lung /

rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi srung ba thun mong ba'am bir srung phyi ma'i byin rlabs sgom lung dang bcas pa dang / de'i yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i lung / lam 'bras su mi
gtogs kyang sa skya pa'i thug dam chag med bzhi'i nang tshan nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs dang / de'i sgrub thabs dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ bstod pa dang brgyud
'debs ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ bdag 'jug dang byin rlabs bya tshul thar paN gyis mdzad pa bcas kyi lung / rgyab rten lung dang bstan bcos tshad ma'i skor
la ngag dbang brtan rdor gyis mdzad pa'i lam 'bras kyi khrid yig /kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi mngon rtog /lus dkyil/ dbang chu/ gtor chog /rdul tshon chu bor spyan 'dren
pa'i cho ga /zhi rgyas kyi sbyin sreg rnams rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa/ las phyi ma gsum gyi sbyin sreg gi lhan thabs thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon padma
badzra gyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa nyi shu pa/ sdeb sbyor daNDa ka'i bstod pa dang dkyil 'khor gyi bkra shis bcas rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa/ mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi bkra
shis rgyud nas phyung ba/ tshogs 'khor gsang ba kun rgyan ngor chen gyis mdzad pa/ dus tha ma'i cho ga thar paN dang sangs rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa/ rab gnas dpal
'byor rgya mtsho dkon mchog dpal ldan pas mdzad pa/ 'thor nas bsgrub tshul thar paN gyis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa legs par gsan to/ /ngor lugs thun mong ma
yin pa gsung ngag slob bshad kyi skor la rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs bla ma rdor 'dzin ma dang / tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs
dngos grub rin po che'i char 'bebs kha skong dang bcas pa'i lung bcas sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas/ nyams myong tshad ma rgyud la skyed

par byed pa'i khrid dngos ni/ rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos rje'i gsung sgros 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis zin bris su mdzad pa'i khrid yig gsang chen bstan pa
rgyas byed kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bzhed pa ma nor ba la gzhi mdzad/ bum dbang rmi lam man chad kyi khrid 'phro lus pa rgyal dbang lnga pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i yig cha
dang / gzhan yang gsung bshad kyi rgyab skyor du dgos pa'i yig cha rnams kyi steng nas lam gyi sngon 'gro snang ba gsum gyi khrid shin tu zhib pas rgyud sbyangs shing /
de dag gi skabs su thog mar man ngag gi byung tshul dang / byung ba'i chos la bshad sgrub ji ltar bya tshul gyi rnam gzhag zhib par gsung bar mdzad cing / de nas brgyud pa'i
khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed pa dang / dngos gzhi rdo rje theg pa'i lam gyi rtsa ba smin grol gnyis kyi dang po/ smin byed dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad
dang ldan pa'i sgo nas dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi dbang bskur ba aShta'i bzlas lung dang bcas pa dang / de dag gi skabs su khas blangs pa'i dam tshig dang sdom pa'i
rnam gzhag gsal bar ston pa rtsa ltung 'khrul spong rje btsun gyis mdzad pa/ rgyun gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig bdud rtsi ril bu'i bsgrub tshul bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis
mdzad pa/ khyad par gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig tshogs 'khor 'bring po rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa/ 'phags pas mdzad pa'i tshogs 'khor bdud rtsi bum pa/ rje btsun gyis mdzad
pa'i rab gnas don gsal/ sa paN kyis mdzad pa'i aShta'i gzhi bshad kyi lung rnams dang / grol byed kyi khrid la/ dbang gi ye shes la log par rtog pa dgag cing 'og nas
'byung ba'i lam thams cad skyon med du bsgrub pa'i phyir 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi lta ba'i khrid dang / de nas bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil

'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de rjes lus thabs rgyud la dbang bzhi dang rjes su 'brel ba'i lam bzhi'i dang po bum dbang gi lam la phyi bskyed rim gyi khrid sems 'dzin dang
bcas pa dang / de nas phyi rol tu zhen pa'i gdon gyi gnyen por slob dpon gyi zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba yig brgya'i bzlas lung dang bcas pa sngon du 'gro
ba'i nang bskyed rim gyi khrid sems 'dzin dang bcas pa/ phyi nang gi bskyed rim gyi skabs su tshar chen gyi nyi zer sogs kyi steng nas bsgom don la thos bsam gyis sgro
'dogs gcod pa'i bshad pa shin tu rgyas pa dang / de nas bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i byin rlabs 'di khu bo mkhan chen gyi drung nas ma gsan par brten/ rjes sor kun dga' mkha'
grub dbang po las gsan pa yin kyang / 'dir sngon gyi phyag len ltar bris pa yin no/ /byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas gsang dbang dang / shes rab ye shes dang /
dbang bzhi pa ste dbang bzhi po re re la'ang / lam/ lta ba/ grub mtha'/ 'da' ka ma/ bar do/ rmi lam/ sgyu lus dang bcas pa'i khrid de/ mdor na nyams khrid zab mo yongs su
rdzogs pa shin tu zhib pa dang / de dag gi cha lag tu gtogs pa'i byin rlabs kyi skor la/ lam zab phyi ma'i khrid sngon du 'gro ba'i byin rlabs dang / de las 'phros pa'i
bla ma rin chen 'byung ldan gyi byin rlabs/ thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i bla ma rin 'byung gi nyams len bya tshul gyi lung / lam zab nang ma'i byin rlabs dmigs khrid dang 'brel
pa/ de'i nyams len ngor chen gyis mdzad pa/ lam zab phyi nang gi nyams len dang byin rlabs bya tshul thar paN gyis mdzad pa bcas kyi lung / bir srung phyi ma'i byin rlabs
sgom lung dang bcas pa dang / birU pa'i sku'i rnam 'gyur drug gi zin bris dang / bir srung bar chad kun sel ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa/ thar paN gyis mdzad
pa'i nyams len byin rlabs

dang bcas pa rnams kyi lung / bir srung nang ma'i byin rlabs sgom lung dang bcas pa/ de'i byin rlabs dang nyams len/ de nyid lam 'bras kyi gdams ngag dang mtshon byed du sbyar
ba ngor chen gyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i bir srung gsar mar grags pa rnams kyi lung / lam sbas bshad kyi byin rlabs/ rnam 'joms bir lugs lha bdun cu rtsa lnga'i byin
rlabs/ bla ma don yod grub pa la brten pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs/ rten 'brel snying po'i srung ba'i byin rlabs/ gsung ngag rin po che'i brjod
bya'i snying po bsdus pa brda don gsal ba'i byin rlabs/ dbang bzhi'i brda chig brgyud du ston pa'i byin rlabs/ sgrub pa lung sbyin dang / gsang bcu'i rgyas gdab kyi
byin rlabs/ mthar gsung ngag rin po che'i bstan pa gtad pa'i tshul du mgon rkyang gi rjes su gnang ba dang bcas pa rnams dang / gzhan yang ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad
pa'i sems bskyed kyi cho ga /lam zab phyi nang / bla ma rin 'byung / bir srung phyi nang gi byin rlabs bya tshul gyi yi ge rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa gsan zhing legs par
khong du chud par mdzad do/ /yang sa skya pa'i gser chos bcu gsum du grags pa'i nang tshan mchog bsgrubs pas thun mong zhar las 'byung ba dmar mo skor gsum gyi nang nas
mchog tu gyur pa rgyal yum rdo rje rnal 'byor ma las nA ro pas dngos su gsan cing / des kyang pham mthing pa sku mched kho na las gzhan su la'ang ma gnang ba'i nA ro mkha'
spyod kyi sindhU ra'i dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i byin rlabs shin tu zab pa dang / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi khrid yig la sogs pa'i steng nas sngon 'gro
thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ bskyed rim

rnal 'byor bcu gcig /rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma/ bde ba dang 'ja' lus sgrub pa/ yab dang yum la brten pa'i 'pho ba/ nang gi mkha' spyod sgrub pa sogs cha lag yongs su rdzogs pa'i
khrid dang / chos nyid dngos su ston pa'i byin rlabs zab mo dang / rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma che ba'i khrid dang bcas pa/ de dang 'brel ba'i nyer mkho'i lung la/ brgyud 'debs
dang bstod pa ngor chen gyis mdzad pa/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ges mdzad pa'i mkha' spyod gsang ba'i sgo 'byed/ tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs dang smon lam/
dkon lhun gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ bdag 'jug dang byin rlabs bya tshul thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ glo bo mkhan chen gyis mdzad pa'i smon lam dang bkra shis/ byams pa
mchog legs pas mdzad pa'i bkra shis/ sangs phun gyis mdzad pa'i ku sA la'i tshogs bsags kyi ngag 'don dang / dur bdag yab yum gyi gtor chog bsdus pa/ rmor chen pas mdzad
pa'i tshogs mchod nyung ngu rnam gsal/ ngor chen gyis mdzad pa'i za byed rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa rnams gsan/ sa skya pa'i gser chos dmar po skor gsum
du grags pa'i dpal kye rdo rje rtsa bshad kyi rgyud nas bstan pa'i rigs byed ma ngor lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud las bstan
pa'i lha chen tshogs kyi bdag po ngor lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / kye rdo rje'i rgyud 'bum phrag lnga pa sogs nas bstan pa'i khro bo kag chol
'dod pa'i rgyal po ngor lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / rjes gnang de gsum gyi yig cha dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i lung / gser chos tshe dpag
med sprul sku'i rjes su gnang ba dang /

de'i yig cha rmor chen pas mdzad pa'i lung / gser chos 'jam dpal nag po'i rjes gnang sgom lung dang bcas pa dang / de'i yig cha rmor chen dang / zhu chen pas mdzad pa'i lung
/ gser chos mkha' 'gro seng ge'i gdong can sngon mo'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i lung / dus 'khor nas bstan pa'i gser chos khyung khra'i
rjes gnang sgom lung dang bcas pa/ de'i yig cha rmor chen pas mdzad pa'i lung / gser chos dzaM dmar srog sgrub kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha rmor chen pas
mdzad pa'i lung / 'phags pa seng ge sgra'i rjes su gnang ba dang / klu pa'i gser chos bcu bzhir grags pa'i ya gyal seng ge sgra'i ngag srung 'grol gyi gdams pa shin tu zab
pa'i lung dang / chos srung gi skor la/ dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po lcam dral lha brgyad thun mong ba'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha shar chen byams
pa kun dga' bkra shis kyis mdzad pa'i lung / lha brgyad mkha' 'gro sbags te sgrub pa thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / mgon po khro bcu thun mong ma yin
pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / rjes gnang de gnyis kyi yig cha ngag dbang chos grags pas mdzad pa'i lung / gsang ba'i las mkhan pu tra thun mong ba'i rjes su gnang ba dang
/ de'i yig cha sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ mgon po gsang sgrub lha dgu'i sbyin sreg sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa/ drag po'i sbyin sreg ngag dbang
brtan pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ mgon po'i tshogs mchod rmar ston bka' bcu pas mdzad pa/ skong gso'i cho ga dkon mchog dpal ldan pas mdzad pa/ e waM pa'i gsung rgyun ltar
bkod pa'i bstod tshogs dngos grub rgya mtsho dang / nag po chen

po la klu chen brgyad kyis bskor ba'i sgo nas char 'bebs dang rlung gnon rje kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa/ tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i brag rdzong ma'i nyams len snyan brgyud
yin bzhin nor bu/ rje phyogs las rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i skong bsdus rin chen 'bar ba rnams kyi lung / gsang 'dus rtsa rgyud sogs nas bstan pa'i dpal mgon zhal bzhi
pa bsnyen dus kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i lung / shangs pa bka' brgyud pa'i lugs kyi mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu'i rjes su gnang ba
dang / mgon dkar gyi bkra shis bka' rgya ma dang rab gnas bka' rgya ma/ sangs phun pas mdzad pa'i rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg /zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i
sgrub rjes dang / gter bum bsgrub tshul rnams kyi lung / zhing skyong ma mo thams cad kyi gtso mo dpal ldan lha mo dmag zor rgyal mo'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha
sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i lung dang / gsang sngags rnying ma'i skor la/ gter kha gong ma mnga' bdag nyang gi gter byon gu ru drag dmar gyi dbang bskur
ba dang / de'i yig cha bdag chen rgya gar bas mdzad pa'i phrin gzhung / sngags 'chang kun rin gyis mdzad pa'i dbang chog /'jam mgon kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i
phyag len mdzes rgyan rnams kyi lung / gu ru drag dmar nyang lugs kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i lung / ras chen dpal 'byor
bzang po nas brgyud pa'i tshe dpag med lha bcu bdun gyi tshe dbang zab mo mda' 'phel mar grags pa dang / de'i yig cha rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyis mdzad pa'i lung
/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa'i lugs kyi rta mgrin gsang sgrub tu grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i

yig cha ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i lung / gter kha 'og ma gu ru chos dbang gi gter byon phyag rdor gtum po khyung lnga'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha sangs
rgyas phun tshogs kyis mdzad pa'i lung / padma las 'brel rtsal gyi gter byon phyag rdor dregs 'dul gyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub thabs smin gling gter chen gyis
mdzad pa 'dod bum las byung ba'i lung / rdo rje nam mkha' lding khyung dmar gyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig rnying gi lung / grwa mngon dbang phyug 'bar gyi gter
byon dzambha la dmar po zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i rjes gnang chu sbyin dang bcas pa/ de'i yig cha sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i lung / dge ba'i bshes gnyen
nyang ston sgrub pa po'i gter byon thugs rje chen po'i mig 'byed kyi gdams pa dang / de'i gsal byed sngags 'chang bkra shis stobs rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i lung / gter ston
bzang po grags pa'i gter byon gsol 'debs le'u bdun ma dang / ba mkhal smug po'i gter byon gsol 'debs bar chad lam sel rnams kyi lung / gnubs lugs kyi srung ma legs ldan
stag zhon nag po 'khor bcas kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i gtor chog dang rjes gnang thar paN gyis mdzad pa/ skong ba sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas mdzad pa bcas kyi lung
/ gzhan yang sa paNDi ta chen pos mdzad pa'i sdom gsum rab dbye/ lam 'bras kyi phyi nang gsang gsum gyi maNDal dang / snang ba mtha' yas kyi bsgom don/ 'chi kha ma'i gdams
ngag /yan lag bdun pa rnams dang / paN chen shAkya shrIs mdzad par grags pa'i gnas brtan phyag mchod/ byang pa rigs ldan pas mdzad pa'i cho 'phrul smon lam/ dkon mchog
lhun grub pas mdzad pa'i yas

gtam dang bsngo ba/ de la dgos pa'i tshigs bcad sangs phun pas bsgrigs pa/ bar do ngo sprod shar khang pas mdzad pa/ 'od dpag med la brten pa'i 'pho ba dkon mchog dpal ldan
pas mdzad pa/ bum gter gyi lag len dkon mchog lhun grub pas mdzad pa/ de'i zur 'debs sangs phun pas mdzad pa/ 'jam mgon kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i dam tshig rdo rje'i
sgom bzlas dang / bka' bsgo bya tshul thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ brgya bzhi'i cho ga rnams dang / slob dpon padmas mdzad par grags pa'i gser skyems dang / bdag
chen rgya gar bas mdzad pa'i bsang gzhung sogs bsang yig gi skor dang bcas pa'i lung rnams gsan cing / de thams cad kyi phyag len phra mo tshun chad kyang shin tu mthar
phyin par thugs su chud par mdzad pa yin no/ /gzhan yang phyis su mdo khams smad phyogs su 'gro don la phebs pa'i tshe'ang der bzhugs pa'i yongs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen
che rags 'ga' zhig bsten cing chos kyi bdud rtsi bzhes par mdzad la/ der ma zad mang du thos pa la ngoms pa med pa'i bdag nyid chen po 'di phyis sku na mthon por phebs
pa'i tshe'ang / 'gran zla dang bral ba'i mkhas pa 'ga' zhig las chos kyi bdud rtsi bzhes par mdzad de/ de dag kyang sde tshan gcig pa'i phyir 'dir phyogs gcig tu brjod na/
de'ang bdag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'dis dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi chos kyi rgyal srid skyong zhing mkhan po mdzad pa'i skabs/ sde dge chos rgyal chen po bod du phebs
pa'i tshe/ de'i dbu'i mchod gnas pa chen po mkhas grub ngag dbang chos 'byor gyi drung nas/ gur mgon lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / dpal mgon
zhal bsnyen dus dang / sgrub dus thun mong dang / thun

mong ma yin pa/ dkar po tshe 'phel/ ser po rgyas byed/ dmar po dbang sdud/ nag po dgra bgegs sgrol ba rnams kyi rjes su gnang ba rnams legs par gsan par mdzad do/ /rnam 'dren
dam pa 'ba' dpon po kun dga' ye shes kyi drung nas/ bya rgyud gshegs rigs kyi yum du gtogs pa srung ba lha lnga bcu rtsa gcig gi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba legs par
gsan cing / de nas bod chen po'i ljongs kyi 'gro don la rje 'di lan gnyis phebs pa'i dang po'i skabs/ mdo smad bstan 'gro'i dpung gnyen dam pa mi nyag ri khud mchog sprul
rin po che kun dga' mkhas grub dbang po mdo khams sde dge'i rgyal khab tu phebs pa'i tshe/ rje de'i drung nas theg pa chen po pha rol tu phyin pa'i blo sbyong don bdun
ma'i nyams khrid zab mo shin tu zhib pa dang / de'i yig cha sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog gis mdzad pa'i blo sbyong legs bshad kun 'dus kyi lung / bya rgyud de bzhin
gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bo thub pa gnas brtan bcu drug gi rjes su gnang ba dang / rgya gar dam pa sangs rgyas nas brgyud pa'i 'jam dpal smra ba'i seng ge'i rjes su
gnang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtsug tor 'phags pa kun nas sgor 'jug pa gtsug tor dri med lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du rig gtad zab mo dang / de'i dkyil chog
rin chen bsod nams mchog grub kyis mdzad pa/ gtsug tor dri med kyi gzungs bklag pa dang / mchod rten bzhengs pa'i cho ga'i lag len khrigs chags sgra tshad pa rin chen rnam
rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ mchod rten bzhengs tshul 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar lha nyer bdun ma'i
dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi

bdag po 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal dpal mo lugs kyi smyung gnas kyi cho ga rmor chen gyis mdzad pa'i lung / padma'i rigs kyi yum sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i rjes gnang ngor
lugs thun mong ba dang / thun mong ma yin pa 'od zer drug sbrag gi rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas nyams khrid zab mo shin tu rgyas pa dang / spyod rgyud de bzhin
gshegs pa'i rigs kyi bdag po 'jam dpal a ra pa tsa na lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo
rje lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / gsang ba 'dus pa spyan ras gzigs lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / grub chen birWa pas legs par bkral
ba'i 'jam dpal gshin rje'i gshed dmar po lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i khrid
yig sogs kyi steng nas gshed dmar spros med kyi nyams khrid dang / dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs thun mong ma yin pa lha bcu gsum ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur
ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil 'jam mgon kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa'i lung / 'phags yul gyi grub chen brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i byin rlabs dbang bzhi'i tshul du bskur ba dang
/ de'i byin rlabs bla ma'i rnal 'byor a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ grub chen brgyad cu'i rnam thar a bha ya shrIs mdzad pa pa tshab lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ bla ma rdo rje gdan
pas mdzad pa'i bstod pa/ grub chen so so'i rtogs brjod rdo rje'i glu/ rnal 'byor ma nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis mdzad pa'i grub chen brgyad cu byon tshul rnams kyi lung / rdo
rje bdag med ma lha mo bco lnga'i byin gyis brlabs pa dang / mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i kye rdor rgyud gsum dang / slob

bshad brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ gsung ngag rin po che sngon 'gro snang ba gsum dang / dngos gzhi rgyud gsum dang bcas pa'i khrid yig yongs su rdzogs pa dang / bdag chen blo gros
rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i rtsa ltung gi rnam bshad 'khrul spong rab gsal dang / rdo dril gyi rnam bshad bcas kyi lung / rigs byed ma tshar lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i
rjes gnang dang / de'i yig cha ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros kyis mdzad pa dang / rigs byed ma'i sgrub thabs khams gsum dbang du byed pa'i gnad yig tshar chen gyis mdzad
pa bcas kyi lung / Dombi lugs kyi ku ru kulle gsang sgrub lha lnga'i byin gyis brlabs pa dang / de'i yig cha ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i lung / ma rgyud padma
gar dbang gi rigs su gtogs pa sgrol ma ku ru kulle lha lnga'i dbang bskur ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil thar paN gyis mdzad pa'i lung / bla ma gnyan lo tsA ba'i dbang gi lha
gsum mam dmar chung skor gsum du grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i yig cha ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i lung / jo bo lugs kyi tshogs bdag dkar po'i rjes
su gnang ba dang / jo bo lugs kyi tshogs bdag dkar po chags pa'i rdo rje'i rjes su gnang ba dang / rje btsun sa skya pa rnams la chos skyong srung ma'i gdams pa rgya mtsho
tsam bzhugs pa'i nang nas mchog tu gyur pa rdo rje nag po chen po'i skor la/ rtsa ba'i yi ge rnams bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i glegs bam
me 'bar ma/ yan lag gi yi ge rnams tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i kha skong glegs bam/ des bsgrigs pa'i mkhas grub phal cher gyi rna ba'i spyod
yul du ma gyur pa snying gi zungs khrag lta bu thun mong ma yin pa'i snyan brgyud glegs bam/ rmor chen rdo

rje 'chang gis bsgrigs pa'i snyan brgyud dang rjes su 'brel ba'i yang skong glegs bam/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos bsgrigs pa'i 'dod khams dbang phyug dud sol ma'i glegs
bam rnams kyi lung lag len dang bcas pa dang / 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gi rnam 'phrul rgyal sras thogs med bzang po dpal gyi bka' 'bum thor bu'i skor pusta ka gcig
dang / mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyi bka' 'bum pusta ka gcig dang / kun mkhyen smra ba'i nyi ma bsod nams seng ges mdzad pa'i zab mo sngags phyogs
kyi skor gyi bka' 'bum pusta ka bzhi dang / e wa~M bstan pa'i snang byed mkhas grub dpal ldan don grub kyi bka' 'bum pusta ka gcig dang bcas pa'i lung rnams gsan zhing
legs par khong du chud par mdzad do/ /yang sde dge'i dbu bla grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po ngag dbang rin chen gyi drung nas/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs sngon du 'gro
ba'i sgo nas sngon 'gro thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ bskyed rim rnal 'byor bcu gcig /rdzogs rim rtsa dbu ma/ bde ba dang 'ja' lus sgrub pa/ mkha' spyod yab yum
gyi 'pho ba/ nang gi mkha' spyod sgrub pa sogs cha lag yongs su rdzogs pa'i nyams khrid zab mo shin tu zhib pa dang / chos nyid dngos su ston pa'i byin rlabs dang / rdzogs
rim rtsa dbu ma che ba'i khrid dang bcas pa dang / dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur mgon khro bcu'i rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas mkhyen brtse'i khrid yig sogs
kyi steng nas gur gyi mgon po'i phyi khrid rdo rje'i brag rdzong ma/ nang gi brag rdzong drag po sngags rgod/ gsang ba'i brag rdzong sems nyid ye shes kyi 'khor lo'i rtsal
'don te nyams khrid zab mo cha lag yongs su rdzogs pa dang / gsang khrid kyi sngon du 'gro

ba'i gur mgon lha dgu'i rjes su gnang ba dang / zhing skyong stobs 'phrog dbang po zhal bzhi pa'i snying thig ha la nag po'i dpe bum gyi lung lag len dang bcas pa legs par
gsan zhing dpyis phyin par mdzad do/ /lung dang rigs par smra ba gdong dgon bla ma bstan 'dzin phun tshogs kyi drung nas gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i
cha lag tu gtogs pa'i byin rlabs kyi skor bla ma'i rnal 'byor tshar gsum khug pa/ lam zab phyi nang gnyis/ bla ma rin 'byung / bir srung phyi nang gnyis/ lam sbas bshad/
brda don gsal ba/ brda chig brgyud/ rnam 'joms bir lugs/ rten 'brel snying po'i srung ba/ gsang ba bcu'i rgyas 'debs pa/ sgrub pa'i lung sbyin pa rnams kyi byin rlabs dang
/ ga ya dha ra'i lugs kyi mgon rkyang gi rjes su gnang ba/ khyad par rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgrigs pa'i gsung ngag lam 'bras kyi glegs bam pod
ser du grags pa la chos sna drug cu bzhugs pa'i nang nas/ logs su bzhugs kyang rung bar bshad pa'i las dang po pa dang thun mong du dgos pa'i chos bdun ma gtogs yongs su
rdzogs pa mchan dang bcas pa dang / rgyal ba'i lung gis zin pa'i ngor chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras kyis bsgrigs pa'i gsung ngag rin po che pusti dmar chung ngam pod dmar
du grags pa shin tu tshang ma rnams kyi lung dang lag len dang bcas pa/ rgya gar dam pa sangs rgyas bod du lan gsum phebs pa'i tha ma la khams kyi glang thang sgron mar
gter du sbas pa khams ston shes rab dpal gyis gter nas bton pa'i man ngag mkhyud dpyad dkar nag khra gsum gyi lung rnams gsan zhing phyag len kyang mdzad do/ /nyams dang
rtogs pa'i dbang phyug khro shul bla ma ngag dbang smin grol rgya mtsho'i drung nas/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rtsa ba'i rgyud sogs

las bstan pa'i zhing skyong gdong bzhi pa rnam 'gyur bcu bdun gyi rjes su gnang ba rnams dang / de'i dpe bum nor bu'i do shal dang / snyig thig ha la nag po'i skor tshang ma'i
lung dang lag len rnams gsan zhing mthar phyin par mdzad la/ gzhan yang lha 'brang bla ma grub dbang dpal ldan chos rgyal las kyang / 'od dpag med kyi dbang sogs chos
'brel phran tshegs tsam gsan pa yin no zhes thos so/ /yang mdo khams sde dge'i rgyal khab tu lan phyi ma phebs pa'i tshe'ang / sde dge'i dbu bla spangs rtogs nor bu'i mdzod
'chang grub mchog dpal ldan phrin las kyi drung nas/ bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi gtso bo tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang bskur ba sngags kyi bzlas lung dang bcas pa/ kye
rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi dbang bskur ba dang / de'i lugs kyi lus dkyil gyi dbang / bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dbang rnams gsan no/ /sde dge'i dbu bla mkhas dang grub pa'i
gtsug rgyan dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i drung nas/ bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi bdag po 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal lha so bdun gyi dbang dang / gangs can bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje
btsun sa skya pa yab sras rnams las brgyud pa'i man ngag zab mo rnams gtso bor gyur pa'i zab chos 'ga' zhig phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa gser pod du grags pa'i skor la/ thog
mar bya rgyud de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bo klu dbang rgyal po'i sgrub thabs klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa lo chen rin bzang gi 'gyur/ de'i sgrub thabs bcom ldan ral
gris mdzad pa/ bstod pa rong ston gyis mdzad pa/ rjes gnang gi tho yig mdzad byang mi gsal ba rnams dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi bdag po ma ti'i lugs kyi 'jam dkar
dpa' bo gcig grub kyi skor la sgrub thabs paNDi ta ma ti'am gsang mtshan sgeg pa'i rdo rjer grags pas mdzad

pa khro lo'i 'gyur/ des mdzad pa'i 'jam dpal gyi bstod pa/ rjes gnang gi phyag len khro los mdzad pa/ 'jam dkar gyi lo rgyus dang / rtsa ba'i sgrub thabs las kha tshar bzhi

rgyas kyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i 'jam dpal gyi sgrub pa'i rim pa tshig lhug pa/ bstod pa mdzad byang med pa/ 'jam dpal dmar po'i gsung gi rdzogs rim/ 'jam dpal gyi
zhal blta ba'i thabs/ shes rab 'phel ba dang dbang du bya ba'i thabs/ mu drA dbang du bya ba mdzes ma rgyan 'khor/ gzhan gyi ngag rku ba/ pha rol gyi shes rab 'phrog pa/
mngon shes sgrub pa/ rkang mgyogs sgrub pa/ mig rno ba/ sman rnams kyi thun tshad dang / ral gri'i rgyu dang / ril bu'i dbyibs dang kha dog gza' skar dang bcas pa bstan pa/
