dkar nag gi las sbyor/ dbang sdud 'khor lo 'bri tshul gyi gsal byed mdzad byang med pa rnams dang / gshegs rigs kyi khro bo mi g.yo ba dkar po'i skor rmor chen gyis phyogs
gcig tu bsgrigs pa la/ mi g.yo ba dkar po'i sgrub thabs dA na shI las rang 'gyur du mdzad pa/ mkhas pa yon tan khris mdzad pa'i mi g.yo ba dkar po shes rab blo 'phel gyi
sgrub thabs bcud kyi snying po/ mi g.yo ba dkar po'i zhal gdams gsum gyi snyan brgyud yi ger bkod pa/ lta ba bka' rtags kyi phyag rgya'i nyams len gyi gnad dang bcas pa/
mi g.yo ba dkar po'i bstod pa rnams yon tan khris mdzad pa bcas

dang / padma'i rigs kyi yum du gtogs pa sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i skor 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis phyogs gcig tu bsgrig par mdzad pa la/ sgrol dkar sgrub

rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ sgrol dkar bla brgyud kyi lo rgyus mdzad byang med pa/ sgrol dkar gyi rjes gnang dang / de'i zab khrid kyi dmigs rim dang / sbyin sreg gi cho

pa/ rims nad gso ba/ phyugs god srung ba/ mi lo nad can gso ba/ ra lug la spyang ki srung ba/ nad pa'i sngas srung / zhing gi 'bu srung ba/ sris rme

pa 'dul ba/ ser ba srung ba/ rims nad gso ba/ phyugs god srung ba/ mi lo nad can gso ba/ ra lug la spyang ki srung ba/ 'bras phol lhog pa gso ba/ nad pa'i sngas srung / zhing

la brten nas sgrub pa/ nang gtor ma la brten nas sgrub pa/ gsang ba ga'u la brten nas sgrub pa rnams dang / thugs rje chen po'i spyan chab las sprul pa'i dzambha las
jo bo la gdams pa gnang ba'i lo rgyus/ rjes gnang gi tho yig a ti sha'i man ngag las byung ba/ bstod pa jo bos mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa she'u lo tsA

rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi mngon rtogs gter gzhung bde gshegs rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i thugs kyi bcud thig ces bya ba'i nang gses su/ bsgom rim bsdus pa/ dzapra dmigs

la brten nas rang gzhan gyi don sgrub pa/ bar chad gzhom pa/ sde brgyad gzir ba/ lingga dang 'khor lo la brten pa'i las sbyor/ rtsa sngags/ sde brgyad dbang du bsdu ba'i sham
bu'i sngags dang bcas yod pa'i gter gzhung 'khrul med/ dbang bskur ba'i cho ga gter byon/ gtor bsngo/ bstod pa/ rta mgrin gyi zhal gdams zab mo la nang gses su/ rgyal
po ting nge 'dzin dang sngags kyis gcun pa/ 'khor lo dang smyag shad kyi dbyug pa la brten nas rgyal po 'dul zhing gnon pa/ srung 'khor/ srung mdud/ skyer sgang pas chos
skor 'di rnams o rgyan chen po la zhus tshul/ tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i mngon rtogs nyung ngu / byin rlabs kyi cho ga rgyas pa bar chad kun sel dang bcas pa'i lung dang
/ ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung rab pusta ka bzhi'i lung / zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i thang stong lugs kyi tshe rta zung
'brel gyi dbang chog tshe srog rdo rjer sgrub pa'i bcud len/ de'i rgyun khyer ring 'tsho'i tshe'i zil dngar/ de'i tshe sgrub kyi dmigs bsal som nyi'i mdud bu 'grol byed/
sgrol dkar bsnyen thabs zla 'od gsar pa/ byang gter lugs kyi tshe dpag med lcags sdong ma'i sgrub thabs dbang chog dang bcas pa bkra shis 'khyil ba'i sgra dbyangs bcas
kyi lung dang / dpal ldan shangs pa bka' brgyud nas brgyud pa'i mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu'i gdams skor gyi yi ge rnams mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs pas phyogs gcig
tu bsgrig par mdzad pa'i dpe bum gyi lung rnams legs par gsan zhing dpyis phyin par thugs su chud par mdzad do/ /gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po 'di phyis sku na mthon por
son pa'i tshe/ 'gran zla dang bral ba'i mkhas grub chen po rtsod dus kyi kun mkhyen bu ston gnyis pa rdo rje 'chang rin chen blo gsal bstan

skyong dpal bzang po'i drung nas/ dpal phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas bya rgyud nor can gyi rigs su gtogs pa'i rgyal po chen po rnam
thos sras bka' mi 'dra ba bcu drug gi rjes su gnang ba dang / rnam sras snyan grags sgrub pa'i rjes gnang dang bcas pa bya rgyud gshegs rigs kyi bdag po 'phags pa 'od
zer dri ma med pa thub dbang lha bdun ma'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba rnams gsan no/ /yang zhwa ser gyi cod pan 'dzin pa rnams kyi khrod na rgyu skar gyi
dbus na zla ba'i dkyil 'khor ltar gyur pa'i gnas lnga rig pa'i mkhas pa chen po a mdo brag dgon zhabs drung rin po che dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas kyi drung nas/ theg
pa chen po'i gso sbyong gi sdom pa dang / sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog dang mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis blo sbyong skor gyi rgya gzhung dang bod gzhung
gces pa rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i blo sbyong pod kyi lung dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen bka' gdams pa rnams kyi thugs dam lha bzhir grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba rnams
dang / bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi pho nya mo dbyangs can ma dkar mo sa manta shrI nas brgyud pa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i rjes gnang dang sgrub thabs las sbyor
dang bcas pa tshigs bcad ma thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal gyis mdzad pa'i lung / rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i pha rgyud mi bskyod pa'i rigs kyi khro bo phyag na
rdo rje 'khor chen lha bco brgyad kyi ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil 'dul 'dzin grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i lung dang bcas pa/
dpal phyag na rdo rje uu tsarYa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / pha rgyud rnam snang gi rigs su gtogs pa grub chen dpal 'dzin lugs kyi gshed dmar lha bcu gsum ma'i ras bris
kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil bu ston gyis mdzad

pa'i lung dang bcas pa/ dgra nag gi rgyud nas bstan pa'i dbyangs can dmar mo gsang sgrub kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / de'i sgrub rjes 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa dkon mchog 'jigs
med dbang pos mdzad pa'i lung dang bcas pa/ 'jigs byed kyi phyag mtshan mda' gzhu la brten nas bi Sha bsad pa'i las tshogs dug dbang rma bya rgyas pa dang / ma rgyud he ru
ka'i rigs su gtogs pa grub chen dril bu lugs kyi bde mchog phyi dkyil lha lnga'i ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i sgrub dkyil thugs sras lo tsA bas
mdzad pa'i lung dang bcas pa/ dril bu lugs kyi rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i yang snying 'khor lo bde mchog zab mo lus kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / de'i sgrub thabs
dang / bdag 'jug gi sdom dang / bdag nyid 'jug pa dang bcas pa 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i lung dang bcas pa/ ma rgyud padma gar dbang gi rigs su gtogs pa rje ras
pa badzra kIrti nas brgyud pa'i rta mgrin pad dbyug can gyi rjes su gnang ba/ dpal kye rdo rje'i bshad rgyud rdo rje gur nas bstan pa'i 'byung 'dul sems dpa' sum brtsegs
kyi rjes gnang me dbang dang bcas pa/ lha chen tshogs kyi bdag po dmar chen khyad par can gyi rjes su gnang ba rnams gsan par mdzad do/ /yang bod gangs can gyi grub mtha'
ris med kun gyi bstan pa'i srog shing gcig pur gyur pa bcu phrag rig pa'i ma hA paNDi ta nges pa don gyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i drung
nas rgyal ba'i lung gis zin pa'i snyigs dus kyi rdo rje 'chang ngor chen kun dga' bzang po'i bka' 'bum pusta ka bzhi'i lung legs par gsan zhing / gzhan yang mkhas dang
grub pa'i gtsug rgyan khang gsar mkhan rin po che ngag dbang blo gros bzang po'i drung nas/ ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje'i yig steng nas bkra shis tshe ring mched lnga'i

rjes gnang tshe dbang dang 'brel ba yig cha'i lung dang bcas pa gsan pa dang / bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwar snga phyir lan mang du phebs pa'i skabs chos
kyi bdud rtsi gsan pa'ang / yab rje grub pa'i dbang phyug khri chen ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po'i drung nas/ slob dpon dze tA ris bkral
ba'i bya rgyud padma'i rigs kyi gtso bo tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang dang / spyod rgyud gshegs rigs kyi bdag por 'jam dbyangs dmar ser dpa' bo gcig pa'i rjes su gnang
ba dang / dpal kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi dbang bskur ba dang / tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i lam 'bras slob bshad kyi brgyud 'debs kha skong dang bcas pa'i lung dang /
ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po'i lugs kyi tshe sgrub mda' 'phel ma'i dbang bcas dang / lung rtogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag 'jam mgon kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyi drung nas/ thub
dbang gnas brtan bcu drug gi rjes su gnang ba dang / jo bo lugs kyi dme brtsegs ljang nag zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i rjes gnang khrus dang bcas pa/ grub chen lU hi pa'i lugs
kyi 'khor lo bde mchog lha drug cu rtsa gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / kye rdo rje'i man ngag lugs kyi dbang dang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag
dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i lam 'bras kyi skor gsung ngag khog phub/ sngon 'gro snang gsum dang / dngos gzhi rgyud gsum gyi khrid/ dam tshig rnam bshad/ phyi dkyil
dang / lus dkyil rnam bshad/ sems bskyed cho ga /slob ma rjes 'dzin/ tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs/ lam dbang gi mtha' dpyad dang zur 'debs/ aShta'i bzlas lung / bir srung
byin rlabs ngor chen gyis mdzad par zur 'debs dang bcas pa/ bdag med ma/

lam zab phyi nang / bla ma rin 'byung / brda don gsal ba/ lam sbas bshad/ brda chig brgyud/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ gsang bcu'i rgyas gdab rnams kyi byin rlabs bya tshul mtha'
dpyad dang bcas pa/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ges mdzad pa'i rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs/ bir srung nang ma'i byin rlabs/ lam 'bras lugs kyi mgon rkyang gi rjes gnang
bya tshul rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa dang / sngags 'chang bdud kyi stobs 'phrog ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyi drung nas/ ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros kyi yig cha
ltar gter ston rgod ldem can gyis zab gter nas spyan drangs pa'i tshe dpag med lcags sdong ma'i dbang bskur ba phyag len shin tu rgyas pa'i lugs dang / lam 'bras bla mchod
dngos grub rin po che'i bang mdzod tshar chen yab sras kyis mdzad pa dang / slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo'i rnam thar tshar chen gyis mdzad pa/ des mdzad pa'i
bla ma lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa/ des mdzad pa'i rdo rings pa'i sku bstod mtha' yas ma dang / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi rnam thar tshar chen gyi mdzad pa nas/ zhwa lu mkhan
chen gyi rnam thar lnga pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i bar gyi lam 'bras slob bshad lugs kyi bla ma brgyud pa rnams kyi rnam thar gyi lung rnams dang / 'jam mgon ngag gi dbang
po rdo rje rin chen gyi drung nas/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis bla ma sa skya pa chen po la dngos su gnang ba'i blo sbyong zhen pa bzhi bral kyi khrid dang / sgrol
dkar 'od zer drug sbrag gi rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa dang / rdo rje 'jigs byed sa lugs lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / rwa tshar gnyis kyi bzhed pa
thun mong ma yin pa 'jigs byed lha bcu gsum ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / dpyal pa'i lugs

kyi phag mo bden gnyis ma dang / dbu bcad ma dang / don grub ma ste gsum gyi byin gyis brlabs pa dang / rong ston smra ba'i seng ge la grub chen ti phu pas stsal ba'i tshe
sgrub zhag bdun ma'i nyams len dang / brgyud 'debs tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i lung / dpal kye rdo rje Dombi lugs lha dgu dang / mtsho skyes lugs kyi kye rdo rje lha dgu dang
/ nag po dam tshig rdo rje'i lugs kyi dpal kye rdo rje sku gsung thugs snying po kye rdo rje dang bcas pa rnams dang / grub chen birWa pas nag po pa la stsal ba'i kye

chen las/ dpal sa skya pa'i gser chos mchog bsgrubs pas thun mong zhar las 'byung ba dmar mo skor gsum gyi dpe bum rmor chen chos kyi rgyal pos bsgrigs pa dang / de'i kha
skong gi skor dang bcas pa/ sa skya pa'i gser chos thun mong bsgrubs pas mchog zhar las 'byung ba dmar po skor gsum gyi dpe bum tshar chen chos kyi rgyal pos bsgrigs pa

yig steng nas seng gdong dmar mo'i rjes gnang lung dang bcas pa/ gser chos seng gdong sngon mo'i las tshogs rnams kyi lung dang / 'jam mgon dngos grub dpal 'bar gyi drung
nas/ 'jam dkar ma ti lugs kyi rjes su gnang ba dang / kun dga' rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i tshe dbang grub rgyal ma'i yig cha'i lung rnams gsan te mdor na mang du thos pa rgya
mtsho'i pha rol tu son par mdzad do/ /de ltar gsan pa'i chos rnams kyang thos lo tsam du ma bzhag par bsams pa las byung ba'i

shes rab kyis yang dang yang du tshig don thams cad la zhib par dpyad cing / don dang don ma yin pa rnams so sor phyes te som nyi'i 'ching ba mtha' dag las rnam par grol bar
mdzad pa yin no/ /sgom pas nyams su bzhes pa'i tshul yang / spyir bsams byung gi shes rab kyis sgro 'dogs bcad cing gtan la phab pa rnams dus dang rnam pa kun tu brtson
pa rgyun chags pa'i sgom pas nyams su bzhes pa dang / bye brag yi dam lha'i bsnyen sgrub kyi rim pa'ang gong du smos pa rnams dang / gzhan yang khams bod kun tu snga phyir
bstan pa dang sems can gyi don rlabs po che mdzad pa'i skabs gseng rnams su rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma dang / dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po brag rdzong
ma dang / dpal mgon zhal dang / shin tu zab pa'i dbyangs can ma dmar mo gsang sgrub dang / paNDi ta sa manta shrI'i lugs kyi dbyangs can ma dkar mo bcas kyi sku mtshams

sngags ye shes kyi rol par shar pa'i sgo nas mdor na tha mal gyi rnam par rtog pa skad cig tsam yang skye ba'i skabs mi rnyed pa yin no/ /shes bya'i chu gter ma brgal bar/
/kun mkhyen nor bu rnyed min te/ /de phyir rgyal dang sras rnams kyis/ /thos bsam sgom pa'i tshul rnams bstan/ /de yang thog mar thos pa yi/ /sa bon legs par btab byas
na/ /slad nas bsam sgom las byung ba'i/ /shes rab me tog bkra bar 'gyur/ /gzod nas so so yang dag pa'i/ /rig pa mchog la dbang bsgyur yang / /'gro

rnams yongs su bkri ba'i slad/ /tshul 'dir rang nyid 'jug bzhed nas/ /mkhyen brtse nus pa'i yon tan gyi/ /gzi 'od phyogs brgyar 'phros pa yis/ /srid zhi'i mun pa kun sel ba/
/smra ba'i dbang phyug che rnams las/ /zab pa dang ni rgya che ba'i/ /chos kyi bdud rtsi legs blangs pas/ /ma rig pa ni rig pa dang / /mun pa'ang snang ba'i go sar bkod/
/de don bsam pa'i shes rab kyis/ /yang dang yang du dpyad pa'i mod/ /ngang pas chu las 'o ma ltar/ /ma nor don gyi ro mchog myangs/ /de nyid tshul bzhin bsgoms pa dang
/ /yi dam lha yi bsnyen sgrub kyis/ /spang bya'i 'khor bar grags pa yang / /bsgrub bya'i sangs rgyas nyid du bsgyur// //spyi don bzhi pa phrin las kyi gtso bo bstan pa dang
sems can gyi don rlabs po che ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul la gsum ste/ dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi chos kyi rgyal srid chen por mnga' gsol te bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad
pa'i tshul/ mdo khams su mi bdag sa'i tshangs pa chen pos spyan drangs te bstan pa dang sems can gyi don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ slar yang rang gnas gdan sa chen por zhabs
pad bkod de bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul lo/ /de'i dang po ni/ nges pa don gyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas

/nyin bzhin gsal bar mdzad la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi don zhib tu bshad pa la gnyis te/ thog mar dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi chos kyi rgyal srid chen por
mnga' gsol ba'i tshul dang / de nas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul

lo/ /de'i dang po ni/ 'di ltar rjes su thos te/ de'ang dgung lo so gnyis pa me yos lor/ mdo smad sde bzhi dang dge bcu'i dpal gyis mngon par mtho ba'i rgyal khab nas stobs
kyi 'khor los sgyur ba chos rgyal chen po tshe dbang rdo rje rig 'dzin pas khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid spyan 'dren pa'i pho nya'i tshogs rnams rim bzhin
'byor par brten/ rje 'di dgung lo so gsum pa sa 'brug hor zla drug pa'i nang khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang ston 'khor rnams dpal e wa~M chos ldan nas chibs bteg /rje

pa'i gzigs

snang du 'dra sku de nyid yar bzhengs te/ rje 'di'i snyan dar phul ba rnams phyag gis bzhes pa'i snang ba byung zhing / de'i rkyen gyis bde gsal mi rtog pa'i nyams bsam gyis
mi khyab pa thugs rgyud la 'khrungs shing / de nas lha khang 'ga' zhig mjal bar mdzad kyang / bde ba chen po'i nyams skyes drags pas rjes sor bsam blo gtong dus mi dran
par 'dug gsungs shing / 'di ni e wa~M pa'i chos kyi rgyal srid chen po 'dzin dgos pa'i ltas dang / bzung nas kyang bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa cung zad tsam 'byung
ba'i ltas yin pa 'dra gsungs mod/ dag snang 'di ni so so skye bo'i blo yi spyod yul du ma gyur pa'i ngo mtshar shin tu che ba zhig go /de rjes hor zla brgyad pa'i mjug tsam
na mkhas dang grub pa yongs kyi gtsug rgyan e wa~M pa'i mkhan chen khri thog pa byams pa bsod nams dpal 'byor pa phran bu'i spyan 'bras gsal min du gyur pa dang / de'i

dgongs pa khrol bar gyur la/ de nas e wa~M pa'i bla khag khang tshan dang bcas pa thams cad kyis da ni rang re rnams kyi mgon dang skyabs dang dpung gnyen dam par bstan pa'i

pa'i rje 'di dang / rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag khang gsar zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang blo gros bzang po pa dang / nyams dang rtogs pa'i dbang phyug phan khang
zhabs drung rin po che dpal ldan

rin chen chos mdzod pa ste gsum mkhan por 'os shing / de'i nang nas kyang spangs pa dang rtogs pa'i yon tan gang la gzhig kyang rje 'di kho na bstan pa'i bdag po chen por mnga'
gsol ba zhig byung na phan bde'i nyi ma gsar du 'char bar 'gyur ro zhes gleng bar byed cing gnas tshul de bzhin dpal sa skya'i khri chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang
kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po'i gser snyan rin po cher gsol ba na/ spyir dus gsum gzigs pa rnams kyis mi mkhyen pa'am/ mi gzigs pa'am/ thugs su mi
chud pa ni ci'ang srid pa ma yin mod/ 'on kyang legs par brtags shing dpyad pa'i sgo nas bod kha ba can gyi gnam sa'i khyon la dbang sgyur ba'i gzhungs dga' ldan pho brang
pa chen por rgyu mtshan rnams snyan gsan phul ba na/ rgyal khab chen po de nyid nas kyang rje 'di la khyod kyis dka' tshegs la mi blta bar rnam dpyod kyi dpung pas kun

ba dang / 'os su gyur pa'i gdul bya rnams kyang 'khor ba dang ngan song gi g.yang sa las sgrol la/ rnam par grol ba'i nor bu'i khang bzang nyid du 'khrid cig ces pa'i
bka' stsal gnyan po dzambu chu bo'i gser gyi cod pan lta bu shin tu lci zhing gzi brjid che ba dag stsal ba dang lhan cig /sa skya nas 'jam mgon khri chen rin po ches kyang
de ltar bgyid dgos pa'i bka' stsal rin po che'i phreng ba lta bu shin tu lci bar phebs pa dang / ngor gyi bla gra tshang mas kyang gsol ba phur tshugs su btab pa la brten
nas/ spyir sngon gyi rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa rnams kyis kyang sgrol bar ma nus pa'i snyigs ma'i sems can shin tu ma rungs pa rnams kyi khrod 'dir/ bstan pa dang sems
can la phan pa bsgrub pa shin

tu dka' bar snang na'ang / re zhig bya ba'i khur 'di dag bzod par bgyis te bstan pa dang sems can la ci nus kyis phan pa bsgrub par bya'o snyam du dgongs nas rim gyis zhal
gyis 'ches te/ dus phun sum tshogs pa legs sbyar gyi skad du pra dzwa pa ti zhes pa bod skad du skyes bdag ste ljongs 'dir dbang thang dang bstun pa'i ming lcags mo lug gi
lo'i rgyal gyi zla ba'i 'phel phyogs kyi gral tshes bco lnga'i nyin/ gnas phun sum tshogs pa yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi gtsug lag
khang chen por/ ston pa phun sum tshogs pa nges pa'i don du gzod ma nas sku bzhi ye shes lnga'i khyab bdag mi slob pa'i zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang chen po'i go 'phang mngon
sum du brnyes su zin kyang / thun mong gi gdul bya rnams drang ba'i slad du rgyal ba'i myu gu gsar pa'i tshul gyis rnam par rol pa na/ rang don du tshul gnas gsan bsam sgom
pa'i yon tan yongs su rdzogs/ gzhan don du 'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i phrin las la dbang 'byor/ gnyis ka'i don du mkhas btsun bzang gsum dang mkhyen brtse nus pa'i rnam thar
mkha' khyab tu snang ba'i theg pa mchog gi bshes gnyen 'gran pa'i zla thams cad dang bral ba gang nyid/ 'khor phun sum tshogs pa snang ba'i 'khor 'phags pa'i dge 'dun
rab tu mang po dang / mi snang ba'i 'khor 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i tshogs dpag tu med pa dang bcas pas byon te/ mi 'jigs pa bzhi la mnga' brnyes pa'i brdar
seng ges bteg pa'i rin po che'i khri chen po ga la bar/ zhabs mthil 'khor lo'i re khA rnam par bkod nas/ ji ltar 'char ka'i nyin mor byed pa thun mtshams kyi chu 'dzin gzhon
nus mdzes par spud pa bzhin du srid pa gsum gyi gzi brjid ma lus pa gcig tu spungs pa ltar lham mer bzhugs pa na/ 'di ltar mi mjed kyi bdag po tshangs pa dang / lha'i
dbang

po brgya byin gyis bcom ldan 'das la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gsol ba btab pa dang tshul mtshungs par/ chos phun sum tshogs pa dus gsum gyi rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa thams
cad kyi bgrod pa gcig pa'i nor bu'i them skas gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa gtso bor gyur pa'i theg pa gsum gyi gzhung dang gdams ngag gis mtshon rgyal
ba'i bstan pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo'i seng ge'i sgra chen po sgrogs par gsol ba gdab pa'i slad du/ sa bzang 'phags pas ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
chen por stsal ba'i chos kyi dung dang / lam 'bras glegs bam pod ser ma rje btsun rin po che'i phyag dpe 'khrul med dang / bkra shis pa'i rdzas brgyad la sogs pa sngon
du 'gro ba'i sgo nas dpal ldan sa skya'i legs 'bul dang / ngor gyi bla brang khag lnga dang / khang tshan bcu gcig dang / gzhan yang grwa rigs sbyin bdag gi tshogs thams
cad kyis kyang rang rang gi 'byor pa dang bstun pa'i legs 'bul gyi dngos po rgya che ba dang bcas te/ snyigs dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga'
bzang po'i chos kyi rgyal srid chen por yongs su mnga' gsol ba'i skal ba bzang po'i nyi ma gsar du shar bar gyur to/ /de ltar bgyis pa'i dge tshogs thams cad kyang bar ma
dor chud mi 'dza' ba'i slad du 'phags dang mkhas pa dgyes pa'i legs bshad kyis mtshams sbyar te byang chub snying por yongs su bsngo ba'i rgyas gdab par mdzad cing / gzhan
yang ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos gdul bya skal ba dang ldan pa rnams kyi rgyud ma smin pa smin par byed pa'i gnas dbang khang du grags pa dang / de'i yang steng
g.yabs chen du grags pa bcas kyi bzhugs khri so so'i steng du'ang khri 'bul zab rgyas dang bcas te yongs su mnga' gsol zhing / de dag gi dus kyi tshe nam

mkha' thams cad 'ja' sprin kha dog sna tshogs pas gang ba sogs ngo mtshar gyi ltas mang po mngon sum du lhags par gyur to/ /de nas rim pa bzhin rtsis sprod len gyi skor rnams
kyang gna' bo'i lam srol bzang po ji lta ba bzhin mdzad pa yin no/ /mgon khyod mkhas pas 'jam dpal dang / /btsun phyir 'phags pa nye bar 'khor/ /ngang tshul bzang pos
'gro kun la/ /brtse bas lag na padmo nyid/ /de slad mkhyen brtse nus gsum gyi/ /yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ /thub dbang kho na'i rjes 'gro ste/ /gzhan pa'i dper 'os srid
ma yin/ /rgyu des yid kyi brtan pa kun/ /cig car 'phrog pa'i ra mda' ru/ /chos kyi rgyal por mnga' gsol ba'i/ /gsol 'debs rol mo ci yang 'khrol/ /rang bde'i dpal la ma
chags par/ /bstan 'gro'i khur chen len par brtsams/ /dka' yang gzhan don la dgyes pa/ /dam pa rnams kyi chos nyid yin/ /rigs kun bdag po'i mi'i rol par/ /sprul la spyi bos
mi btud su/ /rgyal ba gnyis pa'i sku brnyan yang / /gus pa'i tshul gyis bzhengs la ltos/ /e ma srid zhi'i gtsug tor rtser/ /mngon par 'phags pa'i chos kyi khrir/ /zhabs
kyi chu skyes bkod pa'i mod/ /phan bde'i 'dod rgu ci yang 'jo/ /dge legs bye ba'i dus dang gnas/ /ston 'khor dam chos phun tshogs pa'i/ /nges pa lnga ldan 'og min zhing
/ /sa 'dir gsar du 'phos par gyur/ /de lta'i skal bzang utpal/ /khong nas dgod pa'i dga' ston du/ /shis pa'i mtshan ris mang po yang / /brgya byin mdzub rtses bris bzhin
lhags/ /tshul de'i snyan grags rgyud mangs glus/ /srid zhi'i khams kun khyab pa las/ /yid srubs dpung las rnam rgyal ba'i/ /bde skyid sgo 'phar ci yang phye// //gnyis pa
bstan pa dang sems can gyi don ji ltar mdzad

pa'i tshul ni/ de ltar chos kyi khri la zhabs sen bkod ma thag pa nas lo der phyogs mtha' dag nas 'dus pa'i don gnyer sum brgya skor la gsung ngag rin po che'i chos kyi 'khor
lo bskor ba'i dbu btsugs pa nas bzung ste lcags mo sbrul lo'i bar gyi lo bcu bar ma chad par dgun gyi dus stod mnga' ris/ bar dbus gtsang / smad mdo khams rnams nas gdul
bya skal ba dang ldan pa rdzogs ldan dus kyi sprin phung bzhin du 'dus pa rnams la/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi nyams len du gyur pa grub chen birWa pa'i thugs
bcud gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i sngon 'gro snang ba gsum gyi khrid dang / brgyud pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed pa dang / dbang gi mngon
par rtogs pa brgyad dang ldan pa'i rgyu dus kyi dbang bskur ba dang / lam gyi dngos gzhi rgyud gsum gyi khrid dang / de dag gi skabs su lam dus kyi dbang dang / cha lag
tu gtogs pa'i byin rlabs rnams dang / rgyab rten gyi lung dang bcas pa shin tu rgyas pa tshar re dang / dpyid kyi dus don du gnyer ba sum brgya skor la/ bstan pa rin po
che'i gzhi'am rtsa ba lta bur gyur pa'i dge bsnyen dang / dge tshul dang / dge slong gi sdom pa rnams rim pa bzhin du 'bogs par mdzad pa rnams ni lo bstar bzhin chag med
yin la/ de lta bu'i rgyun chos tsam du ma zad dbyar dgun la sogs pa'i dus nges med rnams su'ang gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i bya ba dang / spyod pa dang / rnal 'byor dang
/ rnal 'byor chen po bla na med pa'i rgyud rnams kyi mngon par dbang bskur ba dang / byin gyis brlab pa dang / rjes su gnang ba dang / rig pa gtad pa la sogs pa rab tu
mang po dang / de rnams dang rjes su 'brel pa'i bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid du ma dang / rgyab rten gyi lung dang / lag tu blang ba'i tshul rnams dang / bla ma gong ma'i bka'
'bum gyi

lung la sogs pa mdor na gdul bya so so'i bsam pa dang mthun par zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo rgyun chad med par bskor te/ skal ba dang ldan pa'i gdul bya rnams
kyi rgyud ma smin pa smin par byed pa dang / smin pa rnams grol bar mdzad de 'khor ba dang ngan song gi sgo ni bkag pa bzhin du gyur/ mngon mtho dang nges legs kyi sgo
thams cad ni dus gcig tu phye ba bzhin mdzad pa yin no/ /chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba de dag kyang bstan 'gro'i don 'ba' zhig la dgongs te phyag len phra zhing phra ba tshun
chod kyang sla chos su ma song bar mdzad cing / gzhan rnams la'ang de ltar bya dgos pa'i bca' ba dam po mdzad pa ni bstan pa'i gsos su smin pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar ba
zhig go /dgung lo so bdun pa chu sprel lo'i hor zla lnga pa'i mjug tsam na 'og min gnyis pa dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen por khri mjal la phebs te/ sa skya gzhung
du maNDal sngon du 'gro ba'i sku gsung thugs kyi rten rnams dang / dar/ ras/ ling / gos chen yug ba ma la sogs pa'i tshan grangs mang po dang / mchod cha'i skor sna tshogs
pa dang / ma hA tsi na'i yul gyi ljon 'dab 'khor drug bco lnga dang / rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu tham pa dang / chibs pa gnyis dang bcas pa'i dngos 'bul rgya che
ba dang / 'jam mgon khri chen rin po che ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po pa dang / sngags 'chang grub pa'i dbang phyug ngag dbang kun dga' rin
chen pa dang / mtha' klas 'gro ba'i skyabs gcig mgon po dngos grub dpal 'bar ba dang / lung rig smra ba'i gtsug rgyan 'jam mgon kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa rnams kyi sku
sger so sor bkra shis pa'i lha reg sngon du 'gro ba'i tshan grangs kha shas dang / ljon 'dab 'khor drug lnga re dang / sa skya zhabs pad par ljon 'dab 'khor lnga dang / rje
btsun ma so sor ljon 'dab 'khor drug re re bcas dang / gzhan yang gsol

gzim mchod gsum dang / mgron gnyer dang / drung yig dang / lde phyung ba dang / rtsA gnyer dang / shing gnyer sogs la'ang rang rang gi go babs dang bstun pa'i gnang sbyin gang
la gang 'os dang / khyad par chos sde lho byang gi lha khang khag rnams su bzhugs pa'i rten gsum ngo mtshar ba rnams kyi mdun du mchod pa'i khyad par shin tu rgya che
ba dang / sprul pa'i lha khang chen mor dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtshor mang ja 'gyed dang bcas pa'i bsnyen bkur gya nom pa bcas bsgrubs nas hor zla drug pa'i mjug tu e wa~M
du phebs pa dang / gzhan yang sku'i 'phrod bzhes kyi tsha rong chu tshan du snga phyir tshar kha shas phebs pa ma gtogs ngor rang du bzhugs/ rje 'di dgung lo zhe gnyis
pa dbang phyug gi lor sde dge chos rgyal chen po tshe dbang rdo rje rig 'dzin pa'ang dbus gtsang du phebs/ sa ngor gnyis kyi gtso byas pa'i dgon sde yod do cog la bsnyen
bkur rgya chen po bstabs/ rje 'di la'ang sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes mdzad cing / lan cig chos rgyal de nyid e wa~M pa'i lha khang rnams mjal du byon pa dang chabs cig
rje 'dis kyang rten gsum rnams kyi byung khungs sogs gsung bzhin phebs pa'i tshe/ gtsang khang du chos rgyal mchog nas thub chen rin po cher 'bul rgyu'i snyan dar zhig rje
'di'i phyag tu phul ba ltar rje 'dis kyang thub dbang rin po cher sgron pa na/ gang nas byung cha med par snyan dar ser po zhig nar gyis byung ste chos rgyal de'i mgul
du son par gyur la/ de la brten nas chos rgyal rang yang sngar rab tu 'byung 'dod shin tu che bar yod kyang stabs 'grig cig ma byung ba la/ da lan gyi rten 'brel 'dis ni
ring nas brnags pa'i don thams cad 'bad med du 'grub par 'gyur ba'i ltas zhig go snyam pa'i dga' spro 'dun gsum cig car du 'phel bar gyur ces grags la/ gang ltar yang rje
'di las kye rdo rje rgyu lam gyi dbang

dang / tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang la sogs pa gsan cing / yon mchod gnyis char thugs yid gcig 'dres lta bur gyur pa yin no/ /mdor na gdan sa zhal 'dzin lo bcu'i ring la/
gtso bor dge 'dun gyi sgrig lam bsrung ba dang / dus dang khyad par gyi dgon pa'i gtong sgo gtang rgyu rnams kyang sngar rgyun las nyams chag spu tsam yang ma song ba'i steng
gong nas gong 'phel du mdzad pa dang / sngar bla khag rim can gyis nyams gso ma byung ba'i sa mchod chen mo'i skabs khyer rgyu'i gos chen gyi 'phan 'dugs rgyal mtshan
la sogs pa'i yo byad rnams dang / gtsug lag khang dang / mgon khang shar nub dang / lam 'bras lha khang bcas kyi gtsos pa'i lha khang khag rnams kyi dngos chas rigs gsar
du bzo dgos gras gsar bzos dang / nyams gso dgos rigs rnams la nyams gso sogs bstan pa'i nyams la phan nges pa 'ba' zhig mdzad pa dang / lha khang khag thams cad la'ang
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga shin tu rgyas pa'i sgo nas dam tshig pa dang ye shes pa dbyer med du bsres te byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar bar mdzad pa dang / lo re bzhin lha khang
khag rnams su bla ma mchod pa dang / gnas brtan cho ga sogs dang 'brel bar spos mar me zhal zas rnams re re nas stong phrag tu longs pa re phal cher chag med du mdzad
pa dang / khyad par lcags 'brug hor zla dang po'i nang rje 'di'i mnal lam du/ ngor gyi rgyab ri rtse nas rtsa ba'i bar zhig pa dang / thar rtse'i pho brang rtse nas rtsa
ba'i bar gas pa sogs byung ba dang / dngos su'ang ngor chen gyi 'dra skus spyan chab gsil ba dang / gzim chung nub kyi zhal 'bag rnams kyi dbu rgyan thod skam rnams don med
du sa la lhung ba dang / thugs dam gtor ma'i rgyan rnams kyang don med du lhung ba sogs mi dge ba'i mtshan ma mang du byung ba ltar/ khams nas khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje
'chang de nyid zhi bar gshegs pa'i

gnas tshul rnams kyang gsan ma thag pa nas dkon mchog la mchod pa dang dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur sogs rgyas par mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang rang zhabs kyi mi ser phran yod rnams
la'ang 'tsho skyong dang mgo 'don la sogs pa shin tu mthar phyin par mdzad pa sogs mdor na rje 'di ni bstan pa dang sems can gyi don kho na dgongs pa las/ dgos med kyi
bya ba dang rang 'dod kyi 'khri ba la sogs pa gtan nas mi mnga' ba dang / gcung mdzod pa nor ldan shes rab bzang po pa'ang bsod nams che zhing bstan pa la lhag bsam dkar
ba dang / bya ba dang bya ba ma yin pa so sor phye ba'i mkhyen rab kyi rtsal che zhing / las zhi drag gang la'ang nus pa phul du son pa zhig yin pa sogs kyis chos dang 'jig
rten gnyis ka'i thad nas de dus lta bu zhes kun gyis bsngags pa'i gnas su gyur pa yin no/ /dpag bsam shing dang bdud rtsi yis/ /kun dga' gsar pa sbyin pa gang / /skyengs
byed chos kyi zla snang gis/ /'khor ba'i tsha gdung mtha' dag bsal/ /khyad par dus gsum rgyal rnams kyi/ /phrin las gcig tu bsdus pa bzhin/ /bi rU'i bzhed gzhung gsung
ngag gis/ /'gro mang grub pa'i dpal la sbyar/ /e ma chos dang srid gnyis ka'i/ /'byor pa phun sum tshogs pa'i chus/ /ljongs 'di'i gdung ba kun bkrus te/ /phan bde'i mtshar
sdug rdzogs par byas/ /rten rnams sngags kyi cho ga yis/ /dam ye gcig tu bsres pa las/ /nyi ma'i 'od kyang zil gnon pa'i/ /byin rlabs gzi byin 'bar bar gyur/ /rgyal sras
kun tu bzang po yi/ /rnam par thar la co 'dri ba'i/ /mchod dang bsnyen bkur la sogs pa'i/ /bsod nams sgo 'phar ci yang phyes/ /de lta'i dge mtshan gdugs dkar po/ /mi
mthun phyogs las rnam rgyal ba/ /srid zhi'i khongs su bsgrengs

pa'i mod/ /'dod rgu'i grib bsil ci yang byin// //gnyis pa mdo khams su mi bdag sa'i tshangs pa chen pos spyan drangs te bstan pa dang sems can gyi don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul
ni/ nges pa don gyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen rtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas/ slar yang bod chen ljongs kyi 'khor los sgyur/ /sde bzhi dge bcu'i nor
bu'i cod pan rtser/ /zhabs sen bkra shis re khA bkod mdzad nas/ /bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel la gsol ba 'debs/ /khyad par rnal 'byor dbang phyug sa skya pa'i/ /snyan brgyud
tshad ma bzhi ldan gdams pas mtshon/ /zab rgyas dam pa'i chos kyis rigs can gsum/ /rnam grol go 'phang bkod la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don zhib tu bshad pa
la gsum ste/ thog mar mdo khams su byon nas bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul/ bar du tshogs gnyis rgya cher spel ba'i slad du dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing du bsnyen
bkur ji ltar bstabs pa'i tshul/ slar yang mdo khams su byon nas bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul lo/ /de'i dang po ni 'di ltar rjes su thos te/ mdo khams sde dge'i
rgyal khab nas lung dang rig par smra ba kun gyi gtsug rgyan gcung zhabs drung rin po che rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po'ang khu bo mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang de nyid
kyi dgongs rdzogs rgya cher bsgrub pa'i slad du/ chos rgyal chen por dgongs khrol nan zhus mdzad nas rim gyis chibs bteg te/ lcags 'brug hor zla bcu pa'i tshes brgyad kyi
nyin e wa~M chos ldan du phebs/ de'i zhabs 'bring dang lhan cig rje 'di gdan 'dren zhu bar sde dge'i sku tshab ni sa mda' bu 'khor bcas kyang 'byor/ rje 'di la chos rgyal
mchog gi zhu yig rnams 'bul ba dang chabs cig mdo khams kyi

bstan 'gro'i dpal mgon dam par nges par chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur dgos pa'i gsol 'debs nan tan gyi snying por bgyis te gsol ba dang / de bzhin du dpal ldan sa skyar yang sde
dge chos rgyal mchog gi zhu yig dang 'brel bar ngor e wa~M chos ldan gyi mkhan rin po che khri thog pa 'di bzhin mdo khams smad phyogs kyi bstan 'gro'i mgon du nges par gtong
grogs mdzad dgos tshul gyi gsol ba rtse gcig tu btab pa la brten/ sa skya nas 'jam mgon khri chen rin po ches kyang 'phral du mdo khams su phebs dgos tshul gyi bka'
nan stsal rung / e wa~M bla brang gzhung gi rtsis sprod kyi skor dang / khams su phebs chas sogs gang ci nas 'phral du 'grig dka' bar brten/ slar chu rta lor mdo khams su
chibs bskyod bskyang rgyu zhus te rtsis sprod kyi gra bsgrigs pa dang / bstan 'gro'i don du 'gyur nges pa'i mdzad phrin gyi 'phro rnams kyang rim gyis grub par mdzad de/
dgung lo zhe drug pa lcags mo sbrul gyi lo'i smin drug zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi rgyal ba gsum pa'i tshes bzang por/ bstan pa'i snang byed dam pa khang sar ngag dbang blo
gros bzang po pa nyid rgyal ba gnyis pa'i chos kyi khri chen por bkra shis pa'i cho ga dang bcas pas yongs su mnga' gsol zhing / de nas rim gyis sa skya'i sku tshab dang
bcas te rtsis sprod kyi skor rnams phyag deb gzhir bzhag gi sngar rtsis ji ltar blangs pa bzhin las nyams chag spu tsam yang ma song ba'i khar sngon gyi rnying hrul rnams
kyang nyams gsos dang / gsar bzos kyi sgo nas shin tu dngos gtsang zhing gya nom par mdzad de rtsis phul ba dang / khyad par gsar du sbyor 'jags stsal ba'i rigs la/ gtsug
lag khang du mkhan chen dpal mchog rgyal mtshan gyi dus ja'i skabs bsham rgyu'i zhal thang che legs gong gsham zhal khebs dang bcas pa dang / gsang ba'i mgon khang

du rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i phyag mtshan rdo rjes mtshan pa'i gri gug dang / tsandan las grub pa'i gaNDi dang / dpal ldan lha mo 'dod pa khams kyi dbang phyug
ma'i phyag mtshan ral gri sdigs pa'i yu ba can dang / mdung dang / rtse gsum ba dan dang bcas pa dang / zhing skyong chen po zhal bzhi pa'i phyag mtshan rdo rjes mtshan
pa'i gri gug dang / zangs kyi thod khrag dang / ral gri dang / mdung dang / rtse gsum ba dan dang bcas pa dang / dngul gyi rkang gling dang / g.yer kha'i phreng ba dang
/ rus pa'i phreng ba dang / zangs bum dngul kha can rnams dang / las mkhan pu Ta'i phyag mtshan ral gri dang bcas pa rnams lcags la gser tshags kyis spras pa shin tu sgros
gtsang ba/ 'di rnams dka' tshegs chen po'i sgo nas mdo khams su bzo rgyu bskur te sbyor 'jags mdzad pa dang / mgon khang nub tu lo dar bzhin skong brgya'i skabs bsham
rgyu'i chos srung rnams kyi spyan gzigs su mdzod gos dmar po yug gcig dang / rgya dngul rta rmig ma spus legs 'degs srang lnga bcu yod pa bcas dang / bla gzhung g.yabs chen
du rgya rol che ba spus legs can cha gcig dang / sgrub mchod chen mo'i skabs bsham rgyu'i kye rdor dkyil 'khor gyi yol ba mdzod gos rgyan bzhi dmar po las grub pa shin
tu spus legs pa can gcig dang / gur/ sam Ta/ bde mchog /gsang 'dus bcas kyi cho ga pa so sor rigs lnga'i dbu rgyan gnyis gnyis dang / gos chen gyi rten khebs gnyis gnyis
te bsdoms rigs lnga gser shog ma brgyad dang / gos chen gyi rten khebs ngo brgyad bcas dang / lam 'bras lha khang du ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi 'dra sku rin po cher mdzod
gos sprin ris ma ser po'i gzhi la grwa dang lcags ri rnams gos chen sgrim gser dmar pos byas pa'i snam sbyar kha gsar spus legs can gcig dang / 'dra sku rin po che'i mdun
du gan dkar

yu ring skyon med kyi nang du zas phud sna tshogs kyis bkang ba bcas dang / rab gsal shar du bka' shog yig rigs gsar sbyor gyi skor la/ ngor chos spyi la dgos pa'i shel tham
chen mo'i rgyab gnon du rgyal tshab de mo no mon han gyi bka' tham gtsang btsan can gcig dang / rtswa 'dam thon skabs shin tu mkho ba'i pho brang dmar po rgyug 'dzin las
khungs dam 'byar la bka' shag nas mgo mchan yod pa gcig dang / chos gzhis 'a zhwa ba'i 'dzin gras sa dang khang pa sogs dbang rigs kyi sa tho sger ba 'brang stod pa'i thel
'byar can rnams dang / yang phugs su lam 'bras lha khang la nyams gso bya rgyu'i rten du 'bru spus legs khal lnga brgya tham par sbyor 'jags gnang ba nyams gso ma byas
bar la ngo bo chud zos su ma song bar rtsis sprad rgyu dang / skyed gang byung bla brang rim can gyi gtong sgo'i zhal 'debs bya rgyu mdzad pa bcas mdor na gsar sbyor dang
bcas pa'i rtsis sprod rnams legs par phul te bstan pa'i mig rgyan dang nyams su phan nges pa 'ba' zhig mdzad do/ /de nas mdo khams su phebs rgyu'i nyer bsdogs rnams kyang
ji ltar 'os pa brtsams pa dang / don du gnyer ba rnams kyi ngor dbang dang rjes gnang la sogs pa'i bka' chos kyang ci rigs par stsal te chu rta hor zla dang po'i mjug
tu yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen por phebs te/ der bzhugs pa'i 'jam mgon sku ngo khag rnams la 'bul ba dang / lha khang khag
rnams su mchod pa dang / 'dus tshogs su mang ja'i bsnyen bkur rnams rgyas par mdzad/ skabs der khri chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan
'dzin bzang po bar de sngon du gdung sras gtan nas ma byung bar brten/ rje 'di la gdung sras 'byon min gyi brtag pa dang / srung ba lha

lnga bcu rtsa gcig gi bka' dbang sogs dgos tshul phebs pa bzhin/ gdung sras kyang mi ring bar 'byon pa'i lung bstan dang / bka' dbang rnams thugs bzhed bzhin phul bas khri
chen rin po che'ang thugs dgyes pa'i rtser son te sangs rgyas dngos kyi 'du shes kyis rje 'di'i zhabs pad bskal brgyar brtan pa'i gsol 'debs phul ba dang / khyad par mdo
khams su'ang rje 'di lta bu la zhabs tog mi sgrub pa dang / 'gal rkyen du 'gro rigs zhu mi su'ang mi 'byung ba gzhir bcas na'ang / de dag la phan pa'i phyir yin gsungs nas
bka' shog cig kyang stsal ba sogs bkur sti bla na med pa mdzad do/ /gdung sras kyang ji ltar lung bstan pa bzhin du yun ha cang mi ring ba na 'jam dpal gzhon nu bkra shis
rin chen ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas te 'khrungs pa yin zhes thos so/ /gang ltar yang 'jam mgon sku ngo rnams las chos 'brel re'ang gsan te hor zla gnyis pa'i mjug
tu e wa~M du phebs/ sku'i rkyen sel du mgon khang khag rnams su skong ba dang / yul lhar bsang mchod la sogs pa skabs su bab pa'i rim gro rnams kyang bsgrub pa dang / der
bzhugs kyi bla grwa kun la chos dang mthun pa'i mdzad sgo gong 'phel dgos pa'i zhal ta sogs stsal te/ dgung lo zhe bdun pa sna tshogs zhes pa chu pho rta'i lo'i sa ga zla
ba'i dkar phyogs kyi gral tshes bcu'i nyin spyi dang bye brag gi chibs skyel gyi tshogs rab tu mang po dang bcas te e wa~M chos ldan nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur/ mar lam
chos grwa chen po bkra shis lhun por phebs/ paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa rje btsun blo bzang dpal ldan bstan pa'i nyi mar dngos 'bul 'ga' zhig dang bcas te mjal phyag zhu
ba dang / lha khang khag rnams su mchod 'bul dang thugs smon sogs zhib par mdzad de rim gyis lha ldan

du phebs/ 'jig rten gsum gyi mchod sdong bla na med pa jo shAka rnam gnyis kyi dbus rten gsum rnams la mchod 'bul dang smon lam sogs rgyas par mdzad/ de skabs rgyal dbang thams
cad mkhyen pa'i mchog sprul tshul khrims rgya mtsho thog mar ngo 'dzin byed skabs su song gshis ma mjal la/ rgyal tshab tshe smon gling pa sogs zhib mjal zhus te rim
gyis chibs bteg /mar lam phu mdo lcags zam skor du zhag gcig bzhugs skabs rje 'dis do nub rang re rnams la chom rkun gyis nyer 'tshe 'dra 'ong las che bas bag yod par gyis
shig ces bka' stsal ba ltar/ zhabs 'bring ba rnams kyis kyang dran shes bzhin dang ldan pa'i sgo nas de nub sgar gyi mtha' bskor te nyal ba sogs byas kyang ji skad du/
'bab chu ji ltar bzlog gyur kyang / /thur du 'bab pa kho nar 'dod/ /ces pa ltar de nub chom rkun gyis rje 'di'i chibs pa dang / phyag mdzod pa'i rta gnyis khrid tshar 'dug
pa/ phyi nyin phyogs mtha' dag tu btsal rung ma rnyed pa la/ rje 'dis phyag mdzub gtad de/ ri pha ka'i rgyab tu 'tshol zhig dang nges par rnyed las che'o/ /zhes bka' stsal
pa bzhin mdzod pa nor ldan shes rab bzang po dang / rje drung bzang po blo gros gnyis 'tshol du byon pas ri de'i rtsa ba na hor pa'i tshong pa 'ga' zhig gi sgar shin
tu che ba zhig snang zhing / de nas yar byon pas ri'i sked pa tsam na sus kyang mi mthong ba'i ri sul zhig tu chibs pa gnyis kyi gdong dang rkang lag thams cad thag pas
bcings te bzhag 'dug skad/ de nas khong dag gis chibs pa gnyis khrid nas tshur byon pas der yod pa'i skye bo thams cad kyi blo la snga na med pa'i dad pa dang spro ba cig
car du 'phel par gyur to zhes grags shing / gtam 'di ni thams cad la mngon sum tshad mas grub pa zhig go /de nas rim gyis

chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur ba na/ rje 'di'i mnal lam phal che bar mi dkar po zhig gis dga' ba dang gus pa'i rnam 'gyur du ma byed cing / res rje 'di'i phyag nas brten/ res chibs
pa khrid de sde dge lhun grub steng gi rgyal khab dang nye ba'i sa ko ko la nas mar byon pa'i snang ba rtag tu byung zhing / de ni sde dge'i gzhi bdag 'bri gnyen gdong
gis thog ma'i bsu ba dang / slad nas phrin las 'ga' zhig kyang sgrub pa'i ltas yin pa 'dra gsungs/ lam bar du 'khod pa'i 'gro ba rnams la'ang chos kyi bdud rtsi cung zad
stsol bzhin pa'i sgo nas rim gyis bod chen po'i ljongs su phebs par gyur to/ /'di ni byang chub sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi rnam par thar pa yin te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
mdo sde dag las/ byang chub sems dpa' ni dpag tshad brgya'i pha rol dag tu'ang sems can rnams la chos ston du 'gro zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /de nas sde dge chos rgyal chen
pos snga phyir phebs bsu'i bkod pa rab tu mang pos mdun nas bsus shing / khyad par dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi chos grwa chen por bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun yod do cog gis
ser sbreng gi bkod pa tshar du dngar ba/ ji ltar li khri'i chu gter dal gyis bskyod pa la dbang gzhu'i ri mos mdzes par 'khyud pas skye bo rnams kyi yid kyi brtan pa cig
car du 'phrogs pas kyang dper bya bar mi bzod pa'i ngo mtshar gyi ltad mo gsar du ngoms bzhin pa'i bsu ba'i tshogs dang bcas te/ gro bzhin gyi zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi gral
tshes bcu gnyis kyi nyin/ mdo khams zal mo sgang gi sa'i thig le sde bzhi dang dge bcu'i dpal 'byor phun sum tshogs pas yongs su gtams pa'i rgyal khab chen po mi mthun
pa'i phyogs thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba ga la ba der/ nye zho'i dri ma med pa bde bar phebs

par gyur to/ /de'i tshe 'chi ba med pa'i lam gyi ngos thams cad kyang sprin dkar gyi dum bu mchod rdzas kyi dbyings can mang po ched du byas pa lta bus gtams pa'i khrod na/
kha dog lnga ldan gyi 'ja' ris rnams rang rang gi mdzes pa'i ngo mtshar ngoms pa 'dra ba sogs dkar phyogs kyi lha dang srung ma'i tshogs kyis kyang phebs bsu'i bkod pa skye
bo rnams kyi mig gi bdud rtsi zla med pa dag ston par byed cing / der 'dus pa'i 'gro ba mi dang mi ma yin pa thams cad kyis kyang mtshan dpe'i dkyil 'khor mngon sum du
mjal ba'i skal ba bzang po'i bdud rtsis yid kyi khye'u rab tu myos pas dad pa dang spro ba'i rtse dga' ci yang dgod par gyur to/ /de nyin chos rgyal mchog nas kyang thog
mar 'os pa'i dga' ston gya nom pa dag bstabs shing / zhib par sang nas mdo smad bstan 'gro yongs kyi mgon dang skyabs dang dpung gnyen dam par chos kyi rgyal srid chen
por mnga' gsol rgyu'i snyan spron rnams phul te/ de'i phyi nyin tshes bcu gsum gyi snga dro'i char rje 'di ston 'khor rnams dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi gondho la chen por
spyan drangs te/ sngon e wa~M pa'i mkhan po rim byon thams cad kyi zhabs kyi padmo rnam par bkod pa'i chos kyi khri chen por bzhugs su gsol zhing / rdo rje 'dzin dbang
'dus pa dang bcas pas 'phags yul du 'chi med grub pa'i dbang po dze tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas legs par bkral zhing / gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir rje btsun sa skya pa
yab sras brgyud 'dzin dang bcas pa la bka' babs pa'i bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag tu med pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor la brten nas zhabs pad bskal brgyar brtan pa'i gsol 'debs
kyi cho ga dang 'brel bar/ lung dang rig par smra ba'i sde snod 'dzin pa dag gis phun sum tshogs pa lnga dang /

maNDal gyi rgyas bshad 'byams klas pa'i tshig gi mchod sprin spro ba sngon du 'gro bas/ stobs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba chos rgyal chen po tshe dbang rdo rje rig 'dzin pa'i phyag
gi padmo rnam par gdengs pa'i mthil na/ stong 'khun gyi yul nas 'thon pa'i bkra shis pa'i lha reg kai lA sha ltar dkar ba thogs te gus pas 'bul ba dang / sku rten du
rgyal ba tshe dpag med la sogs pa'i sku brnyan gser zangs las grub pa kha shas dang / gsung rten du rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che pusta ka brgya dang gsum/ thugs rten
du bka' gdams mchod rten kha shas/ zangs gser las grub pa'i rgyal srid sna bdun dang / bkra shis pa'i rdzas brgyad la sogs pa dang / glang po che'i mche ba dang / gdugs dkar
po tog dang bcas pa sogs chen por 'os pa'i yo byad mang po dang / gos chen gyi bla bre dang yol ba la sogs pa gos chen las grub pa'i yo byad mang po dang / rdo dril dang
/ Da ma ru dang / ting shags dang / rol sil dang / rnga dang / dung dkar dang / dung chen dang / rgya gling la sogs pa'i mchod cha rab tu mang po dang / dngul gyi bum
pa dang / maNDal dang / dngul ting bdun tshar la sogs pa'i dngul las grub pa'i mchod cha mang po dang / dngul gyi 'dren chas cha tshang dang / dngul gyi gsol ltir dang /
shin tu rin thang che ba'i gos chen gyi rigs mang po dang / dar ras ling shug tshang la sogs pa shin tu mang po dang / shel dang dkar yol gyi rigs sna tshogs pa dang / gser
zho lnga bcu dang / rin chen gnyis pa 'degs srang sum brgya lnga bcu dang / gcan gzan gyi pags pa'i rigs rab tu mang po dang / gzim gur yol ba bcas kyi gtsos pa'i gur
g.yab kha shas/ nyer mkho'i thab cha dang bzhugs gdan gyi skor mang po/ nas khal brgya dang lnga bcu/ mar

khal brgya dang lnga bcu/ bzang ja 'khor drug brgya tham pa/ 'bri bcu/ khal nyi shu sga 'khor dang bcas pa/ mdzo mo bcu/ pho mdzo sga stan 'byar ba sum cu/ chibs sga 'khor
'dzom pa gcig dang / chibs pa gsum gyi gtso byas pa'i rta pho sum cu/ dre'u sga 'khor 'dzom pa bcu/ stan dkar brgya tham pa bcas khyon rnam grangs chig stong lnga brgya dang
lnga bcu 'bul bar mdzad cing / bka'i mdun na 'don chen pos tshig don phun sum tshogs pa'i legs 'bul gyi yig ge'ang gsal zhing brjod pa dag pas gsangs mthor sgrogs pa
dang / de'i rjes su chos rgyal chen po'i sku'i bar chad srung ba'i bla ma dang / chos khrims dang / grwa tshang dang / bka'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i mdun na 'don chen po rnams
dang / phyag mdzod dang / mdun skor dang / tshong dpon dang / dpon skya dang / hor 'dra rnams dang / lhun grub steng du gnyug mar bzhugs pa'i bla ma dang / slob dpon dang
/ chos khrims dang / spyi ba'i dus ja khag rnams dang / gzhan yang dge tshul slong rab tu mang po dang / rdzong khag chen po rnams kyi mnga' 'og tu gtogs so 'tshal gyi
bla ma dang / mi dpon dang / dgon pa dang / khyim bdag 'byor pa dang ldan pa rnams te/ de dag so so nas kyang snga na med pa'i dad pa dang spro ba phun sum tshogs pa'i
sgo nas dngos 'byor gyi 'bul ba gya nom pa dang bcas te bod chen po'i ljongs kyi bstan 'gro yongs kyi mgon du legs par mnga' gsol to/ /de lta bu'i dge tshogs thams cad kyang
byang chub snying por yongs su smin pa'i phyir 'bel ba'i gtam gyi mtshams sbyor rgyas par spros te yongs su bsngo ba'i rgyas gdab pa dang / der 'dus pa'i skye bo rnams
kyang 'phags ma gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma'i 'chi med tshe'i rjes su gnang ba sogs chos

kyi bdud rtsis tshim par mdzad do/ /de nas rim gyis rje 'dis kyang chos rgyal chen po'i spyan sngar thog ma'i zhal mjal la rong gi tshul du bkra shis pa'i lha gos kyis thog
drangs/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten khyad par du 'phags pa du ma dang / dar ras ling gos chen mgo snam snam phrug gi rigs rab tu mang po dang / /gcan gzan gyi pags rigs dang
/ shing thog gi rigs mang po dang / gser dngul la sogs pa rin po che'i rigs dang / rta drel mdzo g.yag la sogs pa rnam grangs sum brgya lhag tsam dang / chos rgyal chen
po sku sger du'ang la rong gi 'bul ba dang / bkra shis chos rdzong du bzhugs pa'i lha sras rin po che lcam sring rnams dang / dbu'i mchod gnas su gyur pa'i bla ma rnams
dang / gzhan yang bka'i blon chen rnams dang / phyag mdzod dang / tshong dpon dang / mdun skor la sogs pa rnams dang / dgon pa'i bla ma dbu chos la sogs pa rnams la'ang rang
rang gi go babs dang bstun pa'i la rong dang gnang sbyin sogs skabs su bab pa'i thugs brel rnams rim gyis bcad/ zla ba de'i mjug tu chos rgyal chen po'ang dbyar gzigs
su mgyogs skor gyis phebs pa'i sku'i rkyen sel sgrub par 'byon dgos tshul bka' stsal pa ltar/ lha lung khud/ ru dam/ rdzogs chen dgon/ yid lhung / gting lhung mdzes bum/
smad shod bkra thang sgar sogs su phebs/ nyin re bzhin chos rgyal chen por rnam dme gang rung gi khrus re dang / tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang re bcas chag med du 'bul dgos
pa dang / skabs 'gar sku rim gsar 'phar gyi rigs mang po bsgrub pa dang / mdzes bum sgar du bzhugs skabs/ de'i nye skor de'u mgo'i gzhis kar gdan drangs pa la brten/
mchog sprul rin po che 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtses kyang dgung lo gsum

bzhes pa ma yum gyi pang na 'tsho ba'i skabs thog mar mjal te gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma'i lha dgu'i rjes su gnang ba gsan pas thugs kyi sras su 'gyur ba'i rten 'byung legs
par 'grigs pas mtshon/ don du gnyer ba gzhan dag la'ang rang rang gi mos pa dang mthun pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi ci rigs par stsal te/ hor zla dgu pa'i mjug tu sde dge lhun
grub steng du phebs/ yang hor zla bcu pa'i tshes mgor chos rgyal chen po dza~M thog nor bu rtse'i rgyal khab tu thog sdud la phebs pa'i sku'i rkyen sel sgrub par phebs
dgos byung ba ltar dza~M thog tu zla gcig tsam bzhugs/ rgyun dang khyad par gyi dbang dang rjes gnang dang khrus la sogs pa rnams gang la gang dgos legs par stsal te hor
zla bcu gcig pa'i nang sde dge lhun grub steng du phebs/ hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i tshes nyer lnga nas bzung dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi drug cu dang / cho 'phrul zla bar 'du
ba chen po zhes pa ngor lugs dkyil 'khor bdun gyi sgrub mchod rnams tshogs pa'i dbu bzhugs su phebs/ mdor na de nas brtsams te dgung lo nga bdun pa chu pho 'brug lo'i
bar mdo khams su bzhugs/ thog mar lo lnga drug tsam gyi ring la bshad ma thag pa ltar gyi dbyar gzigs dang / thog sdud la bebs pa'i sku'i rkyen sel sgrub par phebs/ de rjes
rje 'di sku bsnyel gyis dogs pas dgongs khrol byung ba ltar phebs dgos ma byung / 'bri chu rong 'khris su grags par me tog la lan gsum tsam dang / sman shod phyogs su
tshar gnyis tsam dang / lan cig sga stod phyogs su phebs par lo gcig tsam 'gor ba dang / lan cig go 'jo'i phyogs su phebs par lo phyed tsam 'gor zhing / de thams cad du'ang
gdul bya rang rang gi blo dang 'tshams par zab pa dang rgya che

ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te 'gro ba chos la ma dad pa rnams dad par byas/ dad pa rnams kyang 'ga' zhig ni nyan rang gi rigs can du gyur pa la nges par 'byung ba'i gtam
gyis bden bzhi'i 'jug ldog la bkod pa dang / phal cher ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can du gyur pa la byams pa dang snying rje'i gtam gyis theg pa chen po'i lam la bkod
pa dang / skal ba dang ldan pa kha cig ni smin pa dang grol ba'i thabs la mkhas pas gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i lam la bkod cing / de thams cad kyang mthar thug bla na
med pa'i byang chub thob pa'i skal ba dang ldan pa sha stag tu mdzad de/ mdor na thub pa'i bstan pa rin po che phyogs thams cad du dar zhing rgyas par mdzad do/ /gzhan yang
sde dge lhun grub steng gi nye skor gyi khyim bdag dad pa can 'ga' zhig gis gdan drangs pa'i ngor lan kha shas byon pa ma gtogs lhun grub steng gi bla brang phan bde
kun khyab gling rang du 'khor lo gsum gyi phrin las rlabs po che dang bcas te bzhugs shing / sgo stod du phebs skabs ma gtogs lo re bzhin drug 'du'i dbu bzhugs kyang rtag
par mdzad/ rgyun du mi bdag sa'i tshangs pa chen por 'char can gyi dbang khrus rnams dang / skabs su bab pa'i sku rim gsar 'phar gyi rigs rnams bsgrub pa dang / yul phyogs
so sor bde skyid rgya cher 'byung ba'i slad du lha bum dang / klu bum dang / sa bdag gi bum pa la sogs pa tshad ldan du bsgrubs te sba ba dang / gzhan yang char 'bebs
pa la sogs pa zhi rgyas dbang drag dang rjes su 'brel ba'i mdzad phrin rnams ni re re nas smos kyis mi lang / phrin las kyi gtso bo chos 'chad pa'ang chos rgyal mchog gi
thugs bzhed ltar/ rje rang gis gsan pa'i chos phal che ba dang / khyad par mkhas grub phal cher gyi rna ba'i bcud du ma son ba'i gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras

slob bshad du grags pa'i smin byed kyi dbang dang / grol byed kyi khrid dang / rgyab rten gyi lung dang byin rlabs la sogs pa shin tu tshang ba tshar gcig bcas stsal ba dang
/ me khyi tha skar zla ba'i tshes nyer lnga'i nyin chos rgyal chen po tshe dbang rdo rje rig 'dzin pas thugs kyi kun slong nges 'byung gi bsam pa zla ba tshes pa lta bus
khyim pa'i rtags dang cha lugs thams cad spangs shing / rab tu byung ba'i rtags dang cha lugs yang dag par len pa dang / mtshan yang byams pa kun dga' sangs rgyas bstan
pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes btags shing / tshigs snga ma dge tshul gyi sdom pa dang / tshigs phyi ma bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pa rnams rim gyis nod par mdzad
do/ /spyir lam 'bras tshogs bshad cig kyang stsal dgos tshul bka' phebs par/ sa ngor gyi grwa sa rnams su ni bar chad che rigs med kyang / khams phyogs 'dir lam du song
min sna tshogs zhig byung bar snang mod/ 'on kyang bka' nan che ba ltar gsung ngag rin po che tshogs bshad kyi chos 'khor bskor ba'i dbu 'dzugs par mdzad na'ang / brgyud
pa'i khyad par gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed grub mtshams nas dgon der 'brum bu'i nad cig byung bar brten rim gyis 'phro lus par gyur pas slar 'chad par ma mdzad pa las/ gzhan
gdul bya so so'i bsam pa dang mthun par so sor thar pa'i sdom pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sems bskyed pa dang / gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i smin byed kyi dbang
bskur ba dang / grol byed kyi khrid 'bogs pa dang / byin gyis brlab pa dang / rjes su gnang ba dang / rgyab rten gyi lung la sogs pa mdor na rje rang gi gang gsan pa'i chos
rnams re re nas lan grangs mang du stsal ba dang / sa skyong chen po'i dgongs bzhed ltar/

rje nyid kyis kyang thugs bskyed kyis khyab pas sngon mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs dang / rjes su grub dbang kun dga' blo ldan sogs dam pa du ma'i bzhugs
gnas ri khrod drA ma sgang du/ rgyud sdom pa gsum gyis bsdams shing / dpal sa skya'i snyan brgyud zab mo'i nyams len thun bzhi'i rnal 'byor la khor yug tu brtson pa'i
rig pa 'dzin pa'i sgrub grwa gsar du btab pa da lta'i bar gong 'phel du gyur pa dang / dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi chos grwa chen po'i gtsos sa dgon phal che bar rim
gnyis kyi nyams len dang / cho ga'i phyag len sogs ma dag pa rnams dag par bya ba dang / dag pa rnams gong nas gong 'phel du mdzad pa yin no/ /'phags rnams bzhugs pa'i sa
phyogs ni/ /yid srubs dpung las rnam rgyal te/ /padmo'i rtsa lag shar ba na/ /mun pa'i tshogs kyis brdzi nus sam/ /de slad nam mkha'i mtshan can gyi/ /smra ba'i nyi ma nub
gyur kyang / /chos kyi zla 'di spyan 'dren slad/ /mi bdag blo gros de rjes song / /gang de'i bzhed don myur sgrub pa'i/ /pho nya'i tshogs rnams nyer lhags te/ /smra mkhas
'jam dpal dbyangs bzhin du/ /spyan 'dren gtam gyi rgyud mangs len/ /gzhan las phan phyir rang srog kyang / /bzhi mdo'i rtswa bzhin 'dor byed pa'i/ /sman mdzad de yi ye
shes ni/ /bod chen ljongs su gzigs par gyur/ /de nas dus la bab pa'i tshe/ /thub dbang 'khor gyis bskor ba ltar/ /dal gyis gshegs par gyur pa na/ /gtsang phyogs mun pa'i
gling bzhin gyur/ /bsod nams ldan pa'i mi rnams dang / /dkaraphyogs skyong ba'i srung ma gnyis/ /phan tshun ngo mtshar phung po la/ /'gran pa bzhin du bsu bar byed/ /mi
bdag la thod g.yo ba'i rtser/ /zhabs sen zla tshes rnam bkod pas/ /phyogs der nyer 'tshe'i dogs

bral zhing / /thub bstan dga' ston dar bar gyur/ /gzod ma nyid nas khams gsum gyi/ /chos kyi rgyal por mnga' brnyes kyang / /tshu rol mthong 'dis bod chen gyi/ /bstan 'gro'i
mgon du mnga' rab gsol/ /sreg byed me yis tshig min cing / /chu bo'i rgyun gyis mi 'dag pa'i/ /'gro ba'i las nyon dri ma kun/ /khyod kyi thugs rje'i chu yis bkrus/ /zab
rgyas chos kyi sman chen pos/ /'khor ba'i rims nad sel kho nas/ thub dbang rjes su bsngags min te/ /grol ba bzhi ldan 'dis kyang ngo / /de lta'i ngo mtshar mi zad pa/ /nyin
bzhin 'phel bar gyur pa 'di/ /'degs par bzod pa'i nor 'dzin ma/ /dub par ma gyur 'di ci zhig/ //gnyis pa tshogs gnyis rgya cher spel ba'i slad du dbus gtsang dag pa'i
zhing du bsnyen bkur ji ltar bstabs pa'i tshul ni/ spyir rje 'di ni mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa la dbang 'byor zhing / rnam par dkar ba'i phrin
las kyis skye rgu mtha' dag phan pa dang bde ba'i lam du bkod pa la brten nas bod chen po'i ljongs su 'khod pa'i skye 'gro mchog dman thams cad kyi gtsug gi nor bus btud
cing / rang rang gi 'byor pa'i khyad par mang pos mngon par mchod par gyur la/ de la brten nas zang zing gi longs spyod kyang rdzogs ldan gyi dus bzhin du rgyas par gyur
mod/ rgyags pa dang dregs pa lta ci/ mngon par zhen pa cung zad kyang mi mnga'/ der ma zad rang nyid bzang por bsgrub pa'i ched du dgos med kyi thabs skyong dang / rnyed
pas rnyed pa 'tshol ba dang / rab tu byung ba'i yo byad kyis khyim pa rnams kyi sems 'dzin pa la sogs pa log pa'i 'tsho ba dang / ma dag pa'i sbyin pas rang gzhan thams
cad nyes dmigs chen po la sbyor ba sogs

skye bo ngan pa'i spyod tshul thams cad rgyang ring du dor nas/ dad pa can gyis phul ba'i yo byad kyi dngos po phyag tu byung ba thams cad chud zos su ma song bar sku gsung
thugs kyi rten bzhengs pa dang / bla ma dang dkon mchog dang bstan pa dang sems can gyi ched kho nar phangs med du gtong bar mdzad pa yin te/ de'ang snga phyir sku gsung
thugs kyi rten bzhengs pa la'ang / bcom ldan 'das kun rig rnam par snang mdzad dang / gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma dang rigs gsum mgon po bcas kyi sku so sor mda' tshad re
lhag tsam yod pa/ rgyu gser zangs las grub pa/ shin tu sgros gtsang zhing phyags tshad dang ldan pa/ rin thang che ba'i rin po che mang po'i phras mdzes par spud pa sogs
lta bas chog mi shes pa lnga dang / yang gser zangs las grub pa'i jo bo'i sku rgyab yol dang bcas par mda' tshad tsam yod pa shin tu sgros legs pa gcig dang / gser zangs
las grub pa'i byang chub sems dpa' nye ba'i sras brgyad kyi sku so sor khru gang re tsam yod pa brgyad dang / yum chen mo dang / 'jam dpal smra seng dang / seng ge sgra
la sogs pa'i sku gser zangs las grub pa so sor khru gang tsam yod pa shin tu sgros legs pa kha shas dang / gser zangs las grub pa'i kun rig rtsa ba'i lha sum cu so bdun
so sor che chung gi tshad mtho gang re tsam yod pa dang / gser zangs las grub pa'i sman bla mched bdun gyi sku so sor mtho gang tsam re yod pa sogs mdor na gzhan la gtan
gzhag stsal ba dang / rang gi phyag tu bzhugs pa thams cad bsdoms na gsar du bzhengs nges pa'i gser zangs kyi sku kho na'ang brgya phrag gcig tsam yod pa dang / dngul ljang
brdungs kyi sgrol ljang khru gang tsam gcig dang / zangs kyi rnam rgyal ma mda' tshad tsam yod pa bcas kyang gsar du bzhengs pa dang /

sman 'dam las grub pa'i sku 'dra gsar bzhengs kyang mang du mchis so/ /snga phyi kun tu bris sku gsar du bzhengs pa'i skor la'ang / lam 'bras bla ma brgyud pa'i zhal thang
gras 'grig gsum/ grub chen brgyad bcu'i zhal thang gras 'grig gsum/ kye rdor lha dgu gtso bor gyur pa'i zhal thang gcig /sman bla'i zhing bkod/ /mi 'khrugs pa'i zhing bkod/
bde ba can gyi zhing bkod/ dga' ldan gyi zhing bkod/ po ta la'i zhing bkod/ sgrol ma'i zhing gi bkod pa rnams dang / ltung ba bshags pa'i lha so lnga dang / gnas brtan
bcu drug dang / rje btsun rigs byed ma dang / tshogs kyi bdag po dang / 'dod pa'i rgyal po dang / gur/ zhal/ stag zhon/ dmag zor/ bektse sogs mdor na bris thang gsar bzhengs
kho na'ang lnga bcu skor yod cing / de thams cad la'ang bzang gos gya nom pa mang po'i gong gsham dang / zhal khebs la sogs pa blta bas chog mi shes pa 'ba' zhig mdzad
pa dang / gsung gi rten yang nye bar mkho ba'i phyag dpe bris ma dang spar ma pusta ka sum cu tsam bzhengs pa dang / thugs kyi rten kyang phyis su ngor du sAtstsha 'bum
ther re bzhugs pa'i mchod rten khang bu brtsegs pa gnyis bzhengs par mdzad cing / de dag kyang sAtstsha'i gzungs gzhug dang / sAtstsha 'debs tshul dang / mchod rten phyags
tshad dang / mthar rab tu gnas pa la sogs pa rgyud nas ji skad bshad pa bzhin bsgrubs pa dang / mchod pa'i yo byad kyang rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu las grub pa'i
ting phor bdun tshar dang / yang rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu nga lnga las grub pa'i maNDal la sogs pa dngul las grub pa'i mchod cha'i rigs mang po dang / gos chen gya
nom pa mang po'i bla bre dang / phye phur dang / rgyal mtshan dang / 'phan dang /

rten khebs la sogs pa mang du bzhengs par mdzad de/ de'ang rten khebs lta bur mtshon na/ gzhan la sbyor 'jags stsal ba dang / rang nyid kyi phyag tu bzhugs pa sogs snga phyir
bzos tshad brtsis na bzang gos las grub pa'i rten khebs kho na'ang brgya dang nyi shu skor zin pa dang / dkon mchog gi mchod pa dang dge 'dun gyi bsnyer bkur yang / sde
dge lhun grub steng du sngon mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong gi sku dus nas srol dod pa lta bu'i lo re bzhin gyi hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i tshes gnam gang nyin/ drug 'du'i
dbu bzhugs su yin gyis 'dus tshogs spyir tshe chog dang / mgon khang khag rnams su skong ba dang / chos sgrogs pa mang pos gsung rab bklag pa dang / der 'dus pa'i gsang
sngags rnying ma'i bla ma dge slong sngags pa bcas la'ang phyag 'gyed dang rnam gzhag sogs gtong ba'i rgyun mchis pa rnams kyang ma chag par yar ldan du mdzad pa dang /
der ma zad bla brang phan bde kun khyab gling rang du'ang lo re bzhin cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes gcig nas bco lnga'i bar la rje rang gi grwa tshang gang yod kyi steng lhun
grub steng gi dge slong bzhi lnga re bsnan te bla ma mchod pa dang / gnas bcu'i cho ga dang / maNDal bzhi chog sogs gsung ba dang chabs cig nyin re bzhin spos/ mar me/ zhal
zas rnams brgya rtsa re nges par ma chag par mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang zla ba byung ngo cog gi nya stong tshes brgyad phal che bar bla ma mchod pa'am bstan pa gso chog
lta bu'i cho ga gang rung re dang 'brel bar brgya mchod re chag med lta bur mdzad pa dang / skabs skabs su rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur ro cog sgrogs pa sogs bsod nams kyi tshogs
'du bgyis pa'i gtong phod chen po'i sgo 'phar rtag tu dbye bzhin pa dang / khyad par dgung lo nga drug pa lcags mo yos kyi lo'i hor zla lnga pa'i nang / shi gson gyi
dad rdzas mtha' dag chud mi 'dza' zhing dge tshogs

gong 'phel du bya ba'i phyir/ dbus gtsang ljongs kyi bla ma dang dkon mchog la mchod pa dang / dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur rgya cher bsgrub pa'i slad du phyag rdzas ji yod bskur
te rje drung bzang po blo gros dpon 'khor rnams gtong gnang mdzad pa bzhin khong rnams kyang bar chad med par rim gyis byon te/ byang rwa sgreng gi chos grwa chen po nas
bzung / bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa skya'i bar gyi ris med pa'i dgon sde so so'i bla ma rnams su 'bul ba/ rten gsum yongs la mchod 'bul/ dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtshor
bsnyen bkur rnams dpyis phyin par bsgrubs pa dang / khyad par ngor rang du'ang bla khag so sor 'bul ba dang / dgon par mang 'gyed kyi bsnyen bkur nyin bcu'i bar gang
zab dang / gos chen gyi bla bre dang / 'phan la sogs pa mtshar zhing yid du 'ong ba dag sbyor 'jags zhus pa sogs/ mdor na rwa sgreng nas sa skya'i bar du ja dngul song tshad
thams cad ja thog tu phab ste brtsis pas bzang ja 'khor drug brgyad brgya dang lnga bcu tham pa song 'dug pa dang / de'i rigs 'gres sku gsung thugs rten/ mchod cha'i
skor sna tshogs/ dar ras ling gos chen la sogs pa dang / gcan gzan gyi pags pa'i rigs dang / thab cha'i rigs la sogs pa ji snyed cig song ba rnams ni smos kyis mi long /
'bul bar song ba'i rta phyugs kyi rigs kyang rta drel lnga bcu tham pa dang / mdzo g.yag lnga bcu nga grangs tsam song ba sogs mdor na snying po med pa'i zang zing gi dngos
po rnams kyang snga na med pa'i bsod nams kyi phung por bsgyur bar mdzad pa dang / dgung lo nga bdun pa dga' ba zhes pa chu pho 'brug gi lor/ sdom brtson skye rgu'i bdag
po byams pa kun dga' sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan pa dbus gtsang phyogs kyi rten gsum rnams mjal zhing mchod 'bul dang

bsnyen bkur rgya chen pos bsod nams kyi tshogs 'du bgyi ba'i slad du 'byon rgyu'i skabs/ de'i 'gal rkyen sel zhing mthun rkyen gong 'phel du 'gyur ba'i slad du rje 'di la chibs
bskyod bskyang dgos tshul bka' phebs par/ snga lo phyag rdzas ji yod bskur te rje drung dpon 'khor rnams dbus gtsang du btang zin pa da lta phyir ma 'khor ba'i skabs
'dir phebs chas sogs gang ci nas 'grig dka' bar brten/ nan tan gyis dgongs khrol zhu bar mdzad na'ang dgongs pa khrol pa zhig gtan nas ma byung bas phebs rgyu mdzad de/
phebs chas sogs nyer bsdogs mdzad pa dang / don du gnyer ba so so'i chos kyi 'phro rnams kyang rdzogs par mdzad pa dang / khyim bdag dad pa can dag gis kyang rang rang gi
khyim du gdan drangs te 'dod chos re tsam zhu ba sogs kyi re ba rnams kyang rdzogs par mdzad cing / de skabs su phyag sna cung mdzangs pa'i skabs lta bur gyur mod/ 'on kyang
skyes bu blo stobs dang ldan pa rnams kyi thabs kyis bsgrubs na rnyed par dka' ba ma yin pa la/ de bas nor rdzas snying po med pa rnams snying po dang ldan pa'i bsod
nams kyi phung por bsgyur nus pa ni 'jig rten na shin tu dkon zhing ngo mtshar che ba yin no snyam du dgongs te/ nor rdzas sgyu ma lta bu las snying po len pa'i phyir du
'byor pa dang ldan pa 'ga' zhig las ja dngul cung zad kyang g.yar te/ chos rgyal chen po hor zla bzhi pa'i gza' skar legs 'dzom gyi nyin dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi rgyal
khab nas chibs bteg /rje 'di hor zla lnga pa'i tshes lnga'i nyin chibs bteg ste/ yar lam zul phu stod smad/ mkhar mdo/ khra bo thang / gdong tshang dgon rnams su dad pa
can so sos ji ltar gsol ba btab pa bzhin rang rang gi khyim du byon pa dang / chos kyi bdud rtsi'ang ci rigs par stsal te rim gyis rdo ra dmar kor

byon/ de nas mchod yon lhan rgyas te chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur/ rje drung dpon 'khor rnams kyang dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing du bsnyen bkur legs par bgyis zin nas mar byon pa
dang rtsi ge sar 'ben de'u'i mar thang zhig tu mjal/ de nas rje drung dpon 'khor rnams mdo khams su byon/ rje 'dis skabs su bab pa'i chos rgyal mchog gi thugs bzhed rnams
kyang sgrub bzhin pa'i sgo nas hor zla brgyad pa'i tshes gcig nyin bkra shis dbu ma thang du phebs/ de nas chos rgyal chen po lha ldan phyogs su sngon du phebs/ rje 'di
zhag gnyis gsum gyi rjes nas chibs bteg ste byang rwa sgreng gi chos grwa chen por phebs/ rA sgreng khri chen rin po cher maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ dar/ ras/ ling / spu
shun gyi rigs mang po dang / ljon 'dab 'khor drug bcu/ rta drel gnyis bcas phul ba dang / rwa sgreng tA bla mar yang ja gsar gong 'os phul ba dang / khyad par dgon de'i
rten gsum yongs la mchod 'bul dang / snyan dar gang zab/ 'dus tshogs spyir mang ja'i bsnyen bkur rnams zab par zhus te dpal stag lung gi chos grwa chen por phebs/ stag lung
bla ma rin po cher 'bul ba/ rten gsum yongs la mchod 'bul/ 'dus tshogs su mang ja'i bsnyen bkur rnams mdzad nas dar lung gnyan gyi pho brang dang / rdo rje'i gnas chen
brag yer pa rnams su'ang gnas mjal dang mchod 'bul legs par mdzad de/ chos dang srid kyi 'byor pa phun sum tshogs pa'i chu rgyun mtha' dag gcig tu 'khyil ba'i gnas/ yul
dbus 'gyur 'chang gi lte ba lha ldan du khrums zla'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin phebs/ thog mar 'phags pa lag na padmo'i rnam par 'phrul pa rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa tshul
khrims rgya mtsho'i gser zhal rin po che

legs par mjal ba dang chabs cig /maNDal sku gsung thugs rten dang / gsol ja bzhes 'bras kyi dod Tam srang brgyad phul bstun/ maNDal sku gsung thugs rten rnams gzhung rang nas
stsal ba'i lam srol mchis pa ltar/ gus pas 'bul ba sngon du 'gro bas/ dar/ ras/ ling / gos chen gyi rigs dang / spu shun gyi rigs rab tu mang po dang / mchod cha sogs
dngos chas sna tshogs pa dang / rgya dngul 'degs srang brgya tham pa/ bod dngul Tam srang lnga bcu tham pa/ bzang ja 'khor drug bcu/ rta drel bdun bcas 'bul bar mdzad pa
dang / chos srid phrin las kyi 'khor los sgyur ba srid skyong tshe smon gling par yang / maNDal sku gsung thugs rten gsol ja bzhes 'bras kyi dod dngul Tam srang brgyad dang
/ dar/ ras/ ling / gos chen gyi rigs dang / spu shun gyi rigs mang po dang dngos chas kyi rigs sna tshogs pa dang / rin chen gnyis pa Tam srang brgya tham pa/ bzang ja
'khor drug lnga/ rta drel gsum bcas 'bul lam zhus par/ phyir slog tu na bza' sku chas sogs rgya che ba dang / yas phyir gyi lam yig dang / dos rta/ rtswa shing sogs phon
che ba dang / ja yod rigs la ja khral rtsa chag sogs bka' drin mtshungs zla med par stsal ba dang / bstan rgyas gling / kun bde gling / tshe chog gling rnams dang / dga'
ldan khri rin po che sogs su'ang 'bul ba gang zab dang / gzhan yang bka'i blon chen rnams dang / spyi khyab mkhan po dang / rtse shod kyi gsol gzim mgron gnyer rnams dang
/ lha sa bla brang gi phyag mdzod pa dang / gnyer tshang pa dang / rtse'i phyag mdzod pa dang / gnyer tshang pa dang / mi dpon dang / rtswa gnyer dang / shing gnyer sogs
la'ang go babs dang bstun pa'i ja gsar skabs su gang bab re stsal ba dang / khyad par srid zhi'i mchod sdong mtshungs zla ma mchis

pa ston mchog thub pa'i dbang po'i sku brnyan rnam pa gnyis kyi gtsos pa'i rten gsum phal che bar zhal gser gsol ba dang / dar gos gya nom pa mang po'i snyan dar phul ba dang
/ khyad par jo shAka rnam gnyis kyi mdun stong mchod shin tu rgyas pa dang / lha khang gzhan rnams su mchod 'bul gang zab re mdzad pa dang / smon lam chen mo'i skabs kyi
'dus tshogs rin po cher mang ja gnyis kyi bsnyen bkur zhu ba'i dod du bzang ja 'khor drug bdun cu tham pa lha sa bla brang gi phyag mdzod par 'bul lam zhus pa dang / rtse
rnam rgyal grwa tshang / gling khag gsum gyi grwa tshang / tshe chog gling / 'bras spungs 'dus spyi/ de'i nang gses gling khang tshan/ se ra 'dus spyi/ de'i nang gses
tre bo khang tshan/ dga' ldan/ rgyud stod smad/ rme ru/ bzhi sde rnams su mang ja'i bsnyen bkur zab pa dang / nA lendra/ ra bstod sogs lha ldan dang nye ba'i dgon pa rnams
su'ang mang ja dang / bsngo 'brel sogs 'bul lam zhu rgyu bskur bar mdzad de/ thog mar rje 'di lho gnas zhig la phebs rtsis mdzad rung / sa skya nas 'jam mgon khri chen
rin po che ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang pos kyang mi ring bar 'byon dgos tshul gyi bka' mchid dbyangs kyi rgyal mo'i rgyud mangs nas drangs
pa lta bu phebs pa sogs kyis sde dge chos rgyal chen por yang snyan spron phul te/ rje 'di hor zla brgyad pa'i mjug tu lha ldan nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur/ yar lam snye
thang sgrol ma dang / rong byams chen rnams kyang mjal/ mchod 'bul dang / mang ja'i bsnyen bskur sogs zhus te rim gyis gzhis rtser phebs/ de skabs paN chen rin po che chab
bzhes su phebs nas ma bzhugs par brten bkras lhun du rjes su phebs rgyu mdzad de/ gzhis

rtser zhag gsum tsam bzhugs nas hor zla dgu pa'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin e wa~M pa'i bla khag khang tshan dang bcas pa'i phebs bsu dang / thab bsu dang / 'dus tshogs kyi ser
sbreng gi bkod pa lta bas chog mi shes pa dang bcas te/ yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal e wa~M chos ldan du nyer 'tshe'i dri mas ma gos par bde bar phebs par
gyur to/ /de nas kyang gza' skar legs 'dzom gyi nyin e wa~M bla brang du gzhung du mdo sngags bstan pa'i mnga' bdag mkhan rin po che las thog pa byams pa dpal ldan bzang
po'i mdun du/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang / dar/ ras/ ling / spu shun gyi rigs mang po dang / mchod cha dang thab cha sogs dngos chas kyi rigs sna tshogs pa dang / ljon
'dab 'khor drug nyer lnga/ rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu tham pa/ rta drel lnga/ mdzo g.yag brgyad bcas 'bul bar mdzad pa dang / bla brang phun tshogs khang gsar du lung
rig smra ba'i gtsug rgyan mkhan rin po che ngag dbang blo gros bzang po pa dang / klu ldings bla brang du zhabs drung rin po che dpal ldan phun tshogs pa dang / phan bde
khang gsar du zhabs drung rin po che kun dga' bstan pa'i blo gros pa ste so so'i mdun du'ang sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang / dar ras ling sogs dang / spu shun gyi rigs
mang po/ mchod cha dang thab cha sogs dngos chas kyi rigs sna tshogs pa dang / ljon ja 'khor drug bco lnga re/ rgya dngul 'degs srang bco lnga re/ rta drel gnyis re/ mdzo
g.yag lnga re bcas phul ba dang / thar rtse rang du'ang rnam dkar mchod thebs kyi rten du 'bul ba shin tu stobs che ba dang / e wa~M pa'i lha khang rnams su'ang mchod 'bul
gang rgyas dang / khyad par gtsug lag khang du mchod pa zab pa dang bcas te dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtshos bla ma mchod pa dang / kun rig gi

cho ga dang tshe chog sogs nyin nyer gsum gyi bar 'tshogs par mdzad pa'i thog mar nyin bcu la phyag 'gyed ja gtang bar dge 'dun bco lnga re la ljon ja sbag re phul ba dang
/ yang nyin bcu gnyis la dngul 'gyed btang bar nyin re bzhin grwa pa re la dngul Tam phyed re phul ba dang / yang nyin gcig la dge slong re la phyag 'gyed Tam re phul ba
ste/ mdor na nyin nyer gsum gyi bar du bsnyen bkur rgyas par mdzad pa dang / gtsug lag khang du bzang gos kyi 'phan sogs sbyor 'jags stsal ba dang / gzhan yang dgon pa'i
dbu chos rnams su 'bul ba dang ja gsar gang zab/ khang tshan bcu gcig po so sor rang rang gi thob khungs dang khang tshan che chung la gzhig pa'i ja gsar dang gtan bzhag
gang zab re dang / bla khag so so'i phyag gnyer las tshan gyi rigs dang / thar rtse rang gi las tshan dang / ban tshang dang / lto zan gyi rigs dang / ngor pa'i chos gzhis
kyi mi ser sogs la'ang ja gsar dang gnang sbyin sogs skabs su gang bab re dang / rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sde/ de'i nang tshan gur pa grwa tshang / zhwa lu chos sde/
srad rgyud pa/ srad dgon pa khra mo rnams su mang ja'i bsnyen bkur sogs mdzad do/ /sde dge chos rgyal chen po'ang ris su med pa'i dgon khag so sor bsnyen bkur rgya cher stsol
bzhin pa'i sgo nas hor zla bcu pa'i nang snga phyi'i phebs bsu dang ser sbreng gi tshogs dang bcas te e wa~M du phebs/ bla khag so sor 'bul ba dang / rten gsum rigs
la mchod 'bul dang / 'dus tshogs su mang 'gyed kyi bsnyen bkur sogs byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i rnam par thar pa la co 'dri ba bzhin mdzad/ rje 'di las nA ro mkha'
spyod ma'i khrid dang / kye rdor rgyu lam gyi dbang la sogs pa'i bka' chos 'ga' zhig gsan te hor zla bcu gcig pa'i nang sa skyar phebs/ rje 'di'ang zla ba de'i mjug
tu sa la gnas pa'i 'og min chen po dpal ldan sa skyar phebs te/ khri chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po'i gser zhal rin
po che

mjal ba dang chabs cig sa skya gzhung gi 'bul bar/ maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ dar/ ras/ ling / gos chen gyi rigs dang / spu shun gyi rigs mang po/ mchod cha dang gos chas
dang thab cha sogs dngos chas kyi rigs sna tshogs/ rgya dngul 'degs srang brgya tham pa/ ljon ja 'khor drug lnga bcu/ rta drel bzhi bcas phul ba dang / khri chen rin po
che sku sger gyi 'bul bar/ dar/ ras/ ling la sogs pa'i tshan grangs dang / ljon ja 'khor lnga/ chibs pa gcig bcas phul ba dang / sngags 'chang bdud kyi stobs 'phrog ngag
dbang kun dga' rin chen pa dang / mkhyen brtse nus pa'i dbang phyug mgon po dngos grub dpal 'bar ba dang / mdo sngags bstan pa'i mnga' bdag 'jam mgon kun dga' rgyal mtshan
pa dang / mkhas grub rgya mtsho'i gtsug rgyan rje btsun 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma bcas kyi sku sger so sor yang / dar/ ras/ ling la sogs pa'i tshan grangs dang / ljon
ja 'khor drug gsum re/ chibs pa re re bcas dang / gdung sras 'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen pa dang / ngag dbang bkra shis rin chen pa gnyis kyi sku sger so sor yang ljon ja
'khor drug gsum re dang tshan grangs kha shas/ gzhan yang bkra shis brtsegs su bzhugs pa'i rje btsun ma/ zhabs brtan lha khang du bzhugs pa'i rje btsun ma/ btsun mo pho brang
gi rje btsun ma gnyis dang / bde mchog rje btsun ma/ khro khang rje btsun ma bcas dang / lha khang mkhan rin po che bcas su so sor tshan grangs kha shas dang / ljon
ja 'khor drug re re/ sa skya zhabs pad par ljon 'dab 'khor drug gsum dang / rta gcig /gzhan yang gsol gzim dang / mgron gnyer dang / drung yig dang / lde phyung ba dang /
rtswa gnyer dang / shing gnyer sogs la'ang 'dris zab dang bstun pa'i ja gsar skabs su gang bab re dang / khyad par phyogs de'i rten gsum ngo mtshar

can rnams kyi drung du mchod 'bul dang gser gsol dang / dar gos gya nom pa mang po'i snyan dar 'bul ba dang / sprul pa'i lha khang chen mor dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtshor mang
ja gnyis kyi steng phyag 'gyed zab par phul ba dang / 'jam mgon khri chen rin po ches bka' chos 'ga' zhig dgos tshul phebs pa rnams kyang thugs bzhed bzhin phul te e wa~M
du phebs/ de rjes hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i mjug tu chos grwa chen po bkra shis lhun por phebs te/ paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa rje btsun blo bzang dpal ldan bstan pa'i nyi
ma'i mtshan dpe'i dkyil 'khor mjal ba dang lhan cig /maNDal sku gsung thugs rten gsol ja bzhes 'bras kyi dod dngul Tam srang brgyad dang / dar/ ras/ ling / gos chen gyi
rigs dang / spu shun gyi rigs dang / mchod cha'i rigs la sogs pa dang / rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu tham pa/ ljon ja 'khor drug sum cu so lnga/ rta drel lnga bcas phul
ba dang / zhabs pad mdun du'ang tshan grangs kha shas dang / ljon ja 'khor drug lnga/ rta gcig bcas dang / gzhan yang rtse'i gsol gzim mgron gnyer phyag mdzod sogs su'ang
'dris zab dang bstun pa'i ja gsar gang 'tsham re dang / khyad par dgon de'i rten gsum yongs la mchod 'bul dang / 'dus tshogs spyir mang ja'i bsnyen bkur dang / de'i
nang gses rgya khang tshan par mang ja dang ja gsar sogs zab par mdzad de e wa~M du phebs/ mdor na snga na med pa'i gtong phod kyi gru char gshin pos tshogs gnyis kyi snye
ma dgung la reg par mdzad pa yin no/ /brtan zhing sra ba'i rgyas btab pa'i/ /lhun po dag kyang tha mar 'jig /dngos kun mi rtag chos nyid can/ /'di la phyir bcos su yis
shes/ /de bas sgyu ma'i longs spyod kyis/ /bsod nams gter chen bsgrub bya zhes/ /kun gyi blo yi bsgo skal ni/ /

gang 'di gcig pus thob pa bzhin/ /sna tshogs nor gyi 'du byed kyis/ /rten gsum rdul snyed bsgrubs bgyis kyang / /gzhar yang 'dzad par ma gyur pa'i/ /srid 'di'i 'byor pa shin
tu mang / /khyad par srid pa'i longs spyod kyis/ /zhi bde 'gugs pa'i bya ma rta/ /ched du mngags pa'i rig sngags 'dis/ /kun kyang bsod nams dpal la sbyar/ /gang de'i 'byor
pa'i khyad par gyi/ /mi zad nam mkha' mdzod kyi sgo/ /ru bzhi'i ljongs su phye ba ni/ /gdengs can gtsug gi nor bu bzhin/ /shin tu gtong ba'i sbyin pas kyang / /tshim
med bdag nyid che 'di mtshar/ /'on te dbyar gyi dpal mo yis/ /phan pa ster la ngoms ma gyur/ /gang phyir mchog gi zhabs skyes rdul/ /yul dbus sman ljongs la bkod pas/ /skal
bzang dga' ba'i dga' ston dang / /dad dang dpal 'byor lhan cig 'phel/ /rab 'byams mchod pa'i sprin chen gyis/ /phyogs kun dog por 'gengs pa 'dis/ /kun bzang rnam par 'phrul
pa la/ /'gro 'di'i gud pa lhod kyis dogs// //gsum pa slar yang mdo khams su byon nas bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ de'ang 'di ltar rjes su thos te/
sde dge chos rgyal chen por rje 'dis sku na mtho ba sogs kyis slar mdo khams su 'byon mi dgos pa'i dgongs khrol yar lam byang thang nas bzung ste zhu bar mdzad par/ ha lam
dgongs khrol yong rtsis lta bu yin pa la/ chos rgyal chen po sa skyar phebs skabs da dung lan cig mdo khams su ma byon pa'i thabs med tshul gyi bka' nan phebs par/ yang
bskyar dgongs khrol zhu bar mdzad na'ang dgongs pa khrol ba zhig gtan nas ma byung bar brten lan cig mdo khams su chibs kyi gdong bsgyur bar thag bcad/ sde dge'i chos rgyal
chen po hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i nang sa skya nas ngor du phebs/ der

zhag bcu skor tsam bzhugs nas lha ldan du sngon nas phebs/ rje 'di chu sbrul hor zla dang po'i mjug tu sa skya nas 'jam mgon khri chen rin po ches bang mi ched gtong gi bka'
nan gong che phebs pa la brten sa skyar phebs/ 'jam mgon khri chen rin po che dang / de sras bkra shis rin chen bcas su gsang 'dus 'jam rdor gyi dbang dang / gshed dmar
lha lnga'i smin byed kyi dbang dang grol byed spros med kyi khrid la sogs pa'i bka' chos rnams thugs bzhed bzhin phul/ gsang 'dus 'jam rdor gyi dbang stsal ba'i nyin khri
chen rin po ches rje 'di gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rjer dngos su gzigs/ de nub khri chen rin po ches dam rdzas stong rdo dang / khri rdo mang po rje 'di la phul zhing
thugs dgyes tshor dang bsngags brjod mtha' yas pa mdzad ces grags/ 'jam mgon dngos grub dpal 'bar nas kyang tshe dbang sogs rkyen sel 'ga' zhig dgos tshul phebs pa bzhin
