'bul bar mdzad/ tshur yang sku ngo rnams las gong du thos pa mdzad pa'i skabs su bshad pa ltar gyi bka' chos ci rigs pas gsan te e wa~M du phebs/ mdo khams su phebs rgyu'i
sta gon sogs skabs su bab pa'i thugs brel rnams rim gyis bcad/ hor zla bzhi pa'i mjug mdo khams su phebs nye'i skabs sa skya nas 'jam mgon khri chen rin po ches sa
skyar lan cig ma byon thabs med yin tshul gyi bka' nan phebs par brten/ ngor nas sa skya bar zhag gcig mdzad de phebs/ sa skyar nyin zhag lnga bzhugs/ de'i bar la 'jam mgon
khri chen rin po ches rgyun du nyams bzhes bskyangs pa'i thugs dam gyi lha gang yod kyi dbang dang rjes gnang rnams thugs bzhed bzhin phul/ sa skya nas ngor bar zhag gcig
mdzad de phebs/ de nas dgung grangs

nga brgyad pa rnam rgyal zhes pa chu mo sbrul gyi lo'i hor zla bzhi pa'i dmar phyogs kyi rdzogs pa gsum pa'i nyin spyi dang bye brag gi chibs skyel gyi tshogs dang bcas te
yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal e wa~M chos ldan nas chibs bteg /mar lam byang brgyud kyis phebs te hor zla lnga pa'i mjug tu bkra shis dbu ma thang du phebs/
/de nas mchod yon lhan rgyas pa'i sgo nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur/ mdo khams sde dge'i rgyal khab nas snga phyir phebs bsu'i tshogs nyi zer gyi rdul ltar lhags pa rnams dang
lhan cig rim gyis byon/ hor zla brgyad pa'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin dgon pa'i ser sbreng la sogs pa phebs bsu'i bkod pa lta bas chog mi shes pa sa dang nam mkha'i kha dog
kyang bsgyur bsnyam byed pa dang bcas te/ dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi rgyal khab chen por nyer 'tshe'i dri ma med par mchod yon thams cad bde bar phebs par gyur to/ /de
nas bzung ste dgung grangs re gnyis pa me bya lo'i bar lo bzhi mdo khams su bzhugs/ nye skor gyi sbyin bdag dad pa can rnams kyis gdan drangs pa'i ngor lan kha shas phebs
pa ma gtogs gzhan phyogs gang du'ang ma phebs/ lo re bzhin drug 'du'i dbu bzhugs kyang rtag par mdzad/ rgyun du chos rgyal mchog gi thugs bzhed ltar gyi dbang khrus rigs
'bul ba dang / rgyal khab chen po der 'phral yun kun tu bde skyid rgya cher 'byung ba'i slad du sku rim gsar 'phar gyi rigs mang po bsgrub pa dang / khyad par chos rgyal
mchog gis slar yang gsol ba btab pa bzhin du/ grub chen birWa pa'i thugs bcud thun mong ma yin pa gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras slob bshad du grags pa'i smin grol yongs
su rdzogs pa shin tu rgyas pa tshar gcig dang / nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i smin grol yongs su rdzogs pa dang / gzhan yang sa skya pa'i gser chos kyi skor dang /

mgon po che chung gi skor la sogs pa dang / don du gnyer ba'i gdul bya gzhan dag gi ngor yang so sor thar pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / khyad par gsang sngags rdo rje
theg pa'i spyi bka'i skor dang / bye brag rgyud sde so so'i smin byed kyi dbang bskur ba dang / rjes su gnang ba dang / grol byed kyi khrid dang / rgyab rten gyi lung
la sogs pa mdor na chos kyi 'khor lo bar ma chad par bskor te gdul bya mtha' dag rnam par grol ba'i 'byor pa dang ldan par mdzad pa dang / phyogs der sa dgon ji snyed cig
mchis pa rnams kyi gtsos grub mtha' ris med pa'i chos sde rnams su mo khrims dang chang khrims shin tu dam par bsdams pas mtshon dge 'dun gyi sgrig lam lhod pa rnams gsar
du bsdams pa dang / grwa grangs nyung ba rnams mang por bsgyur ba dang / chos rgyal chen po dang bka' mol mdzad de/ ze chen dgon nas ma hA paNDi ta 'jam dpal dgyes pa'i
blo gros dang / dpal sa skya nas dga' ldan dpon slob rin po che lung dang rig par smra ba byams pa smon lam grags pa dag chos grwa chen po lhun grub steng du gdan drangs
te phyi nang gi rig pa'i gnas yan lag dang bcas pa'i bshad grwa btsugs pa dang / mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i sdom pa gsum gyi rab tu dbye ba'i spyi
don dang / 'grel pa sogs spar du bzhengs pas mtshon/ mdor na yon mchod gnyis kas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa'i dus la 'gran pa bzhin rgyas par
mdzad pa yin no/ /gzhan yang yul phyogs de nyid kyi nad rims la sogs pa'i mi 'dod pa'i rkyen ngan pa thams cad zhi ba dang / dpal dang 'byor pa mtha' dag rgyas par bya
ba dang / phun sum tshogs rgu thams cad dbang du bsdu ba dang / mi dang mi ma yin gyi nyer 'tshe mtha' dag rgyang ring

du bskrad pa la sogs pa zhi rgyas dbang drag dang rjes su 'brel ba'i sgo nas phyogs de'i bde skyid dgung la reg par mdzad pa yin la/ 'di skabs bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma
dam pa mkhas btsun grub pa'i khyu mchog zhabs drung rin po che 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan pa'ang bod nas phebs te sku rtsar bcar bzhugs kyi ngos gsung gi bdud rtsi
mtha' yas pa bzhes pa sogs thugs sras kyi dwang mar gyur pa yin no/ /kun gyi bran bzhin 'gro don la/ /brtson pas rang bde thob pa rnams/ /rtag tu gzhan la phan pa'i las/
/rang gi srog bzhin 'dor mi byed/ /kun la snyoms pa'i nyi 'od kyis/ /padmo lhag par dga' byed ltar/ /thugs rjer nye ring ma mchis kyang / /skal par ldan rnams rjes su
'dzin/ /smon lam g.yab mos bos pa yi/ /lus can thar par bkri ba'i slad/ /brtson 'grus shing rta la 'dzegs te/ /bod chen ljongs su gshegs par gyur/ /ngan par spyad rnams g.yang
sa las/ /bsgral nas yang dag lam bzang la/ /sbyar mdzad rnam thar dpag dka' ba/ /rgyal ba rnams dang khyad par gang / /srid zhi ji bzhin gzigs pa'i nyis/ /bde chen
ye shes cher bskyed de/ /sdug kun drung phyung bdud dpung btul/ /mgon pos chos 'khor yongs rdzogs bskor/ /thub bstan dbyar gyi mtsho bzhin du/ /spel ba'i dge mtshan phung
po 'dis/ /sngon byon mkhan slob chos gsum gyi/ /grags pa'ang nyams par byas kyis dogs/ /khyod kyi phrin las zla 'od kyis/ /phun tshogs chu gter 'phel bgyid pa'i/ /sngon
med ngo mtshar blta ba'i slad/ /nyi zla skar tshogs lhags par nges// //gsum pa slar yang rang gnas gdan sa chen por zhabs bkod de bstan 'gro'i don ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul
la gnyis te/ thog mar gtong ba chen po'i sgo 'phar yangs por phyes te bsod nams kyi

tshogs 'du mdzad pa sngon du 'gro ba'i zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos 'khor ji ltar bskor ba'i tshul dang / byang phyogs bod kyi rgyal po gzhung sa dga' ldan pho brang pa chen
pos chen por 'os pa'i mtshan dang yo byad kyis chen po'i go sar mnga' gsol nas rnam dkar gyi phrin las ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul lo/ /de'i dang po ni 'di ltar rjes su
thos te/ rje 'di mkhyen brtse nus gsum gyi yon tan mtshungs zla ma mchis par brten zang zing gi longs spyod dbyar mtsho bzhin 'phel bar gyur mod/ ji skad du/ dbu ma bshes
pa'i spring yig las/ longs spyod g.yo ba snying po med mkhyen nas/ /dge slong bram ze bkren dang bshes rnams la/ /sbyin pa tshul bzhin stsal bgyi pha rol tu/ /sbyin las
gzhan pa'i gnyen mchog ma mchis so/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar snying po med pa'i nor rdzas rnams las snying po dam pa len pa'i phyir du dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing du bsnyen bkur
stob pa dang / rje rang yang sku tshe'i smad du 'du 'dzi dang rnam g.yeng spangs te bshad sgrub la brtson pa lhur bzhes pa'i slad du chos rgyal chen por dgongs khrol yang
yang zhu bar mdzad par rim gyis me bya lor bod du 'byon chog pa'i dgongs khrol byung bar brten/ de skor gyi nyer bsdogs rnams brtsams pa dang / don gnyer so so'i chos
kyi 'phro rnams kyang rdzogs par mdzad pa dang / nye skor gyi dgon khag so sor mang ja dang 'gyed chas gtan gzhag sogs gya nom pa dang / khyad par lhun grub steng gi chos
grwa chen por dge 'dun bdun brgya tsam bzhugs pa thams cad kyis kun rig gi cho ga nyin bzhi lnga tsam tshogs par nyin re bzhin dge 'dun brgyad re la phyag 'gyed ljon ja
sbag re dang / bcu re la ljon ja sbag re spel mar mdzad pa dang lhan cig lhun grub steng gi gtsug lag khang du gos chen bzang bsgrigs kyi phye phur cha dang /

gos yug gi 'phan bcas sbyor 'jags mdzad pa dang / phan bde kun khyab gling gi bla brang rang du'ang / chos rgyal mchog gi dbu'i mchod gnas rim byon gyi nyer mkho'i sbyor 'jags
su/ gser zangs las grub pa'i bcu gcig zhal rgyab yol dang bcas par khru phyed do tsam yod pa zhig dang / gzhan yang mkhar rag dang sman 'dam las grub pa'i sku 'dra kha
shas/ ston pa gtso bor bzhugs pa'i nye sras brgyad kyi zhal thang gras 'grig dgu/ 'jam dbyangs stong sku'i gser thang gras 'grig lnga/ rnam rgyal stong sku'i zhal thang
gras 'grig lnga/ grub chen brgyad bcu'i zhal thang gras 'grig dgu/ gzhan yang mdzad bcu'i zhal thang dang / 'od dpag med kyi zhing bkod dang / kun rig rtsa lha dang / mkha'
spyod ma dang / rnam par rgyal ma dang / sgrol ljang dang / yang grub chen brgyad cu dang / chos srung stag zhon dang / rnam sras rta bdag brgyad la sogs pa'i zhal thang
mang po dang / gsung gi rten du 'bum pusta ka bcu gnyis can gnyis dang / brgyad stong pa dang / sangs rgyas mtshan 'bum dang / grwa tog gser gsum dang / bka' thang sde
lnga dang / klu 'bum dkar nag khra gsum bcas kyi glegs bam dang / thugs kyi rten du gser zangs las grub pa'i bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad dang / li'i mchod rten bcas dang
/ mchod pa'i yo byad kyi skor la/ gos chen gser ma'i phye phur gsar legs cha gcig dang / gos chen gyi rgyal mtshan gsar pa cha dang / gos chen gyi yol ba dang / gos chen
gyi ka 'phan bzang zhan brgyad tsam dang / ras khra'i gnam rgyan kha shas dang / gos chen gyi g.yab dar dang / rkang gling cha dang / li rag sogs las grub pa'i phud phor
dang mchod kong che 'bring sna tshogs pa dang / chos srung rnams kyi spyan gzigs su ral gri gser shan

can dang / me mda' lnga dang / kr-iShNa sA ra'i pags pa dang / mda' sag la sogs pa dang / gzhan yang bzhugs 'bol dang / kha gang ma dang / gral gdan sogs shin tu mang ba dang
/ cog rtse bzang 'bring sna tshogs pa dang / thab cha'i skor la khro rag zangs sogs kyi snod spyad mang po dang / ma hA tsi na'i yul gyi ljon ja 'khor drug drug cu tham
pa dang / mar rgya nyis brgya dang sum cu bcas gsar sbyor mdzad pa dang / chos rgyal chen po'i dbus dad pa can phal mo ches phebs brdzong gi rigs gya nom pa phul zhing
/ phar yang de rnams la chos dang zang zing gi sbyin gtong skabs su gang bab mdzad cing / sku'i dbon thugs kyi sras mchog dam pa zhabs drung rin po che 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po gdan tshab tu mnga' gsol te/ dgung lo re gnyis pa gser 'phyang gi lo'i snron gyi zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi gral tshes bzang por chibs skyel
gyi tshogs rgya che ba dang bcas te dpal ldan lhun grub steng gi rgyal khab nas chibs kyi gdong bsgyur/ sde dge chos rgyal chen po byams pa kun dga' sangs rgyas bstan pa'i
rgyal mtshan pa'ang sga len steng bar chibs skyel du byon/ der thog mtha' bar gsum dge ba'i smon lam dang bka' bsgo sogs rgyas par stsal/ chos rgyal chen po mchog nas
kyang rdo ra dmar ko bar gyi chibs skyel du ldan dpon tshe 'phel 'khor dang bcas pa dang / e wa~M chos ldan gyi gdan sa rang du ma phebs bar gyi zhabs 'bring bar phu ma'i
'dun 'khor tshe ring 'phel dpon g.yog rnams gtong gnang mdzad pa bzhin rim gyis chibs bteg /mdzod pa nor ldan shes rab bzang pos lo snga ma rnams su sde dge dang gling tshang
rgyal khab gnyis dmag 'khrugs gzhi che tsam byung bar bar 'dum byas par legs 'grig byung rung / phran bu'i mtha' bsdu rgyu

lus pa rnams mthar phyin pa'i slad du rjes su zla gcig tsam bzhugs/ rje 'dis zul phu stod smad/ mkhar mdo/ khra thang / shang tho dgon/ gdong tshang dgon rnams su dad pa can
so sos ji ltar gsol ba btab pa bzhin chos kyi bdud rtsi'ang ci rigs par stsal/ de nas we re rdo sges kyi chu tshan du chab bzhes mdzad cing zhag kha shas bzhugs skabs mdzod
pa 'khor bcas kyang 'byor/ de nas chibs bteg ste rdo ra dmar kor byon/ der zhag kha shas bzhugs te sga stod phyogs kyi dgon khag rnams dang / dad pa can dag gis phebs
brdzong sogs rim par bstabs shing / de thams cad la'ang chos dang zang zing gi sbyin pas tshim par mdzad nas hor zla bdun pa'i tshes mgor rdo ra dmar ko nas chibs kyi gdong
bsgyur/ ri klung gi rgyud du ma dang / gnam gyi dum bu sa la lhung ba lta bu'i thang chen po mang po brgal te rim gyis byang rwa sgreng gi chos grwa chen por phebs/
der bzhugs pa'i rten gsum yongs la mchod 'bul dang / de skabs rwa sgreng khri chen rin po che ngag dbang ye shes tshul khrims rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po 'bras spungs su sku
yon gsan sbyong mdzad par phebs nas bzhugs mi snang yang / rwa sgreng bla brang gi 'bul skal du maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ ja 'khor drug bdun/ rta drel gsum/ mdzo g.yag
bzhi/ gzhan yang tshan grangs kha shas dang / tA bla mar yang ja gsar gang 'os dang / dgon par mang ja'i bsnyen bkur bcas rgyas par mdzad nas stag lung du phebs/ der
yang stag lung bla ma rin po cher maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ ljon ja 'khor drug gsum/ rta drel gnyis/ mdzo g.yag gnyis/ tshan grangs kha shas bcas dang / dgon de'i rten
gsum rnams la brgya mchod rnam lnga dang / 'dus tshogs su mang ja'i bsnyen

bkur bcas bsgrubs shing / de nas dar lung gnyan gyi pho brang dang / brag yer pa rnams su'ang mchod 'bul dang thugs smon zhib par mdzad nas hor zla bcu pa'i nang lha ldan du
phebs/ de skabs rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen pa tshul khrims rgya mtsho zhing khams gzhan du gzigs pa'i ngang tshul bstan par gyur na'ang / de'i sku gdung rin po che'i
mdun du maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ bzang ja 'khor drug brgya tham pa/ rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu tham pa/ bod dngul Tam srang lnga bcu tham pa/ rta drel bcu bzhi/
mdzo g.yag nyi shu/ gzhan yang mchod cha dang thab cha'i skor dang / tshan grangs kyi rigs shin tu mang ba dang / rgyal tshab chen po tshe smon gling par yang / maNDal sku
gsung thugs rten/ gsol ja bzhes 'bras kyi dod dang / bzang ja 'khor drug lnga bcu dang / bod dngul Tam srang lnga bcu tham pa/ rta drel bdun dang / mdzo g.yag bcu dang
/ tshan grangs kyi rigs rab tu mang po dang bcas 'bul lam zhus par/ phyir yang 'bul slog rgya che ba dang / lam yig dang / dos rta rtswa shing sogs phon che ba dang / ja
khral rtsa chag sogs gzigs skyong zla med par stsal ba dang / kun bde gling dang / bstan rgyas gling / tshe chog gling rnams su so sor ja 'khor lnga re dang / rta drel gnyis
kyi gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas re dang / rwa sgreng khri chen rin po che 'bras spungs su bzhugs par zhal mjal zhu ba dang chabs cig maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/
ljon ja 'khor gsum bcas dang / gzhan yang bka' shag dang / spyi khyab mkhan po dang / rtse shod kyi gsol gzim mgron gnyer rnams dang / lha sa bla brang gi phyag mdzod pa
dang / gnyer tshang pa dang / rtse'i phyag mdzod pa dang / gnyer tshang pa dang / mi dpon dang / rtswa gnyer dang / shing

gnyer sogs su'ang go babs dang 'dris zab dang bstun pa'i ja gsar gyi sa bcad re dang / khyad par srid zhi'i mchod sdong zla med pa jo shAka rnam gnyis kyi mdun du stong mchod
rgyas pa dang / gzhan yang rten gsum yongs la gser gsol dang mchod 'bul la sogs pa dang / rtse rnam rgyal grwa tshang / gling khag bzhi'i gra tshang / 'bras spungs 'dus
spyi/ de'i nang gses gling khang tshan/ ser 'dus spyi/ de'i nang gses tre bo khang tshan/ dga' ldan/ rgyud stod smad/ rme ru/ bzhi sde rnams su mang ja'i bsnyen bkur dang
/ smon lam chen mo'i skabs kyi 'dus tshogs su mang ja gnyis kyi bsnyen bkur zhu ba'i dod du bzang ja 'khor drug bdun cu tham pa lha sa bla brang gi phyag mdzod par phul
ba sogs byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i rnam par thar pa la co 'dri ba bzhin mdzad nas lha ldan nas chibs bteg /yar lam lcags zam chu bo ri'i dgon par mang 'gyed
dang / lcags zam bla ma rin po cher ljon ja 'khor gcig gi gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas dang bcas pa'i 'bul ba dang / rong du byams chen bzhugs pa'i dgon par mang 'gyed
kyi bsnyen bkur dang / gtan gzhag sogs stsol bzhin pa'i sgo nas rim gyis gzhis rtser phebs/ bkras lhun du paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa rje btsun blo bzang dpal ldan bstan
pa'i nyi ma'i gser zhal rin po che mjal ba dang chabs cig maNDal sku gsung thugs rten/ gsol ja bzhes 'bras kyi dod dang / rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu tham pa/ bzang
ja 'khor drug bzhi bcu/ rta drel bdun/ mchod cha dang / thab cha'i skor sna tshogs/ dar/ ras/ ling / spu shun la sogs pa'i tshan grangs shin tu mang ba phul ba dang /
zhabs pad mdun du'ang / ljon ja 'khor drug bdun dang / rta gcig bcas dang / gzhan yang rtse'i

gsol gzim mgron gnyer phyag mdzod sogs la'ang 'dris zab che chung dang bstun pa'i ja sar skabs su gang bab re dang / khyad par dgon de'i rten gsum yongs la mchod 'bul dang
/ 'dus tshogs spyir mang ja'i bsnyen bkur dang / de'i nang gses rgya khang tshan par mang ja ja gsar sogs skabs su ji ltar bab pa rnams legs par mdzad nas hor zla bcu gcig
pa'i dkar phyogs kyi gral tshes bcu gsum gyi nyin spyi dang bye brag gi chibs bsu dang / thab bsu dang / khyad par dgon pa'i ser sbreng gi tshogs dang bcas te yon tan rin
po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal e wa~M chos ldan du nyer 'tshe'i dri mas ma gos par bde bar phebs par gyur to/ /de nas kyang rim gyis gza' skar legs 'dzom gyi nyin e wa~M
bla brang gzhung du rje 'di'i sku mched mdo sngags bstan pa'i mnga' bdag mkhan rin po che khri thog pa rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po'i drung du/ maNDal sku gsung thugs
rten/ dar/ ras/ ling / spu shun la sogs pa dang / mchod cha dang / thab cha'i rigs sna tshogs pa dang / rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu tham pa dang / ljon ja 'khor drug
lnga bcu/ rta drel lnga bcas 'bul bar mdzad pa dang / phan bde khang gsar du mkhas grub rgya mtsho'i gtsug rgyan mkhan rin po che byams pa dpal ldan bzang po pa dang /
zhabs drung rin po che kun dga' bstan pa'i blo gros pa gnyis lhan rgyas pa'i mdun dang / bla brang phun tshogs khang gsar du zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang blo gros bstan
'dzin pa dang / klu ldings bla brang du zhabs drung rin po che dpal ldan phun tshogs pa ste so so'i mdun du'ang / sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang / dar/ ras/ ling / spu
shun gyi rigs dang / mchod cha dang / thab cha'i skor sna tshogs pa dang / rgya dngul 'degs srang nyer lnga re dang /

ljon ja 'khor drug nyi shu re/ rta drel gsum re bcas phul ba dang / thar rtse rang du'ang rnam dkar mchod thebs kyi rten du 'bul ba shin tu stobs che ba dang / mkhas dang grub
pa'i dbang phyug mkhan rin po che dpal ldan chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa dang / khang ser dpon slob rin po che bcas su'ang 'bul ba gang zab dang / dgon pa'i chos khrims dang
/ bla khag so so'i phyag gnyer sogs las tshan gyi rigs dang / thar rtser rang gi las tshan grwa tshang sogs dang / ngor chos kyi mi ser sogs la'ang ja gsar dang gnang
sbyin skabs su gang bab stsal nas/ zla ba de'i mjug tu lung rtogs chos tshul rgya mtsho'i 'byung gnas dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen por phebs/ rigs dang dkyil 'khor
rgya mtsho'i khyab bdag khri chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po'i mdun du sa skya gzhung gi 'bul bar/ maNDal sku gsung
thugs rten/ ljon ja 'khor drug brgya tham pa/ rgya dngul 'degs srang lnga bcu dang / bod dngul Tam srang lnga bcu tham pa/ rta drel bdun/ gzhan yang mchod cha dang / thab
cha'i rigs dang / dar/ ras/ ling / gos chen/ spu shun la sogs pa'i tshan grangs rab tu mang po dang / khri chen rin po che sku sger gyi 'bul bar ljon ja 'khor drug bdun
dang / chibs pa gcig gi gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas dang / sngags 'chang grub pa'i dbang po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen pa dang / bstan dang 'gro ba'i dpal mgon mgon
po dngos grub dpal 'bar ba dang / mdo sngags bstan pa'i snang byed 'jam mgon kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa dang / gdung sras rin po che 'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen pa dang
/ ngag dbang bkra shis rin chen pa bcas kyi sku sger so sor yang / ljon ja 'khor drug lnga re dang rta re'i gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha

shas re dang / rje btsun ma khag so sor yang ljon ja 'khor drug gnyis re'i gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas re dang / lha khang mkhan rin po che'i mdun du'ang / ljon ja 'khor
drug gsum gyi gtsos pa'i tshan grangs kha shas dang / sa skya zhabs pad pa'i mdun du gzhung gi 'bul bar/ ljon ja 'khor drug gcig dang / rta gcig gi gtsos pa'i tshan grangs
kha shas dang / gzhan yang zhabs pad sku sger dang / gsol gzim mgron gnyer drung yig la sogs pa'i las tshan thams cad la'ang 'dris zab che chung dang bstun pa'i ja gsar
gang 'tsham re dang / khyad par phyogs de'i rten gsum byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba rnams su gser gsol dang / mchod 'bul shin tu rgyas pa dang / sprul pa'i lha khang
chen mor dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya mtshor mang ja gnyis kyi steng phyag 'gyed dge 'dun bco lnga rer bzang ja sbag re phul ba sogs gtong ba chen po'i sgo 'phar yangs por phyes
te hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i nang ngor du phebs/ khang tshan bcu gcig po thams cad la'ang ja gsar dang / khyad par rang rang gi skong brgya tshogs pa'i skabs 'phar ja'i bsnyen
bkur dang 'brel bar/ thob khungs dang khang tshan che chung gi babs dang bstun pa'i gtan gzhag gsar sbyor rigs zab par stsal ba dang / dgung grangs re gsum du phebs
pa sa khyi hor zla dang po'i tshes gcig nas bzung ste e waM ba'i lha khang khag thams cad la mchod 'bul shin tu rgya che ba dang / khyad par e wa~M chos ldan gyi gtsug lag
khang chen por dge 'dun drug brgya tsam tshogs pa thams cad zla ba gcig bar ma chad par bsnyen bkur bar mdzad de/ de'ang nyin re bzhin brgya mchod dang 'brel bar bla ma
mchod pa dang / ngan song sbyong rgyud nas bstan pa'i kun rig rtsa ba'i lha sum cu rtsa bdun mgron thabs kyi lha dang bcas pa/

grub chen dze tA ris bkral ba'i tshe dpag med lha dgu'i sgrub mchod rnams legs par btsugs te/ nyin re bzhin dge slong bcu re la phyag 'gyed bzang ja sbag re byas pa dang /
yang dge slong bco lnga re la bzang ja sbag re byas pa spel ma'i tshul gyi nyin bco lnga dang / yang nyin re bzhin grwa pa re la dngul Tam phyed re dang / dngul zho re dang
/ dngul Tam re byas pa res mos kyi nyin bco lnga ste mdor na zla ba gcig gi bar la bsnyen bkur ba dang chabs cig /gtsug lag khang du gos chen bzang bsgrigs kyi phye phur
cha gcig dang / rgya mthongs khor yug tu gos chen bzang bsgrigs kyi phur ma rnams gsar sbyor mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sder mang jas bsnyen
bkur ba dang / de'i nang gses gur pa grwa tshang par mang ja 'gyed dang bcas pa'i steng 'khar rnga la sogs pa'i gtan gzhag 'ga' zhig kyang stsal ba dang / zhwa lu dang /
snar thang dang / srad rgyud pa dang / srad dgon khra sogs nye skor gyi dgon pa phal che bar mang ja gral 'gyed dang bcas pas bsnyen bkur ba sogs mdor na byang chub sems
dpa' kun tu bzang po'i rnam par thar pa dang rjes su mthun par mdzad pa yin no/ /hor zla dang po'i mjug tu e wa~M pa'i dus chos lam 'bras grub mtshams zhig nas/ mkhan rin
po che khri thog pa rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po mgul cham lta bus cung zad sku khams bsnyen tshul bzhes par brten/ lo der phyogs mtha' dag nas 'dus pa'i don gnyer nyis
brgya lhag tsam la rje 'dis mkhan po mdzad de rab tu byung ba dang / bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i sdom pa legs par stsal te thams cad kyang dge slong 'dul ba 'dzin pa sha stag
tu bsgrub par mdzad pa yin no/ /de rjes hor zla gsum pa dang / bzhi pa rnams su phan khang zhabs drung rin po che kun dga' bstan pa'i blo gros

sogs zhal slob nyung shas zhig la kye rdor bka' babs bzhi'i dbang dang / bde mchog lU nag gi dbang la sogs pa bka' chos 'ga' zhig stsal/ hor zla lnga pa'i nang sa skya nas
'jam mgon khri chen rin po ches sa skyar phebs dgos tshul gyi bka' nan stsal bar brten/ hor zla drug pa'i nang sa skyar phebs/ khri chen rin po cher sku'i rkyen sel gyi dbang
rjes 'ga' zhig dang / khyad par gdung sras rin po che 'jam mgon ngag dbang bkra shis rin chen par/ grub chen a bha yA ka ra guptas bkral ba'i rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang
'bring po'i lugs kyi dkyil 'khor zhe gnyis dang / de'i steng du darpaN A tsarYas kri ya sa mutstsha las phyung ba'i dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum bsnan te bzhi
bcu zhe lnga'i dbang bskur ba rnams phyag len rnam par dag pas stsal te kha'u'i chu tshan du phebs/ der zhag kha shas bzhugs nas hor zla brgyad pa'i mjug tu e wa~M du phebs/
don du gnyer ba 'ga' zhig la zab lam nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i khrid la sogs pa stsal/ lo de'i mjug tu sa skya nas 'jam mgon khri chen rin po che dang / de sras smra ba'i
nyi ma ngag dbang bkra shis rin chen gnyis rgyal rtser chibs bskyod bskyangs pa'i mar lam ngor du phebs/ bla khag rnams kyis kyang rang rang gi 'byor pa dang bstun pa'i
'bul ba dang bsnyen bkur zab par bstabs/ rje 'di sku mched rnams nas kyang 'bul bsnyen shin tu rgya che bar mdzad/ rje 'di las dbang dang rjes gnang 'ga' zhig kyang gsan/
slar chibs skyel gyi tshogs dang bcas te e wa~M nas chibs bteg /rje 'di dgung grangs re bzhir son pa sa mo phag gi lor rje nyid kyi gsung gis bskul ba bzhin mdo khams
sde dge nas 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'ang zhabs

kyi padmor son pa nas bzung / dgung grangs re bdun pa chu pho stag gi lo'i bar gtso bor thugs dam kho na la bzhugs pa dang / gong du bshad pa'i rten bzhengs phal cher zhig
la gzungs gzhug sogs 'bul ba dang / kun gzigs 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub pa rnams kyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor
rje rang gis gsan pa'i dbang dang rjes gnang zur bka'i rigs phal che ba dang / bla ma gong ma'i bka' 'bum gyi lung rnams stsal ba dang / de'i nang tshan srung ba lha lnga
bcu rtsa gcig dang / gdugs dkar nyer bdun ma dang / gsang ba 'dus pa rigs gsum dang / bde mchog lU nag gnyis la sogs pa'i dbang dang rjes gnang zur bka' 'ga' zhig dang
/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang / snar thang brgya rtsa'i rjes su gnang ba dang / mus chen sems dpa' chen po dang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge'i bka' 'bum gyi lung rnams
ni don du gnyer ba so so'i ngor lan gnyis gsum re stsal ba dang / yang dze tA ris bkral ba'i mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu dang / tshe dpag med lha dgu dang / ngan song sbyong rgyud
nas bshad pa'i kun rig dang / phyag rdor 'chi 'joms dang / 'jigs byed rwa lugs lha dgu la sogs pa nye bar mkho ba'i dbang 'ga' zhig dang / dmar po skor gsum dang / nor
lha dang / chos srung gi skor sogs rjes gnang zur bka' 'ga' zhig dang / nye bar mkho ba'i lung 'ga' zhig dang bcas pa rnams ni lan grangs mang por stsal ba dang / khyad
par sa skya nas 'jam mgon khri chen rin po che yab sras gnyis kyis bka' nan gang che stsal bar brten/ lo re bzhin sa skyar lan gnyis gsum re chag med du phebs te/ gdung
sras rin po che 'jam mgon smra ba'i nyi ma ngag dbang

bkra shis rin chen theg mchog bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan par/ 'phags yul gyi grub chen birWa pa'i thugs bcud thun mong ma yin pa gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras slob bshad du
grags pa'i smin grol cha lag dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs pa tshar gcig gis gtsor byas pa'i rje rang gis gsan pa'i dbang lung phal che ba stsal ba dang / yab sras gnyis char
gyi sku'i rkyen sel dgos rigs rnams dang / yab rje khri chen rin po ches rgyun du nyams su bzhes pa'i thugs dam gyi lha rnams kyi dbang rjes rnams yang yang 'bul dgos
pa dang / sgrol ma lha khang gsar bzhengs la rab tu gnas pa sogs ji ltar bzhed pa'i don mtha' dag sgrub par mdzad pa dang / bka' chos stsal ba'i skabs rnams su'ang khri
chen rin po che sogs kyi thugs rgyud la snga na med pa'i nyams bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'khrungs pa dang / gzhan yang rgyal yum nyi zla dbang mor gdung sras ma byung bar brten/
rje 'di la gdung sras myur 'byon gyi skyabs 'jug zhus pa ltar/ srung ba lha lnga bcu rtsa gcig gi dbang dang sor 'brang ma'i 'khor lo bcas stsal te/ ji ltar lung bstan
pa bzhin du yun ha cang mi ring bar gdung sras kun dga' bsod nams ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dang bcas te 'khrungs pa dang / rgyun du bdag chen yab sras rnams kyis thugs brtag
zhus pa rnams kyang ji ltar lung bstan pa de kho na ltar las 'pho 'gyur lan gcig kyang mi 'byung ba sogs dam pa rnams kyi ye shes gzigs

pa'i snang ngo na sangs rgyas dngos dang khyad par med cing / sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mtha' dag kyang mdzad pa'i phyir/ nges par rdo rje 'chang yin pa la the tshom cung zad
kyang mi mnga' ba'i thugs dad mtha' yas pa mdzad cing / rgyun du mtshan nas gsungs pa'i tshe'ang thar rtse rdo rje 'chang zhes gus pa chen pos gsungs pa yin no/ /de skabs
shig tu zhwa ser can gyi bstan pa'i snang byed dam pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i mkhas pa chen po sog po don grub rgyal mtshan pa'ang e wa~M du byon te/ rje 'di las bka' chos
'ga' zhig gsan par mdzad de/ chu stag lo'i nang zhwa lu nas rtsod dus kyi kun mkhyen bu ston gnyis pa rdo rje 'chang rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong dpal bzang po'ang e
wa~M du phebs/ rje 'di las kye rdor bka' babs bzhi la sogs pa'i bka' chos 'ga' zhig gsan/ tshul yang gong du thos pa mdzad pa'i skabs su bshad pa ltar gyi rnam sras kyi rjes
gnang sogs gsan pa dang / yang zhwa ser gyi cod pan 'dzin pa rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu lta bur gyur pa bcu phrag rig pa'i ma hA paNDi ta a mdo bkra shis 'khyil gyi brag
dgon zhabs drung rin po che dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas pa'ang e wa~M du phebs/ rje 'di las dbang dang / rjes gnang dang / lung la sogs pa'i bka' chos 'ga' zhig gsan
cing / tshur yang gong du bshad pa ltar gyi bka' chos mang du gsan par mdzad pa sogs zab rgyas

kyi chos 'khor rgya cher bskor ba dang / slar yang phyi lo chu mo yos kyi gnam lo gsar du 'char ba'i dpyid kyi dus su'ang dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi bla brang thar pa rtser
rtsod pa'i dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen rtse'i dbang po dang / gnas lnga rigs pa'i mkhas pa chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub pa bcas
kyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras slob bshad du grags pa'i smin grol cha lag dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs pa lan cig stsal bar mdzad do/ /snga
lo sde dge chos rgyal chen po byams pa kun dga' sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan pa zhi bar gshegs pa'i dgongs rdzogs bsgrub pa dang / mkhan rin po che rnal 'byor 'jam
dpal bzang po mdo khams su gdan drang pa'i slad du sde dge'i sku tshab dpon 'khor rnams 'byor bar brten/ rje 'di dgung grangs re brgyad pa chu yos hor zla lnga pa'i tshes
gsum nyin mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po dang / kun gzigs 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po ston 'khor rnams mdo khams su chibs bteg /lo
de'i mjug tu sa skya nas 'jam mgon khri chen rin po ches bka' nan stsal bar brten rje 'di sa skyar phebs/ 'jam mgon khri chen rin po che yab sras rnams su bka' chos rnams
thugs bzhed bzhin phul te e wa~M du phebs/ de phyin chad sa skyar phebs dgos tshul gyi bka' nan yang yang stsal rung / sku na mtho ba'i stabs kyis dgongs khrol nan cher
zhu bar mdzad de phyogs gang du'ang ma phebs par e wa~M rang du gtso bor thugs dam kho na bzhugs shing / bka'

chos stsal ba'i rim pa'ang / dgung grangs re dgu pa shing 'brug lor 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub pas gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ grub chen a bha yas bkral ba'i rdo rje
phreng ba dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum dang bcas pa rnams kyi dbang bskur ba dang / grub chen brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i byin rlabs dang / blo sbyong don bdun ma'i
khrid dang / blo sbyong zhen pa bzhi bral gyi khrid dang / ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum gyi lung dang bcas pa rnams dang / gzhan yang dbang dang rjes gnang
zur bka' 'ga' zhig dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes su gnang ba rnams stsal/ dgung grangs bdun cu pa shing sbrul lor don du gnyer ba 'ga' zhig gi ngor/ kye rdo rje
bka' babs bzhi'i dbang dang / lam 'bras pod dmar ser gyi lung dang / blo sbyong glegs bam gyi lung la sogs pa stsal/ 'di lo mdo khams nas rje 'di'i dbon zhabs drung rin
po che 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan pa'ang e wa~M du phebs/ dbus gtsang thams cad du bsnyen bkur dang 'bul ba sogs gya nom pa mdzad/ dgung grangs don gcig pa me rta
lor/ bstan pa'i snang byed dam pa zhabs drung rin po che 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan pa'i dbus bdag cag rnams kyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ gsung ngag rin po che
lam 'bras slob bshad kyi smin grol cha lag dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs pa bka' drin chen pos stsal/ dgung grangs don gnyis pa me lug lo dang / don gsum pa sa sprel lo gnyis
su dbang dang rjes gnang zur bka' re zung las bka' chos che rigs ma stsal/ sa sprel lo mdo khams

nas mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po bcas kyang ris su med pa'i dgon khag so sor 'bul ba dang bsnyen
bkur gya nom pa mdzad bzhin pa'i sgo nas e wa~M du phebs/ dgung grangs don bzhi pa sa bya lor/ bdag cag rnams kyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i smin grol
yongs su rdzogs pa dang / dpal ldan don grub pa'i bka' 'bum gyi lung la sogs pa'i bka' chos 'ga' zhig stsal/ 'di lo zhabs drung dbon rin po che 'jam dbyangs nam mkha'
rgyal mtshan pa'ang mdo khams su phebs/ dgung grangs don lnga pa lcags khyi lor kun gzigs 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang pos gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ gshed dmar lha
lnga'i smin byed kyi dbang dang / grol byed spros med kyi khrid dang bcas pa dang / gzhan yang 'jigs byed lha bcu gsum ma'i dbang dang / rjes gnang zur bka' 'ga' zhig stsal/
dgung grangs don drug pa lcags phag lor lo snga ma'i nang nas mgul blo lta bus bsnyun yun cung zad ring zhing sku mdangs zhan par thar rtse rang nas kyang zhabs brtan
dang gsol sman gyi 'phrod bzhes sogs nar mar phul cing / lhag par kun gzigs bla ma 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang pos yon sbyar te/ mkhas btsun grub pa'i gtsug rgyan
rdo rje 'dzin pa ngag dbang legs grub dpon slob rnams kyis sgrol dkar 'od zer drug sbrag gi sgrub mchod gnad smin mtha' rten dU rba'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa mdzad de/
kun gzigs bla mas zhabs brtan 'bul mtshon dang lhan cig tshe rdzas phul skabs rje bla ma nyid kyang

dgyes nyams che zhing / mdangs rmi lam du rang re'i bla brang gi shar gyi rtsig rmangs 'di zhig la khad du snang ba sems mi bde ba'i nyams kyis gnyer pa mkhyen rab la 'di bcos
dgos tshul mol bas de ma thag las mi kha shas dang bcas rtsig pa sra brling zhig 'phral du grub song ba da ste lo shas brtan par 'dug snyam yid bde bar byung ba la dpags
na/ da res nad 'dis skyon mi 'dug cing / da dung lo shas 'tsho ba 'dra zhes bka' stsal ba ltar/ de 'phral sku khams rim gyis dwang ste sku'i gzi byin sngar bzhin rgyas
pa dang / bstan 'gro'i dpal du zhabs pad yun ring por 'tsho zhing gzhes pa'i dge mtshan mngon du gyur/ de skabs sde dge rgyal sras bla ma rin po che dbus gtsang gi phyogs
su bsnyen bkur stob bzhin pa'i sgo nas e wa~M du phebs/ des gsol ba btab pa ltar rje nyid kyis mkhan po dang / mkhan chen bla ma rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang pos las kyi
slob dpon mdzad de bdag cag la sogs pa dad pa'i dge 'dun grangs tshang ba'i dbus su rab tu byung zhing bsnyen par rdzogs pa dang / gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras slob bshad
kyi smin grol cha lag yongs su rdzogs pa lan cig dang / dbang dang rjes gnang zur bka'i rigs kyang kha shas stsal/ de lo 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'ang
sde dge dang lhan cig tu mdo khams su byon/ de nas bzung ste dgung grangs gya gnyis pa me sbrul lo'i bar gtso bor thugs dam kho na la gzhol bar mdzad cing / snga phyir
bdag gis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ rigs gsum spyi dang / 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal lha so bdun dang / gdugs dkar lha nyer bdun ma dang / srung ba lha lnga bcu rtsa gcig dang
/ 'jam

pa'i dbyangs a ra pa tsa lha lnga dang / phyag rdor 'chi 'joms dang / 'jigs byed rwa lugs lha dgu dang / gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje dang / bde mchog nag po pa dang
/ kye rdo rje bka' babs bzhi rnams kyi dbang bskur ba dang / rjes gnang zur bka' 'ga' zhig dang / klu sgrub rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i lam 'bras slob bshad pod dang / ngag dbang
brtan rdor gyis mdzad pa'i lam 'bras tshogs bshad dang / mus chen bka' 'bum rnams kyi lung dang / khro bcu'i rjes gnang sngon du 'gro ba'i rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i phyi
khrid dang / mgon pod me 'bar ma dang / kha skong dang / snyan brgyud dang / yang skong dang / dud sol ma'i dpe bum rnams kyi lung rnams bka' drin chen po'i sgo nas stsal
ba dang / gzhan yang de skabs rnams su sku rten gsar bzhengs dang / thar rtse rang gi lha khang khag rnams la snga phyir rab tu gnas pa lan bzhi tsam mdzad pa dang /
nor bum dang / klu bum dang / sa bdag snying gter rnams kyi bum pa mang po tshul bzhin du bsgrubs par mdzad de/ yul phyogs so sor sba ba sogs bstan pa dang sems can gyi don
kho na las nam yang g.yel ba mi mnga' ba yin no/ /mgon khyod bsod nams spel ba'i slad/ /gtong ba'i sgo brgya dbye 'dis ci/ /gdod nas sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin/ /yongs su
rdzogs par byas min nam/ /'on te sems dpa' che rnams kyis/ /spyod tshul gzhan la slob pa'i phyir/ /snying po med pa'i nor rnams kyang / /snying po dam pa'i dpal la sbyar/
/rang nyid srid zhi thams cad kyi/ /mchod sdong mtshungs pa med brnyes kyang / /da dung rgyal ba'i bstan pa la/ /gus pa'i srid zhu ci yang mdzad/ /gdul bya'i blo gros
dang 'tsham par/ /chos kyi 'khor lo rab

bskor bas/ /ma dag pa yi 'jig rten kyang / /dag pa'i zhing khams bzhin du byas/ /'di na chos kyi bdud rtsi'i rgyun/ /'bebs par byed pa mang mod kyang / /khams dang bsam pa
bag nyal la/ /brtags te ston pa khyod 'dra su/ /de slad shes bya kun gzigs pa'i/ /nyi ma'i gnyen de 'di min nam/ /gzhan du thams cad mkhyen pa yi/ /chos smra 'di 'dra ji
ltar 'byung / /rang don byang chub brnyes bzhin du/ /zab mo'i lam la brtson pa sogs/ /'gro 'di thar par bkri ba'i slad/ /rgyal sras spyod tshul bsam mi khyab/ /nyes spyod
phra zhing phra ba yang / /gzod ma nyid nas spangs zin phyir/ /de slad khyod kyi phrin las kyis/ /rtag tu phun tshogs 'ba' zhig ster// //gnyis pa byang phyogs bod kyi rgyal
po gzhung sa dga' ldan pho brang pa chen pos chen por 'os pa'i mtshan dang yo byad kyis chen po'i go sar mnga' gsol nas rnam dkar gyi phrin las ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul
ni/ sngon bod chos rgyal mes dbon rnams kyi sku dus nas bzung ste/ deng sang gi bar du brang ti'i gdung rabs rim byon thams cad kyis spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la
bya ba chen po byas shing / 'gro ba mang po phan pa dang bde ba'i lam la bkod pa dang / khyad par gzhung sa dga' ldan pho brang pa chen por yang rnam kun lhag bsam lhur len
gyis sri zhu gang che zhus dang zhu mu yin par ma zad/ snga ma shing yos lo dang / me 'brug lo gnyis su yid srubs kyis rgyud bskul ba'i pha rol gorSha nas bod chos ldan
gyi zhing khams su tshur rgol byung bar brten/ dmag 'khrugs gzhi che tsam byung ba'i skabs su'ang / rje 'di'i sku mched mdzod pa nor ldan shes rab bzang po gzhi rtse'i
rta khal mgo byed du bsko bzhag stsal bar yang dpon

'bangs spyi sger tshang mar phan thogs shin tu che bar byung ba dang / lhag par de skabs bod ljongs su 'khod pa'i 'byor ldan yod rigs la gzhungs nas dmag phogs kyi yod 'don
'gel bar mdzad gshis/ thar rtser yang bod dngul Tam srang phyed sum brgya skor dang / nas khal sum stong skor dang / ja mar sogs shin tu phon che ba 'bul dgos bka' phebs
byung ba rnams kyang gtsang 'bul zhus par brten/ de rnams kyi gzigs bzos bdag rkyen du thar rtser rang gi bla rabs rim can la sha 'dzin ni thig thi gu chi mkhan po zhes
pa'i cho lo dang / tham ka che ba gru bzhi dang / chung ba rgyun tham sgor mo dang / rta dar/ na bza'i skor dang / chibs par tog dang / ze khebs dang long khebs la sogs pa
mdor na mkhan chas cha tshang ba stsal ba dang / thar rtse rang gi bla ma sgar pa dang / tshong pa sogs stod smad lho byang gang du song yang ja khral dang la khral dang
thab khral gyis mtshon pa'i khral rigs che phra mtha' dag sprod mi dgos pa dang / bla gzhis rgya mtsho gling pa thar rtse rang la gtsang chod yin pa sogs kyi shel sbam
bcas legs par stsal bar mdzad mod/ 'on kyang bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa yon tan rin po che'i phung por gyur pa 'di dag bskal pa dpag tu med pa'i sngon rol nas srid
dang zhi ba'i mtha' la mi gnas pa'i khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po'i rgyal srid chen po bdag gir mdzad zin na'ang / skabs su bab pa'i gdul bya rnams kyi blo'i rim pa dang
bstun te mchog dman bar gsum gyi sprul pa sna tshogs pa'i sgo nas sems can gyi don mdzad par gor ma chag la/ rgyu mtshan de'i phyir na tshe 'di snang gi rnyed pa dang /
bkur sti

dang / go sa dang / thob thang sogs la ltos dgos pa min rung / re zhig 'jig rten tshu rol mthong ba rnams kyi snang tshul dang bstun te/ rje 'di dgung grangs brgyad cu gya
gnyis pa dang / mkhan rin po che rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po dgung grangs drug cu re dgur son pa dmar ser can zhes pa me mo sbrul gyi lo'i sa ga zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi
gral tshes lnga'i nyin/ ji ltar 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po la rgyal srid rin po che rnam pa bdun gyis yongs su mnga' gsol ba ltar/ sku tshe brtan bzhugs kyi cho ga dang
'brel bar bshad ma thag pa'i mtshan dang / yo byad rnams dang / gzhan yang legs 'bul gyi tshogs dang bcas pa'i sgo nas bod gangs can gyi mkhan po che gras su yongs su
mnga' gsol bar gyur to/ de nas bzung ste dgung grangs gya drug tu phebs pa lcags bya lo'i bar gtso bor thugs dam kho na la gzhol bar mdzad/ skabs skabs su bde kye gsang
gsum gyi sgrub mchod rnams kyang zhag kha shas re gsung bar mdzad pa dang / sa skya nas gdung sras rin po che 'jam mgon phyogs kyi glang po'ang snga phyir lan gnyis tsam
phebs nas rje 'di las bka' chos 'ga' zhig gsan pa dang / bdag cag don gnyer rnams kyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor jo bo lugs kyi sgrol ma nyer gcig dang / dpyal lugs phag mo
skor gsum gyi byin rlabs sogs dang / nye bar mkho ba'i lung 'ga' zhig dang bcas pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi'ang ci rigs par stsol bar mdzad cing / mdor na sku na de tsam du son
kyang / sku gzugs kyi babs ha cang lci ba dang / thugs rab mi gsal ba sogs mi mnga' zhing / thugs dam sogs la lhod pa med pa ni

shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i gnas yin no/ /de ltar sku tshe rangs por dam pa'i chos 'chad pa dang / rtsod pa ni gdul bya rnams kyis ma rtogs pa dang / log par rtog pa'i the tshom
gyi drwa ba sel ba'i slad du 'di rnams ni 'thad la/ 'di dag ni mi 'thad pa'o/ /zhes rgyu mtshan dang bcas pas bka' stsal ba rnams yin la/ gsung rtsom ni gsang 'dus mi bskyod
pa'i cho ga nag 'gros ma dang / sde dge'i gzhi bdag 'bri gnyan gdong gi bsang mchod dang / khams phyogs kyi dgon sde 'ga' zhig gi bca' yig dang / zhal gdams dang /
gsol 'debs kyi skor re zung las rgya che rigs ma mdzad do/ /gzhan yang lo re bzhin cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes gcig nas bco lnga'i bar nyin re bzhin spos/ mar me/ zhal zas
rnams brgya phrag re dang 'brel bar dge slong bco lnga skor gyis bla ma mchod pa dang / gnas brtan cho ga dang / sgrol ma maNDal bzhi pa'i cho ga sogs gsung ba dang / rgyun
du'ang nya stong tshes brgyad phal che bar brgya mchod re dang bcas te dge slong nyung shas res bla ma mchod pa sogs gsung ba dang / yang rje 'di sku mched rnams nas lo
re bzhin dge slong bco lnga skor gyis rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur rin po che gsung sgrogs tshar re ma chag par mdzad pa dang / dus dus su zhabs brtan rim gro'i rigs kyang shin
tu rgya che ba sgrub pa dang / sngar bsnyen bkur zhu ba ma byung ba'i dgon sde 'ga' zhig la'ang mang ja'i bsnyen bkur sogs stsal ba dang / bal yul gyi mchod rten dang /
lha ldan gyi jo shAka rnam gnyis bcas kyi mdun du'ang snga phyir mchod 'bul yang yang bskur bar mdzad pa dang / mkhan rin po che rnal 'byor 'jam dpal

bzang pos e waM pa'i mkhan sa zhal 'dzin gnang ba'i skabs/ thar rtse nas gtsug lag gi tshogs 'bol yongs su rdzogs pa gsar bzos dang / de'i steng gi grum rtse'i gral gdan rnams
gsar sbyor mdzad par yang rin chen gnyis pa rdo tshad mang du song ba dang / gtsug lag khang du gos chen bzang bsgrigs kyi rten khebs nyer lnga dang / bla gzhung g.yab
chen du mkhan slob zur bzhi dang bcas pa'i snam sbyar nang gos las grub pa sogs sbyor 'jags stsal ba dang / rje 'di sku mched gnyis kyi dgongs bzhed dang / de'i phrin las
kyi gdugs dkar gyen du 'degs pa mdzod pa nor ldan shes rab bzang po pas gtso byas te/ e wa~M pa'i bla khag thams cad thun mong gi sgo nas bla brang gzhung gi g.yab chen
gyi skor la nyams gsos dang / de rjes ngor chen gyi dgongs rdzogs su bzhengs pa'i bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad kyi gtso byas pa'i mchod rten rnams la nyams gso dang / thog
g.yab gsar du brje ba dang / de rjes lam 'bras lha khang dang / dngul gdung lha khang steng shod rnams la nyams gso rnams phul du phyin par mdzad cing / de'i tshe'ang
g.yab chen gyi nyams gso'i skabs thar rtser rang gi gzhung sger ltos pa dang bcas pa'i zhal 'debs byas rigs thams cad bsdoms pas bod dngul rdo tshad sum cu so gcig tsam
zin pa dang / mchod rten gyi nyams gso'i skabs rje 'dis bod dngul Tam srang brgya zhal 'debs su stsal ba dang / dus phyis bdag gis e wa~M pa'i mkhan sa'i las khur gzung skabs
kyang / e wa~M pa'i bla khag thams cad thun mong gis 'dus tshogs kyi tshogs khro gnyis gsar bzos dang / rnying pa gnyis la nyams gsos mdzad cing / thar rtse sger nas
tshogs khro gcig gsar

bzos kyis sbyor 'jags mdzad song bar 'gro dron thams can zhib tu brtsis pas tshogs khro gcig la bod dngul rdo tshad bco brgyad tsam zin song ba dang / de lta bu'i tshogs khro
sbyor 'jags mdzad pa'i nyin/ gtsug lag khang du dkon mchog gi rten gyi drung du brgya mchod rnam lnga dang / gos chen gyi bla bre khyad par du 'phags pa gcig gsar sbyor
stsal ba dang 'brel bar 'dus tshogs rin po cher bla ma mchod pa'i cho ga btsugs te bsnyen bkur gya nom pa dang / phyag 'gyed dge 'dun brgyad re la ljon ja zhabs bcu sbag
re dang / de'i steng du tshab ra'i dar 'gyed la sogs pa mdor na sems med rnams kyang dge ba la rjes su yi rang ba snyam byed pa mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang mdzod pa nor
ldan shes rab bzang pos bstan 'gror phan du re ba'i lhag bsam bzang pos ngal ba khyad du bsad de gzhungs chen por snga phyir snyan sbron yang yang phul te/ ngor bla brang
gzhung nas lo re bzhin tsher chen rtswa bogs gser mgur zho lnga dang / ja'u si sbag gcig chag med du sprod dgos pa rtsa chag tu song ba dang / yang bla brang gzhung nas
lha khang rgyab kyi rten bogs lo re skor ltar gyi Tam lnga bcu re dang / lo re rten ltar gyi Tam nyer lnga re spel ma'i tshul gyis ma chag par sprod dgos pa da phyin rtsa
chag tu song ba dang / yang bla khag lnga spyi 'thus nas/ gal te gser gling pa'i rgya shing rngod gsum dang / gwa khral dang / lam thog pa rdzong sogs khral 'khri yongs
bsdoms dngul Tam srang zhe lnga re'i rtsis tsam lo re bzhin ma chag par sprod dgos pa rtsa chag tu song ba dang / yang ngor pa'i chos gzhis srad chu bzang bar bar skabs zhig
nas bcu gnyis chag dod ces

ba'i khral lo bcu gnyis re'i mtshams nas Tam srang zhe lnga re sprod dgos byung 'dug pa rtsa chag tu song ba dang / yang srad chu bzang sar pa cha rkang bdun gyi khral 'khri
rgya shing rdod gsum sogs ma chad par sgrub mu la sum zur re de snga lo mang por chag pa dang / yang srad chu bzang pas gwa khral Tam srang nyer lnga re lo re bzhin chag
med du sprod dgos pa la/ da phyin lo re bzhin Tam srang gsum re las sprad mi dgos pa dang / yang e wa~M bla brang gzhung du sbra dud rkang gsum las med pa la/ bar skabs
zhig nas de'i steng spra dud rkang gnyis kyi khral 'khri byung 'dug pa'i nang nas/ sbra dud rkang gcig gi khral 'khri rtsa chag tu song ba dang / sbra dud rkang gcig gi
tshab tu thar rtser rang gi khang zhing 'dzal zer ba de bcug pa sogs e wa~M bla brang gzhung dang / de'i chos gzhis mi ser bcas la phan sleb shin tu che bar byung ba dang
/ khyad par tshe 'dir snang gi bya gzhag dang stobs 'byor tsam gyis sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la bya ba byed nus pa ma yin te/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa zhes pa'i ming gi
gdags gzhi ni dam pa'i chos bshad pa dang sgrub pa kho na yin la/ bshad sgrub med pa'i yul phyogs la dgon pa zhes ming du gdags kyang don la grong pa dang khyad par ci'ang
med pas snying yod rnams kyis sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa 'phel ba dang / rang nyid kyang 'khor ba dang ngan song gi g.yang sar mi lhung ba'i ched du bshad pa dang sgrub pa
la rtse gcig tu brtson par bya dgos pa yin la/ de'ang thog mar bshad pa la ma brten par sgrub pa mi 'byung bas na/ slob dpon mkhas pa rnams kyis 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum
la 'bad pa dang / slob ma rnams kyis kyang sngon du thos bsam la 'bad pa ni med du mi rung ba'i bstan pa'i gzhi chen po

yin par brten/ bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po 'dis kyang sa ngor gyi phyogs su phyi rig pa'i gnas dang / nang mdo rgyud kun la 'chad
nyan mthar phyin pa zhig byung na ci ma rung snyam du dgongs shing / de'ang sa ngor gyi phyogs su phyi nang gi rig gnas kun la 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum tshul bzhin du
bgyid par nus pa'i mkhas pa su'ang ma mchis par brten/ 'dzam gling bsod nams kyis mgron du khug pa'i mchog gi sprul pa'i sku rin po che nges pa don gyi thams cad mkhyen pa
'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po 'di nyid thar rtse rang la sger chod du stsal thub par sde dge chos rgyal chen por snyan sbron phul ba na/ des kyang dgyes bzhin
pa'i sgo nas stsal zhing / de lta bu'i 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i dbang po 'di nyid ni sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi mkhyen brtse nus gsum gcig tu
bsdus te snyigs dus kyi bstan 'gro'i mgon du bsam bzhin du sku'i skye ba bzhes pa'am/ rnam pa gcig tu na rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam par 'phrul par gdon mi za ste/
rtsod bral dus bab kyi gter ston chen po mchog gyur bde chen gling pa'i zab gter las kyang chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan gyi rnam 'phrul du bshad pa dang / yang bdag
gi bla ma rtsod dus kyi kun mkhyen bu ston gnyis pa rdo rje 'chang rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong gis mdzad pa'i 'khrungs rabs gsol 'debs las ni gnas gsar pa 'jam mgon
mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi rnam 'phrul byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po 'di gnyis ka yin par bshad la/ 'di'ang rdo rje'i bka'
nges pa'i gtan tshigs dang bcas

pa zhig ste/ rig 'dzin yongs 'dus kyi chos bdag lung bstan sogs su gnas gsar ba mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan gyi rnam 'khrul yin par bshad pa
dang / yang las 'phro gling pas ni lang gro'i rnam 'phrul du bshad cing / don 'di dag la brten nas rgyal mchog lnga pa rin po ches kyang thog ma'i sprul gzhi ni 'jam pa'i
dbyangs yin la/ de nas shA ri'i bu/ chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan/ lang gro dkon mchog 'byung gnas sogs yin par bshad do/ /gang ltar yang sa la gnas pa'i byang chub
sems dpa' chen po rnams ni 'bad med lhun gyis grub pa'i phrin las kyis sems can gyi don rgyun mi 'chad pa kho na las/ tshe 'di'i snang shas la ltos dgos pa min na'ang /
re zhig byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med dang thugs rgyud gcig par bzung ste/ thar rtse rang gi zhabs drung du mnga' gsol bar mdzad cing / de lta bu'i rje btsun bla ma 'jam pa'i
dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po des kyang 'chad pa dang / rtsod pa dang / rtsom pa la sogs pa'i sgo nas brtse chen snying po'i zhabs kyi ring lugs mtha' dag shin tu dar
zhing rgyas par mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang gsang sngags snga 'gyur ba dang / jo bo bka' gdams pa dang / dwags po bka' brgyud pa dang / shangs pa bka' brgyud pa dang /
zhi byed kyi skor dang / bu lugs dang / jo nang dang / bo dong pa la sogs pa ris su med pa'i chos tshul mtha' dag dar rgyas su mdzad pa dang / khyad par de dag gi nang gses
chos rgyun shin tu phra ba mar me snum zad lta bur gyur pa ji snyed mchis pa thams cad kyang nyams pa gsos te slar yang dbyar mtsho ltar spel ba dang / rje btsun sa skya
pa nas brgyud pa gtso bor gyur

pa'i man ngag thor bu'i skor mtha' dag kyang rgyun mi nus pa'i ched du phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs par mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs kun las btus pa puu sta ka brgyad tsam bzhugs pa thams
cad kyang deng skabs spar du spel bzhin pa'i skabs dang / o rgyan chen pos chos bdag tu ji ltar lung bstan pa bzhin du rtsod bral dus bab kyi gter ston chen po mchog
gyur bde chen gling pas spyan drangs pa'i zab chos rnams kyang phyogs thams cad du dar zhing rgyas par mdzad pa dang / snga na med pa'i rten gsum ngo mtshar can bsam gyis
mi khyab pa bzhengs pa sogs mdor na phrin las nam mkha' dang mnyam zhing ris su med pa'i bstan pa'i srog shing gcig pur gyur pa yin no/ /yang gnas lnga rig pa'i mkhas pa
chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub bam/ mtshan gzhan ngag dbang blo gros snying po gzhan phan mtha' yas pa'i 'od zer zhes yongs su grags pa 'di nyid kyang sku
na chung ngu'i dus nas mdo rgyud mtha' dag la mkhyen pa'i spyan ras gsal bar gyur na'ang / bsten par bya ba'i slob dpon mkhas pa su'ang ma bzhugs par brten phyi rig pa'i
gnas la sbyangs pa mdzad pa zhig ma byung la/ phyis su bcu phrag rig pa'i ma hA paNDi ta 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po e wa~M du phebs pa na/ bdag cag gi dpal
ldan bla ma dam pa 'dis/ da ni khyed kyis kyang phyi rig pa'i gnas la sbyangs pa mthar phyin pa mdzod cig ces bskul ba na/ des kyang de bzhin du mdzad de phyis gnas lnga
rig pa'i ma hA paNDi ta chen por gyur la/ slar yang de'i phrin las kyi rgyun gong nas gong du 'phel ba'i slad du thar rtse rang gi zhabs drung du mnga' gsol bar mdzad
cing / de lta bu'i mkhas pa chen po des kyang

ngor lugs dkyil 'khor bdun la sogs pa'i cho ga mang po nag 'gros su mdzad de spar du spel ba dang / dge 'dun gyi sde chen po gsar du btsugs te 'jam dbyangs sa skya pa'i rang
lugs gsal bar byed pa'i sdom gsum gyi bstan bcos gtsos legs bshad ji snyed spel ba dang bcas bshad sgrub kyi rgyun 'dzugs pa sogs dpal sa skya pa chen po'i bstan pa'i srog
shing gcig pur gyur te phrin las nam mkha' dang mnyam par gyur ro/ /de lta bu'i mkhas pa chen po rnam pa gnyis kyis dpal sa skya pa'i bstan pa rin po che dar zhing rgyas
par mdzad pa'ang bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po 'di'i phrin las kyi rgyun las byung ba yin par shes par bya'o/ /gzod nas de
bzhin gshegs kun gyis/ /srid zhi'i bla mar dbang bskur ba/ /gang de slar yang gzengs bstod pa'i/ /'gro 'di'i blo gros shin tu 'khrul/ /'on te tshur mthong mgu ba'i slad/
/chen po'i go sar mnga' gsol ba/ /de dag kun gyi blo de yang / /khyod kyi rnam 'phrul las gzhan ci/ /e ma che rgu'i gtsug tor rtser/ /zhabs kyi chu skyes nyer bkod pa/
/bde 'byung gtsug na mdzes pa yi/ /zla shel bzhin du rnam par mdzes/ /de lta'i ngo mtshar nyin byed kyis/ /byis blo'i padmo rgyas gyur kyang / /dpyod ldan rnams ni de tsam
du/ /ya mtshan kunda bzhad ma lags/ /khyod kyi 'byor pa mi zad pas/ /snyigs ma'i rgud pa kun 'phrogs te/ /rdzogs ldan lta bur bgyis pa 'dis/ /byed po'ang pham par byas
kyis dogs/ /de ltar mod kyi rgyal sras rnams/ /rang gi spyod tshul spyod pa la/ /ha cang mtshar du brtsi ba yi/ /blo de byis pa yin snyam bgyid/ /rgyal

rnams rang gi bstan pa la/ /btang snyoms mdzad pa'i dus mtha' 'dir/ /khyod kyi phrin las shing rta yis/ /mkhas pa'i nyi gzhon rnam par drangs/ /de lta'i smra ba mchog rnams
kyis/ /thub bstan nyin bzhin spel ba ni/ /rkang gnyis gtso bo 'jig rten 'dir/ /byon pa'i dus la 'gran par bzhin/ /de slad mgon khyod yon tan la/ /rgyal dang khyad par ma
mchis kyang / /snyigs dus bstan pa spel ba la/ /rgyal ba las kyang lhag par mthong / /khyod kyi thun mong ma yin pa'i/ /ngo mtshar rmad byung khab len gyis/ /mkhas rnams
yid kyi lcags phye ni/ /lan cig min par kun tu sdud// //spyi don lnga pa chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i grub 'bras bstan 'dzin gyi slob ma ji tsam byung ba'i tshul ni/ snyigs
dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i rnam thar gsol 'debs las/ yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag thams cad
mkhyen/ /dpal ldan sa skya'i 'jam mgon yab sras sogs/ /gangs can mkhas grub kun gyis phyag byas shing / /gsung gi bdud rtsi gzhes la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/
dam pa 'dis ni zang zing la mi blta ba'i byams pa dang / 'khor ba las sgrol 'dod kyi snying rje chen pos kun nas bslangs te/ ji skad du/ mdo ting 'dzin rgyal po las/ 'phral
du brjod par mi bya yi/ /snod la brtag pa byas nas bya/ /gal te snod ni shes gyur na/ /gsol ma btab kyang bshad par bya/ /'khor ni mang po 'khod nang du/ /gal te ngang
tshul ngan mthong na/ /khyod kyis yo byad bsnyungs mi bshad/ /

sbyin pa'i bsngags pa brjod par bya/ /gal te 'dod pa chung zhig ste/ /tshul khrims dag par gnas yin na/ /khyod kyis byams pa'i sems bskyed la/ /yo byad bsnyungs ba'i gtam gyis
shig /gal te sdig 'dod chung gyur cing / /tshul khrims ldan pa mang gyur la/ /gnyen po rnyed pa de yi tshe/ /tshul khrims bsngags pa brjod par bya/ /zhes sogs gsungs
pa ltar gdul bya rang rang gi snod dang bstun te ngal ba dang dub pa'i rnam pa cung zad kyang mi mnga' bar gong du ji skad bshad pa ltar gyi gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras
tshogs bshad tshar bcu dang / slob bshad tshar drug ste bcu drug dang / rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang tshar gnyis/ kye rdor bka' babs bzhi'i dbang tshar drug la sogs pa mdor
na rje rang gis gang gsan pa'i zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos mtha' dag lan grangs mang po'i bar du stsol bar mdzad pa la brten/ zhal slob kyang stod mnga' ris skor gsum/
bar dbus gtsang ru bzhi/ smad mdo khams sgang drug rnams nas gdul bya skal ba dang ldan pa sprin bzhin du 'dus pa rnams re re nas smos kyis mi lang mod/ mdor bsdu ba'i
dbang du byas te brjod na/ gangs ljongs skye rgu'i skyabs gcig sa skya 'khon gyi gdung brgyud du 'khrungs pa lnga/ rgyal bas lung gis bsngags pa'i ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
chen po'i chos kyi khri la zhabs sen rnam par bkod pa drug /'jig rten gyi khams na 'gran zla dang bral ba'i mkhas pa chen po 'dzam gling mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan lnga/
kun mkhyen e wa~M pa chen po'i ring lugs 'dzin skyong spel gsum byed pa la rab tu chas pa'i zhabs drung rnam pa brgyad/ bstan pa stobs kyis 'dzin pa'i chos rgyal chen
po yab sras bzhi

gtso bor gyur pa'i rgyal rigs du ma/ stobs dang 'byor pas sgeg pa'i mi chen du rlom pa mang po/ rgyal po'i bla'i mchod gnas su mnga' gsol zhing zab rgyas kyi chos tshul ston
pa bdun/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum la dbang 'byor pa'i bshes gnyen lung rig smra ba drug /dgon sde so so'i mkhan po dang slob dpon dang sprul sku dang chos rje'i rigs mang
po/ rtse gcig tu sgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i rnal 'byor pa mang po/ sdom pa gsum char gyi bka' drin rdzogs par nos pa'i slob ma sum stong tsam/ chos 'brel tsam zhus
pa'i slob ma grangs las 'das pa rnams su yod pa las/ dang po gangs ljongs skye rgu'i skyabs gcig sa skya 'khon gyi gdung brgyud du 'khrungs pa lnga ni/ mkhas dang grub
pa'i gtsug rgyan yab rje grub pa'i dbang phyug ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang po/ mtha' klas bstan 'gro'i dpa' mgon 'jam dpal ngur smrig 'dzin
pa mgon po 'dis dbang re zung las bka' chos che rigs ma gsan dngos grub dpal 'bar/ gter ston mchog gyur bde chen gling pa'i zab gter las sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms kyi
rnam 'phrul du lung bstan pa'i sngags 'chang bla ma khri chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang bkra shis rin chen theg mchog bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ smin grol gdams pa rgya
mtsho'i gter gyur sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dpal ngur smrig rnam rol gdung sras phyogs kyi glang po dang lnga'o/ /gnyis pa rgyal bas lung gis bsngags
pa'i ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen po'i chos kyi khri la zhabs sen rnam par bkod pa drug ni/

bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang chen po mtshan brjod par dka' ba don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba rnal 'byor
'jam dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang / rgyud sde'i rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag khang sar mkhan rin po che ngag dbang blo gros bzang po pa dang / 'di gnyis kyis kye rdor
rgyu lam gyi dbang tsam las bka' chos che rigs ma gsan de'i sku'i dbon po gzhan phan byang chub sems kyis 'gro ba rnams smin grol la 'god pa mkhan rin po che ngag dbang
blo gros bstan 'dzin pa dang / shin tu lkog gyur gyi chos rnams kyang mngon shes kyi me long dwangs pa'i ngos su shar ba phan khang mkhan rin po che kun dga' bstan pa'i blo
gros pa dang / lung rigs smra ba'i dbang phyug khang sar mkhan rin po che ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa dang / da lta chos kyi khril zhabs sen rnam par bkod pa'i
khang gsar mkhan chen rin po che 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho pa dang drug go /gsum pa 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir 'gran zla dang bral ba'i mkhas pa chen po 'dzam gling
mdzes par byed pa'i rgyan lnga ni/ mchog tu gyur pa nyi ma lta bu gcig dang / zla ba lta bu bzhi ste lnga las/ dang po ni rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs mi'i srid pa 'dzin
pa snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa 'dzam gling byang phyogs kyi thub dbang gnyis pa lta bur gyur pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas so/ /gnyis
pa zla ba lta bu bzhi ni/ rtsod dus kyi kun mkhyen bu ston rin po che dang / de nyid kyi rnam par 'phrul pa rdo rje 'chang tshar pa chos kyi rje sogs slar yang rang nyid
kyi bstan pa spel ba la bsam bzhin du sku'i skye ba bzhes pa mkhas dang grub pa gnyis

char gyi yon tan phul du son pa rdo rje 'chang rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas dang / brtse chen snying po'i zhabs kyi ring lugs 'dzin skyong spel
gsum byed pa la kun mkhyen e wa~M pa nyid dang rnam dbyer med pa'i gnas lnga rig pa'i mkhas pa chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang legs grub bam mtshan gzhan ngag dbang
blo gros snying po gzhan la phan pa mtha' yas pa'i 'od zer du grags pa'i zhal snga nas dang / zhwa ser gyi cod pan 'dzin pa rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu lta bur gyur pa
a mdo bkra shis 'khyil gyi brag dgon zhabs drung rin po che bcu phrag rig pa'i ma hA paNDi ta chen po dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas kyi zhal snga nas dang / mnyam med ri
bo dge ldan pa chen po'i bstan pa'i snang byed mtshungs zla dang bral ba lnga rig smra ba'i dbang po sog po don grub rgyal mtshan pa rnams so/ /dus 'di tsam na mkhas pa chen
po de dag gi phrin las kyis bod dang bod chen po'i ljongs thams cad mdzes par byas pa yin no/ /bzhi pa kun mkhyen e wa~M pa chen po'i ring lugs 'dzin skyong spel gsum
byed pa la rab tu chas pa'i zhabs drung rnam pa brgyad ni/ rje 'di'i sku'i dbon po mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan bsam las 'das pa bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa
zhabs drung rin po che 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan pa dang / dpal brtse ba chen po'i sku zhang shar pa'i rigs su sku 'khrungs pa'i klu ldings zhabs drung rin po
che ngag dbang ye shes rgyal mtshan pa dang / de'i sku'i dbon po mdo sngags bstan pa'i snang byed klu lding zhabs drung rin po che shes rab chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa dang
/ de'i sku mched lung rtogs yon tan rgya mtsho'i bdag

nyid zhabs drung rin po che byams pa tshul khrims phun tshogs pa dang / mkhyen brtse nus pa'i gter mnga' phan khang zhabs drung rin po che dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan pa
dang / zhwa lu sku zhang gi rigs su sku 'khrungs pa'i khang sar zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang blo gros snying po pa dang / rje rang gi snag dbon thar rtse zhabs drung
ngag gi dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs rin chen rdo rje pa dang / mkhyen pa'i spyan ras bkra ba gdong tshang zhabs drung rin po che rnams so/ /lnga pa bstan pa stobs kyis 'dzin
pa'i chos rgyal chen po yab sras bzhi la sogs pa ni/ gsung rab mang po'i pha rol tu son cing 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum dang stobs kyi sgo nas bstan pa 'dzin pa sde dge chos
rgyal chen po tshe dbang rdo rje rig 'dzin pa'am phyis rab tu byung ba'i mtshan byams pa kun dga' sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan pa dang / de'i lha sras che ba chos
rgyal byang chub sems dpa' chen po dam tshig rdo rje tshe ring rnam rgyal ba dang / lha sras bar pa rgya chen chos kyi spyan ldan byams pa kun dga' 'jam dpal phan bde'i
snying po pa dang / lha sras chung ba mkhyen rab kyi me tog bkra ba tshe dbang rdo rje dgra 'dul ba ste bzhi dang / snga 'gyur rnying ma'i bstan 'dzin chen po gling zhal
ngo rje drung par grags pas kyang gus 'dud bsnyen bkur bla na med pa dang bcas rgyud sde'i dbang bskur 'ga' zhig ched du gsan pa dang / gzhan yang bka' chos kyi 'brel
pa tsam thob pa'i gling tshang la sogs pa rgyal rigs su gtogs pa shin tu mang ngo / /drug pa mi chen du gtogs pa ni/ mda' dpon chen po tsha rong pa yab sras gnyis dang /
mda' dpon rin spungs pas gtso byas pa'i dbus gtsang gi ljongs su 'khod pa'i mi chen mang po dang / sde dge chos

rgyal chen po'i bka'i blon chen rnams dang / phyag mdzod la sogs pa dang / gzhan yang khams phyogs kyi sga stod dang / rag shul dang / hor pa sogs kyi dpon khag dang / go 'jo
sde pa khag sogs mi chen phal che bas rje 'di'i zhabs la ma btud pa cher med pa yin no/ /bdun pa rgyal po'i bla'i mchod gnas su mnga' gsol zhing zab rgyas kyi chos tshul
ston pa bdun ni/ 'jam dbyangs gong ma chen po'i mchod gnas lcang skya thams cad mkhyen pa sogs ris su med pa'i grub mtha' yongs kyi gtsug gi nor buu lta bur gyur cing
'chad rtsod rtsom gsum la dbang bsgyur ba'i khro shul bla ma ngag dbang smin grol rgya mtsho pa dang / smin grol gdams pa'i gter mdzod bla ma ngag dbang chos 'byor pa dang
/ yi dam gyi lha mang po'i bsnyen sgrub pha mthar son pa grub mchog ngag dbang rin chen pa dang / grub pa mchog gi ded dpon bla ma dpal ldan phrin las pa dang / mkhas dang
grub pa'i gtsug rgyan bla ma dge 'dun rgya mtsho pa dang / snyan brgyud rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag bla ma ngag dbang bzang po pa dang / nyams dang rtogs pa'i dbang phyug
bla ma 'jam dbyangs blo gsal rnams so/ /brgyad pa bshes gnyen lung rig smra ba bdun ni/ rab 'byams mdo rgyud rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son cing 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum la thogs
pa med pa'i mkhas pa chen po shar bla ma kun dga' dpal ldan/ phun tshogs gling gi mkhan po lung rig smra ba bka' chen blo bzang dge legs kun khyab/ lnga rig smra ba'i
dbang po sde gzhung bla ma blo gros dbang phyug /lung rig smra ba klog pa ba shes rab rgya mtsho/ rgya chen chos kyi spyan ldan bla ma bstan pa dar rgyas/ mkhas btsun bzang
po'i gter gyur phan bde bzang po/

mkhas pa'i dbang po 'jam dbyangs yon tan mtha' yas rnams so/ /dgu pa dgon sde so so'i mkhan po dang slob dpon dang sprul sku dang chos rje'i rigs ni/ bzhad thub bstan yangs
pa can gyi mkhan po dang / rgyal rtse gur pa mkhan po sogs mkhan po'i rigs du ma dang / e wa~M nas khang ser dpon slob 'jam dbyangs grags pa dang / dpon slob ngag dbang
dge legs pa dang / dpon slob nam mkha' rgyal mtshan pa dang / 'bras yul skyed tshal gyi slob dpon dkon mchog chos 'phel sogs slob dpon gyi rigs su gtogs pa shin tu mang po
dang / khams phyogs kyi sa dgon yod do cog gi sprul sku che phra ji snyed cig bzhugs pa rnams dang / sde dge'i shar nub kyi bla ma snga phyir byon pa rnams dang / lhun
grub steng gi dgon dpon ye shes dpal ldan pa/ gling dpon po'i zhal ngo mgo zi drung pa dang / sga stod bra'u dpon bla sogs mdor na khams phyogs kyi sa dgon yod do cog gi
dgon dpon dang / slob dpon dang / dbu mdzad la sogs pa ni re re nas smos kyis mi lang ngo / /bcu pa rtse gcig tu sgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i rnal 'byor pa ni/ sde
dge chos rgyal chen po'i mnga' zhabs su 'khod pa'i tshe 'di blos btang gi rnal 'byor pa ji snyed cig bzhugs pa rnams dang / sga stod kyi phyogs su'ang rtse gcig sgrub pa'i
rgyal mtshan 'dzin pas nyams rtogs gong 'phel du gyur pa mkha' spyod grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po skye rgu dgon gyi mtshams pa ngag dbang bsam gtan pa dang / nyams dang
rtogs pa'i dbang phyug grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba seng rtse kun dga' dpal 'byor pa dang / mang du thos shing sgrub pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa grub pa mchog gi

ded dpon 'khor lo gsum gyi phrin las rmad du byung ba khri 'du skal bzang dgon gyi snang rtse ri khrod du bzhugs pa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa kun dga' chos dbang sogs rnal 'byor pa
shin tu mang po dang / gzhan yang gling tshang dang / hor khog dang / li thang sogs su bzhugs pa'i rnal 'byor pa du ma dang / e wa~M rang du'ang spong ba pa phrin las rab
rgyas dang / 'jam dpal bstan 'dzin dang / bsod nams bzang po sogs snga phyir rje 'di'i zhal slob kyi mtshams pa shin tu mang ngo / /bcu gcig pa sdom pa gsum char gyi bka'
drin rdzogs par nos pa'i slob ma ni/ rje 'di e wa~M pa'i chos kyi khri la lo bcu bzhugs pa'i skabs/ lo re bzhin sdom pa gsum char gyi bka' drin rdzogs par nos pa'i slob
ma mang dus sum brgya tsam dang / 'bring gi dus phyed sum brgya skor dang / nyung dus kyang nyis brgya re 'ong bar snang la/ gzhan yang snga phyir khams su phebs skabs
dang bod du bzhugs skabs kyi slob ma byung ba thams cad bsdoms pas sum stong zin pa tsam yod par mngon no/ /bcu gnyis pa chos 'brel tsam thob pa'i slob ma ni/ mdo khams
sde dge'i phyogs kyi kar rnying gi bstan 'dzin skyes bu mkhas grub du mas mtshon te/ stod mnga' ris nas smad rgya mtshams la thug gi bar bgrang ba las 'das pa yin no/ /snyigs
dus bstan 'gro'i dpal nyid du/ /mi yi srid pa legs bzung ste/ /phrin las kun gsal dang mnyam pas/ /thub bstan dbyar gyi mtsho bzhin spel/ /des kyang khyod thugs ku mud
gnyen/ /tshim pa'i cha shas ma rdzogs par/ /slar yang 'khor ba ma stong bar/ /de srid bstan pa spel ba'i slad/ /khyod gsung dbyar gyi dpal mo yis/ /

skyed bsrings dam pa'i me tog ni/ /bsngags 'os dri bsung ring 'thul bas/ /phyogs rnams thams cad dog por byas/ /de tshe bshad dang sgrub pa yis/ /srid zhi'i khyon kun 'gengs
pa dang / /lhan cig nying slob mkhas dang grub/ /sa chen rdul dang mnyam par sprul/ /de slad dngos dang brgyud pa yi/ /bka' drin gzhal bar dka' ba 'di/ /theg dka'i dogs
pas nor 'dzin khyon/ /rnam pa drug tu 'dar ba snyam/ /e ma mgon khyod yon tan la/ /tshad bzung nus pa lta ci smos/ /slob ma nyid slob bcas pa yi/ /ngo mtshara'ang tshangs
blos gzhal mi nus// //spyi don drug pa sdom pa gsum la gces spras su mdzad cing nyams rtogs ji ltar 'khrungs pa'i tshul bye brag tu bshad pa ni/ snyigs dus kyi thams cad
mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i rnam thar gsol 'debs las/ brtan mkhas tshul khrims dri yis phyogs kun khyab/ /gzhan phan
byang chub sems gnyis gting nas 'byongs/ /tha mal 'khrul snang lha dang ye shes su/ /yongs shar grub pa'i dbang por gsol ba 'debs/ /brtse chen brnyes pa bzang po'i ring lugs
la/ /gzhan dring mi 'jog shes nas dad thob bzhin/ /ris med bstan la dag pa'i snang ba yis/ /bsngags pa'i me tog 'thor la gsol ba 'debs/ /rab 'byams lhag pa'i lha yis
rjes bzung zhing / /ji lta ji snyed shes bya kun mkhyen kyang / /yon tan sbas pa'i ngang tshul lhur mdzad phyir/ /rnam thar bsam mi khyab la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes gsungs pa
ltar bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'dis ni bstan pa'i snying po sde snod gsum gyi nyams su blang bya bslab pa rin po che rnams

la nyams bzhes snying por mdzad pa la brten nas/ spangs pa dang rtogs pa'i yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa la dbang bsgyur zhing / de dag gi ngo mtshar cha shas tsam yang so
so skye bo'i blo gros kyis brjod par mi nus mod/ 'on te rags rim tsam brjod na/ spyir ni yang srid snga ma rnams nas dge ba la goms pa brtas pa'i shugs kyis sku na chung
ngu'i dus nas kyang rang bzhin gyis kha na ma tho ba ci yang mi mdzad na/ sku nar son zhing bslab pa rin po che rnams zhal gyis 'ches tshun chad nas de rnams dang 'gal ba
lta ci smos/ khyad par lhag pa tshul khrims kyi bslab pa ni bstan pa'i gzhi ma yin par dgongs nas/ dgag sgrub gnang gsum gyi bslab bya phra zhing phra ba rnams kyang spyan
gyi 'bras bu ltar gces par bskyangs te blang dor tshul bzhin du mdzad cing / de la brten nas ltung ba che ba'i rigs lta ci/ nyes pa shin tu phra zhing phra bas kyang ma
gos par brten sku lus las kyang sbyar ba'i spos bzang po dang / kaShmI ra'i gur gum dang / ga bur dang / tsan dan la sogs pa'i phun sum tshogs pa'i dri gang gis kyang mtshon
du med cing / de dag zil gyis gnon nus pa'i tshul khrims kyi dri bsrung zh-im po rgyang ring du 'thul ba dang / gang du bzhugs pa'i gnas khang dang / na bza' dang /
sku chas thams cad la'ang yun ches ring po'i bar dri bzang pos khyab pa ni thams cad la mngon sum du snang ba 'di yin la/ rgyu mtshan de'i phyir na btsun pa brtan pa'i yon
tan dang / mkhas shing phan 'dogs pa'i yon tan thams cad lhun gyis grub pa'i rje btsun dam pa 'di ni sngon gyi 'phags pa dgra bcom pa rnams dang tshul mtshungs pa yin
no/ /der ma zad bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam

pa 'di ni bskal ba dpag tu med pa'i sngon rol nas byang chub mchog tu thugs bskyed cing / de'i bslab par bya ba mtha' dag tshul bzhin du bslabs pa la brten/ sku tshe 'dir yang
thog ma nyid nas theg chen gyi rigs sad pa'i stobs kyis byang chub kyi sems rin po che rnam pa gnyis thugs rgyud la rang shugs kyis 'khrungs shing / gzhan la phan pa
kho na lhur mdzad pa yin la/ khyad par sems bskyed kyi sdom pa gsan tshul chad de nas bshad pa'i dkar po'i chos bzhi la sogs pa'i bslab bya mtha' dag sgrub pa dang / nag
po'i chos bzhi la sogs pa'i spang bya thams cad spong ba dang / gzhan yang ltung ba dang / ltung med dang / ltung ba'i gzugs brnyan dang / ltung med kyi gzugs brnyan rnams
kyang ma nor bar mkhyen bzhin pa'i sgo nas blang dor tshul bzhin du mdzad pa dang / gal te ltung ba phra mo tsam 'byung srid na'ang phung po gsum pa la sogs pa'i sgo nas
bshags bsdam tshul bzhin du mdzad pas rgya mtsho chen po ro dang mi 'grogs pa bzhin du nyes pas mi gos pa yin no/ /gzhan yang mgon med pa dang / skyabs med pa dang / dpung
gnyen med pa'i sems can nyam thag pa dag gzigs pa'am gsan pa tsam gyis rang dbang med par spyan chab 'byung zhing / de dag la phan pa'i thabs kho na lhur mdzad pa dang
/ dbul zhing phongs pa rnams gzigs pa'am gsan ma thag tu ji ltar 'dod pa'i zas dang gos la sogs pa lhug par stsol ba dang / rje rang gi zhal nas kyang / nged la bzang po
byung bas dga' tshor dang / ngan pa byung bas sdug rgyu med pa zhig yod pa yin zhes bka' stsal ba ni 'jig rten chos brgyad mgo snyoms shing / rang 'dod kyi 'khri ba dang
bral ba ste/ de la brten nas skye bo

ngan pa rang gis rang nyid ngan song du lhung bar byed pa kha cig gis skur pa 'debs pa dang / log sgrub sgo du ma nas brtsams kyang de dag la thugs 'khrugs pa med par slar
yang lhag par brtse ba'i sgo nas gnod len du phan 'dogs pa sogs byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i spyod tshul las nam yang g.yo ba med pa yin no/ /khyad par gsang
sngags rdo rje theg pa'i rgyud sde chen po bzhi dang 'brel ba'i dbang bskur ba rnams legs par gsan phyin chad bya ba'i rgyud kyi spyi'i dam tshig gsum/ khyad par gyi dam
tshig bcu gsum/ spyod pa'i rgyud la thun mong ma yin pa'i dam tshig bzhi/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud la khas blangs kyis thob pa rigs lnga spyi dang so so'i dam tshig /cho gas
thob pa'i dam tshig dpal mchog nas bshad pa bcu/ rdo rje 'byung ba nas bshad pa gcig ste bcu gcig /rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud kyi dbang bzhi so so'i dam tshig rnams
kyang srung sdom gyi ra ba las nam yang mi 'da' bar mdzad cing / de'i ngang nas dngos grub thams cad kyi rtsa ba dpal ldan bla ma dam pa rnams dang lhag pa'i lha tha mi
dad par 'du shes pa'i sgo nas thugs dad bsam gyis mi khyab pas gsol ba 'debs pa dang / gong du bshad pa'i yi dam gyi lha'i ljags bsnyen rnams mdzad pa dang / dus rgyun gyi
thugs dam nyams bzhes kyi rim pa'ang lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi nyams len gyi gnad zab mo dang ma bral ba'i sgo nas lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang / dpal kye
rdo rje phyi nang sbrags ma'i mngon rtogs lam dus kyi dbang blang ba dang bcas pa shin tu rgyas pa dang / rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi srung ba dang / nA ro mkha' spyod ma ste
sa skya pa'i chag med bzhir grags pa rnams dang / 'jam dbyangs dkar po dang / dbyangs can

ma dkar dmar gnyis dang / 'byung 'dul dang / mgon dkar dang / rdo rje brag rdzong ma rnams kyi mngon rtogs bzlas pa dang bcas pa dang / spyan ras gzigs kyi bdag bskyed sngon
du 'gro ba'i dzaM ser nag gi chu sbyin dang / gtor ma brgya rtsa dang / dbyu gu drug cu rtsa bzhi dang / yi dwags la chu sbyin dang bcas pa rnams dang / gtor bsngos kyang
kye rdo rje/ mkha' spyod ma/ 'byung po 'dul byed/ seng gdong ma/ mgon dkar/ rigs byed ma/ gur/ zhal/ dur bdag /las mgon/ stag zhon/ dmag zor ma/ bektse/ mkha' 'gro'i spyi
ste de rnams la gtor 'bul gyi cho ga shin tu rgyas pa dang bcas pa rnams ma chag par mdzad cing / de'ang bka' chos 'chad nyan gyi skabs ma gtogs rgyun par snga dro nas
nyi ma phyed ma zin tsam gyi bar du thugs dam kho na dang / de nas skabs su bab pa'i thugs brel rnams bcad de/ slar yang dgongs mos srib nas bzung ste mtshan phyed ma zin
tsam gyi bar du thugs dam kho na la gzhol bar mdzad pa yin la/ khams phyogs su chibs bskyod bskyangs pa'i dus sogs skabs 'gar thug brel shin tu che ba'i skabs kyang nyin
mo bka' chos 'chad spel sogs mdzad cing / mtshan mo thugs dam kho na la gzhol bas gtor bsngos grub pa dang nam lang pa 'ang shin tu mang zhing / de lta bu'i brtson 'grus
kyis mnyam pa bzhag pa'i rnal 'byor rnams dang / mnyam par ma bzhag pa'i rnal 'byor thams cad ltag sprad de nyams su bzhes pa la brten nas dus skad cig tsam la'ang tha
mal pa'i rnam par rtog pa skye ba'i skabs mi rnyed pa yin no/ /rtogs pa'i yon tan nyams snang la sogs pa'ang bdag cag gdul bya thun mong ba rnams kyi skal pa dang mthun
par mthong thos cung

zad byung ba 'ga' zhig kyang bsnyad na/ dgung lo bcu tsam bzhes pa'i skabs/ rje 'di thar rtse'i gzim chung bsam gtan yang rtser bzhugs pa'i snga dro'i dus shig gi tshe gzim
chung g.yab chen du gzigs pa na/ de'i nam mkha' thams cad sprin gyis gang ba'i gseb na rgyal chen rnam thos sras bzhugs shing / sa gzhir gzigs pa na sa gzhi thams cad kyang
chu'am shel gyi rnam pa lta bu la nam mkha'i gzugs brnyan shar ba'i tshul gyis rnam thos sras khra lam mer gsal ba mngon sum du gzigs pa dang / yang nub cig mnal lam
du nam mkha' nas ne'u le shin tu yid du 'ong ba/ lus kyi spu mdog kyang rma bya'i sgro'i thig le ji lta ba bzhin gyi nor bu'i ri mo sna tshogs su yod pa nyi shu rtsa gcig
thar rtse'i pho brang steng gi gser zangs kyi ganydzi ra'i steng du babs/ de nas kyang rim gyis babs te gzim chung bsam gtan yang rtser song ba'i snang ba zhig byung gsung
ste/ de ni bla brang 'di 'byor pa je cher song ba 'di'i ltas dang / dza~M lha nyer gcig gi g.yang skyabs 'dra'ang byas pas de la blta ba 'dra gsung ba dang / yang skabs
shig gi tshe mnal lam gyi gsal snang du/ mdun gyi nam mkhar rin po che sna tshogs las grub pa'i khri shin tu rgya che zhing dpangs mtho ba/ de'i steng gi mdun nas brtsams
te g.yas skor du gnas brten chen po yan lag 'byung nas bzung 'phags pa'i gnas brtan chen po bcu drug bzhugs shing / de rnams kyi phyag stabs kyang / yan lag 'byung phyag
gnyis mnyam gzhag mdzad pa ma gtogs gzhan rnams ngag 'don dang mthun zhing / gnas brtan re re'i sku tshad kyang thog tshad re tsam yod pa dang / khri de'i mdun du rje
rang nyid bzhugs shing / mchod pa'i tshul gyis rgyal rnga zhig brdungs pa

dang / thugs rgyud la snga na med pa'i bde gsal mi rtog pa'i nyams bsam gyis mi khyab pa skyes pa'i snang ba zhig byung gsung ba dang / khri de'i dbus su thub pa'i dbang po
bzhugs pa ma mthong ba ni lung rtogs kyi bstan pa nyams dma' ba 'di la blta ba 'dra gsung zhing / thub dbang gnas bcu dang bcas pa'i bris thang yang gsum bzhi tsam bzhengs
par mdzad pa dang / e wa~M pa'i mkhan sa zhal 'dzin gnang ba'i skabs shig gnal lam du lha ldan gyi phyogs thams cad thal rlung lta bu zhig gis gang bar rmis pas/ phyogs
der mi bde ba zhig 'ong ba 'dra zhes gsungs pa bzhin du phyis lha ldan du skye mkhar lcog spe ba dang / tshe smon gling pa sogs 'khrugs 'dzings sna tshogs pa zhig byung
ba dang / yang de skabs shig gi mnal lam du/ sa skya'i phyogs thams cad na bun lta bu zhig gis gang bar rmis pas der yang mi bde bar zhig 'ong ba 'dra gsungs pa bzhin du
sku ngo khag rnams thugs mthun min sna tshogs pa zhig byung ba dang / sa skya nas yab rje ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis mthu stobs bstan 'dzin bzang pos rje 'di mkhan chen
nam mkha' bsam grub kyi rnam 'phrul yin ces gsungs shing / rje rang gis kyang dmigs bsal gyi zhal gsar rang mi mdzad rung / de ltar yin rtsis 'dra zhig mdzad kyi yod pa
dang / rje bla ma 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse dbang pos kyang rdo rje 'chang 'di nyid las smin byed kyi thog ma 'khor lo bde mchog nag po spyod pa'i lugs kyi dbang bka' gsan
pa'i bum dbang gi skabs dpal 'khor lo sdom pa zhal phyag yongs rdzogs kyi skur lam gyis gzigs pas rkyen byas/ de phyin rje 'di shrI tsakra sambar dang dbyer med pa'i
mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i rnam 'phrul du nges pa'i thugs dad brtan po dang / sku tshe'i tshad kyang de las lhag par

bzhugs snyam pa'i gsal snang 'khrungs pa phyis thog tu khel zhing / spyir yang snga phyi lan du mar mnal lam du rjes su bzung zhing dbugs dbyung bas byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma
mang du brnyes pa mngon sum gyis grub pa dang / yang mdo khams su thog mar pheb pa'i tshe sde dge smad shod rdzong sar dgon ngos kyi sa phyogs dang / rga stod kyi khri
'du skal bzang dgon pa'i thad kyi sa phyogs dang / rdza khog ste de gsum gyi yul phyogs dang / dgon pa sogs ji lta ba bzhin 'di dang 'di lta bu yod snyam pa'i sems la sa
ler 'char ba zhig yod gsung ba dang / de'i rgyu mtshan ci lags zhus pa na/ tshe snga ma'i bag chags zhig yin pa 'dra tsam las mi gsung yang / don la sku tshe snga ma'i gnas
tshul mtha' dag tshul bzhin du mkhyen pa'i gtan tshigs khyad par can zhig yod par gor ma chag pa dang / yang mdo khams su brag rdzong ma'i sku mtshams zla ba gsum tsam
bzhugs pa'i mjug tu/ de'i sbyin sreg mdzad pa'i tshe bya rog cig thal byung du babs te/ rje 'di'i sku mdun gyi gsol lcogs kyi steng dang / sku'i g.yas g.yon du phar 'gro
tshur 'gro 'ga' zhig byas te/ mthar rje 'di'i gzim chung nang du song te yun cung zad cig bsdad de slar 'phur song ba sku 'khor ba dag gis mthong ba dang / rje rang gi zhal
nas kyang / chos skyong 'di shin tu myur ba zhig yin te/ 'di'i bsnyen pa byed pa'i tshe khrid yig dang bsnyen thabs sogs nas 'byung ba ltar gyi rtags phal cher 'ong ba
zhig yod pa yin gsungs pa la dpags na rtags mtshan khyad par can mang po byung bar gdon mi za ba dang / yang skabs 'gar gnal lam du a tsa ra lag na rkang gling thogs pa
zhig gis glang po cher khal bkal ba zhig ded nas 'ong ba rmis la/ de ni

dpal mgon zhal 'dis phrin las zhig sgrub pa'i ltas yin pa 'dra gsung ba dang / yang sde dger bzhugs skabs lo re bzhin 'bri gnyan gdong gi mgor char 'bebs la yang yang phebs
pa'i skabs phal cher la'ang / gnyan gdong nas rje 'di'i bzhugs gnas sgrub khang la 'ja' zug pa skye bo phal cher gyis mthong ba dang / yang lan cig gnyan gdong mgor char
'bebs la phebs pa'i skabs shig drag char chen po zhig babs par/ de'ang rje 'di'i phebs lam gang yin zheng du 'dom gang tsam yod par char 'bru re gnyis las mi 'bab cing de
min sku'i g.yas g.yon thams cad la babs pa der yod pa'i zhabs 'bring ba thams cad kyis mthong ba dang / yang lan cig yid lhung du phebs pa'i skabs shig /rje 'di'i dbu gur
