gyi phyi thams cad 'ja' kha dog sna lngas gtums shing / de nas 'brog pa zhig gis gdan drangs pa'i sar phebs pa'i skabs kyang / nam mkha' nas 'od dkar po snam bu brkyangs
pa lta bu zhig gis phebs bsu phebs skyel gyi tshul lta bus 'gro 'ong byed pa der 'khod pa thams cad kyis mthong ba dang / gzhan yang sga stod phyogs su phebs pa'i skabs
gzhi bdag mang pos gus pa'i rnam 'gyur byed pa sogs rje rang gis gzigs pa dang / yang sku na chung ngu'i dus skabs 'gar khong pa'i nang nas nyi ma shar ba snyam byed pa'i
gsal seng nge ba'i nyams 'char ba zhig yod ces gsung pa dang / yang dus phyis khang pa'i phyi nang thams cad du ba lta bu zhig gis khengs pa snyam byed pa'i gzigs snang
yang yang byung zhes gsung ba dang / yang phyis su snang ba thams cad yi ge sgrogs shes mi shes tsam gyis khyab pa'i mthong snang zhig rtag tu 'ong gin 'dug ces yang yang
bka' stsal pa dang / yang

mtshan mo snang gsal sogs med pa'i skabs kyang gyang logs kyi ri mo rnams mthong ba snyam byed pa'i gsal snang zhig 'dug ces bka' stsal pa rnams ni rdzogs rim gyi lam mthar
phyin pa'i rtags khyad par can du mngon la/ yang mdo khams su chos skyong gi rjes gnang stsal ba'i skabs kha cig dang / sa skyar yab rje rin po cher chos skyong gi rjes
gnang phul ba'i skabs/ mar me dang nyi ma'i 'od phog pa med kyang gtor bsngos kyi gtor ma'i rgyan rnams don med du skad cig la zhu ba dang / yang skabs 'gar bka' bsgo'i gtor
ma phyag tu bzhes pa dang lhan cig gtor ma gzhan thams cad kyis mgo bo mdun du gug byed pa zhig byung zhing / de dag ni chos skyong rnams ji ltar bsgos pa'i bka' las
mi 'da' ba'i ltas yin par sems la/ khams su rjes ma phebs skabs zhig sde dge lhun grub steng gi shar bla ma mkhas dbang kun dga' dpal ldan pa'i mnal lam du/ rje 'di nyid
sga len steng gi dgon pa'i pha ri de nas chibs pa bzang po zhig la chibs/ dbu'i steng du gdugs ser po shin tu che ba bzung ba med par 'khor/ chibs yob g.yas g.yon du gur
gyi mgon po lcam dral gzi brjid kyi dpal rab tu 'bar ba dag gis brten nas phebs par mthong bas/ de phyin chad rje 'di nges par rdo rje 'chang chen po'i ngo bo ste/ sa bcu'i
dbang phyug chos skyong gi rnam par bzhengs pa rnams kyis kyang zhabs 'bring ba'i tshul du mdzad par gdon mi za ba'i thugs dang gting nas 'khrungs pa'i tshul yang yang
gsungs zhes thos pa dang / yang rje 'di e wa~M pa'i mkhan po zhal 'dzin gnang ba'i skabs/ yid srubs kyis rgyud bslad pa 'ga' zhig gis tho ba tsams par byas kyang / rje 'dis
de dag la mi

dges pa med mod/ chos srung rnams ni ma bcol yang bstan dgra rdul du rlog pa chos nyid yin pa ltar/ pha rol po de dag kyang mi ring bar lnga pa'i lam du gyur pa ni bstan srung
rnams bran du 'khol ba'i nus pa yin par mngon te/ rgyu mtshan cis she na/ 'dre mthong ba kha cig gis mgon khang nang nas mi nag po gnyis byung ste/ de dag gis ma rungs
pa de khrid nas tshur 'ong ba mngon sum du mthong ba'i phyir ro/ /yang nor lha'i rigs 'ga' zhig gi rjes su gnang ba stsal ba'i tshe/ gtor ma las chu babs pa mngon sum du
mthong ba dang / ngor du bzhugs skabs zhig gnal lam du/ sde dge dgon chen gyi lha sar 'khris der kham bu'i ljon pa sdong po gsum 'dug kyang / me tog dang 'bras bu sogs
med pa'i dpangs dma' ba las mi snang / de'i phar phyogs thams cad bye thang lta bu nyams mi dga' ba zhig gzigs pas thugs mi bde snyam byed pa zhig byung ba la dpags na lha
sras rin po che dam tshig rdo rje pa sku mched gsum ka'ang sku tshe phrin las ha cang rgyun mi ring ba dang / de rjes tsam sde dge'i bstan srid la'ang bar stongs zhig 'ong
rgyu e yin ces bka' stsal zhing thugs khral gyi rnam pa mdzad pa dang / lha sras bla ma bod du phebs pa'i skad ca gsan skabs mnal lam du/ ngor gyi la chung la nas nyi
ma zhig 'char byung yang / rgyang tsam shar nas phyir 'gros byas te skar ma lta bu'i 'od med pa'i je chung zhig tu yal song ba/ khong pa skye brgyud bzang ba 'dra zhig e
yin kyang / sku tshe dang phrin las bstan phan sogs chen po rang 'ong dka' ba 'dra zhes phebs pa dag phyis su ji lta ba bzhin thog tu son pa dang / gzhan yang dus phyis
bal bod dmag 'khrugs kyi skabs/ dbus gtsang gi 'byor ldan phal che bas nor rdzas gzhan du spo ba sogs byed kyang / rje

'dis de tsam gyi skyon mi 'ong ba'i tshul gsungs pa'ang de kho na ltar mngon du gyur pa sogs de 'dra'i rigs can shin tu mang / spyir yang rgyun par thugs brtag zhu ba'i tshe
ni ci'ang mi mkhyen pa'i tshul gyis 'jam dbyangs rdel mo sogs la nan tan du gzigs te de nas 'byung ba bzhin lung ston par mdzad la/ de'ang ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin thog
tu khel ba kho na 'byung mod/ /de bas kyang skabs 'gar thol byung du bka' stsal pa rnams shin tu tig che bar snang zhing / de la brten nas sde dge chos rgyal chen po sogs
zhal slob dang sbyin bdag rgyus yod pa phal che bas ni thugs brtag zhu ba las gsung sgros kyi tshig zur la brtag pa nyid legs zer ba kho na 'byung / mdor na mngon par shes
pa thogs med du mnga' bar gdon mi za na'ang / bdag cag so so skye bo rnams kyi snang ngo dang mthun par ci'ang mi mkhyen pa'i tshul 'ba' zhig mdzad par mngon/ gzhan yang
sku dngos kyis dbang bskur ba dang / byin gyis brlabs pas ni 'gal rkyen las grol ba smos ci dgos/ ljags chab dang gsang chab tshun gyis kyang skye bo mang po nad gdon
las grol ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar bsam las 'das pa yin no/ /mdor na rang nyid spangs pa dang rtogs pa'i yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa la dbang 'byor yang / rgyags
pa dang dregs pa lta ci/ skye bo dman pa shin tu nyam chung ba tshun chad la'ang zhe sa dang bcas pa'i gtam gyis mgu par mdzad cing / de la brten nas mtshan dpe rjes mthun
pa thob pas blta bas chog mi shes par mdzes shing brjid chags la tshul khrims kyi dri bsung ring du 'thul ba'i sku mthong ba dang / gdul bya so so'i blo dang 'tshams
par 'dod rgur 'char bas rna bar

snyan cing snying la 'babs pa'i gsung bdud rts-i'i sgra dbyangs zab mo thos pa tsam gyis kyang mos gus bcos ma ma yin pa skye ba kho na 'byung ba yin te/ gangs can gyi mgon
po rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs bcu pa tshul khrims rgya mtsho'i zhal snga nas mtshan nyid kyi gsan pa rdzogs pa'i mtshams/ sngags kyi smin grol rgya che ba zhig gsan
bzhes mdzad rgyu byung na/ sngon skyabs mgon lnga pa rin po che'i rnam thar ltar dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gsung ngag slob bshad dang / gser chos bcu gsum/ mgon po che chung
sogs snyan brgyud zab mo'i skor rnams rje 'di las gsan pa'i thugs 'dun 'khrungs zhes bka' stsal tshul nges pa can thos pa dang / sgrub brgyud bstan pa'i gtsug rgyan
si tur chog sprul rin po che lta bus kyang / rje 'di nyid 'brel tshad don ldan du gzigs pa'i thugs mos chen pos snga phyir skyabs 'jug gi rten ched du 'bul bar mdzad pas
mtshon mchog dman bar ma thams cad kyis mgrin gcig tu bsngags pa'i me tog 'thor zhing zang zing gi 'byor pa rgya mtsho'i sprin lta bus mngon par mchod pa dang / lhag par
rang nyid brtse chen snying po'i zhabs kyi ring lugs la shes nas dad pa thob pa bzhin du/ ris su med pa'i grub mtha' gzhan la'ang de lta bu'i dag snang phyogs med du rgyas
pa sogs rnam par thar pa phyogs gang nas gzhig kyang legs pa 'ba' zhig las skyon gyi rnam pa cung zad kyang mi mnga'/ de ltar na sangs rgyas dngos 'jig rten du byon par
snang yang / bdag cag so so skye bo las dang nyon mongs pas bsgribs pa rnams kyis ni so skye rang rgyud par mthong ba 'di ni shin tu 'khrul tshabs che ba zhig go /'ga' zhig
rdo rje theg pa la/ /brten nas so thar 'dor byed pa/ /'khyags pa'i steng gi khang pa bzhin/ /

mtho yang dma' ba nyid du lhung / /la la theg dman la 'chel nas/ /theg pa chen por mi 'jug pa/ /de dag bud med la sred pas/ /rgyal srid 'byor pa btang ba bzhin/ /'phags rnams
sdig pa gzhil ba'i slad/ /dam chos bdud rtsi bsten pa ste/ /kye ma skal ba med rnams kyis/ /chos la brten nas mi dge sgrub/ /mgon khyod de tshul ring dor nas/ /rang srog
bas kyang tshul khrims la/ /gces par bsung 'dis nyes spyod rnams/ /khros nas gzhan du song ba snyam/ /tshul khrims dag pa'i lus mchog las/ /dri zhim spos kyi ngad ldang
ba/ /'jig rten khams 'dir mchis pa yi/ /spos mchog brgya yis bsgrun du med/ /khyad par byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /sdom pa'i dpung tshogs yan lag bzhis/ /rang don yid byed
dgra tshogs kun/ /ming tsam zhig ni lhag mar byas/ /'gro kun snying la bde ster ba'i/ /gzhan phan las 'di bdud rtsi ste/ /tshul min yid byed gcod pa la/ /sog le bas kyang
shin tu rtsub/ /mgon khyod ris med 'gro ba la/ /'dod rgu sbyin pa'i dpag bsam shing / /khyad par shin tu nyam thag dang / /gnod byed rnams kyi gnyen bshes yin/ /rig 'dzin
sngags kyi sdom pa yi/ /nor bu'i gling du rab zhugs te/ /dran dang shes bzhin chu rgyun gyis/ /spang bya'i dri ma mtha' dag bkrus/ /snang ba lha ru shar ba dang / /rlung
sems dbu mar bsdu ba dang / /lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med kyis/ /sa dang lam gyi rtse mor bgrod/ /ji ltar dwangs pa'i rdzing bu ru/ /kun gyi gzugs brnyan shar ba bzhin/
/sgrib bral ye shes me long du/ /dag pa'i gzugs brnyan ci yang 'char/ /ston dang gnyis min dgra bcom pa'i/ /dgyes

pa'i 'dzum zhal bstan pa'i mod/ /sngon nas goms pa'i nyams rtogs kyi/ /sgo 'phar mtha' dag yangs por phyes/ /khyod kyis bzhed pa'i phrin las kun/ /ji lta'i tshul gyis bsgrub
bya zhes/ /bka' lung nod phyir chos srung dang / /nor lha'i tshogs kun lhags sam snyam/ /gang nas bltas kyang 'od zer gyis/ /mun sel nor bu rin chen bzhin/ /rnam thar gang
la brtags byas kyang / /legs pa nyid las gzhan du min/ /kye ma bsod nams chung rnams kyis/ /sangs rgyas sems can nyid du 'dzin/ /chu yang rnag khrag tu mthong ba'i/ yi
dwags rnams dang khyad par gang // //spyi don bdun pa tha mar gdul bya rtag 'dzin can rnams chos la bskul ba'i ched du gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos kyi dbyings su bsdus pa'i
tshul ni/ bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa gdul bya 'dul ba'i dus mkhyen cing thabs mkhas la thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa 'dis ni sku tshe rings por gdul bya so so'i
bsam pa dang mthun pa'i zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo rgyun chad med par bskor te/ sras kyi thu bo rnams ni smin cing grol te mtha' klas pa'i 'gro ba yongs
kyi 'dren pa dam par mnga' gsol/ 'ga' zhig ni ma 'ongs pa na 'gro ba 'dren pa'i nus pa dang ldan par mdzad/ gzhan yang sku mthong ba dang / gsung thos pa dang / mtshan
tsam yid la byed pa dang / sku'i grib ma phog pa tshun chad kyi sems can thams cad kyang phan pa dang bde ba 'ba' zhig la 'god par mdzad pa sogs mdor na sku dngos kyis gdul
bar 'os pa rnams ni legs par btul/ nges pa'i don gyi bstan pa rin po che'ang dar zhing rgyas par mdzad de/ da ni bdag cag skal ba dman pa rnams kyi bsod nams kyi bgo
skal ni re zhig

de tsam du zad pa dang / gdul bya rtag 'dzin can rnams chos la bskul ba'i ched du yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba chen po'i tshul ston par bzhed de/ de'ang spyir lo snga phyi
kun tu skar ma du ba 'jug rings kyis mtshon pa'i ltas ngan can gyi skar ma mang du shar ba sogs mi dge ba'i mtshan ma yang yang byung song ba/ de rnams ni spyir rje 'di'ang
yun ring mi bzhugs pa'i snga ltas dang / gzhan yang khams bod kun tu dus kyi 'khrugs longs mi bzad pa byung ba 'di rnams dang / de la brten nas bstan 'dzin gyi skyes
bu'ang 'ga' zhig zhing gzhan du gshegs pa dang / la la bsnyun pa'i tshul bstan pa sogs mang du snang ba 'di thams cad kyi ltas yin par sems la/ bye brag rje 'di dgung grangs
gya drug tu phebs pa lcags bya hor zla dang po'i lo gsar gyi dga' spro'i nyin/ rje rang gi thugs dam gyi rten 'jigs byed dang / las gshin bcas kyi sku so sor che chung
gi tshad khru gang tsam yod pa/ sku rgyu rdzi khyim du grags pa'i lugs sku shin tu lci ba zhig rje rang gi gzim chung gi rten khri'i nang na bzhugs yod pa lhung don med
cing / lhung mi shes pa lta bu yod kyang / rgyu rkyen ci'ang med par don med du rten khri'i nang nas phyi rol du lhung ste/ mdun gyi mchod pa'i yo byad 'ga' zhig kyang chag
grum du btang ba sogs byung ba ni nges par rje 'di zhing khams gzhan du gshegs pa'i ltas kho na yin par gor ma chag par ma zad/ de nyin sde dge'i bang chen zhig kyang
'byor pas/ rje rang gi zhal nas sde dge chos rgyal mchog gi bstan srid la nyag skeg gis 'tshe ba 'dra 'ong ba'i ltas min nam zhes bka' stsal pa'ang rjes su de kho na ltar
gyur pa sogs mdor na yon mchod gnyis char la ngan pa'i ltas zhig yin par gdon mi za ba dang / de rjes lo de'i sa ga zla ba'i

tshes nyer brgyad nas bzung ste/ thog mar mgul cham zhig gis nyen bslangs pa lta bus skyigs bu nyin mtshan bar ma chad par mdzad 'dug cing / de dang lhan cig sku mtshal dang
chab chu bsdongs te shin tu sku khams bsnyel ba'i tshul bstan cing / de la brten nas sman pa rnams kyis kyang gsol sman sgo gang zab nas phul ba dang / zhabs brtan kyang
e wa~M pa'i gtsug lag khang du 'dus tshogs kyis snga phyir tshe chog lan gsum tsam dang / gzhan yang zhabs brtan gyi rigs rgya gang che lta bu bsgrubs rung / sku khams
dwangs skyed kyi tshul cher mi bzhes par snang bas da lan ji 'drar 'gyur snyam pa'i thams cad kyi blo bag mi phebs pa lta bur gyur rung / hor zla lnga pa'i gral tshes bco
lnga'i nyin bdag cag dge slong bco lnga skor gyis bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag tu med pa'i cho ga dang 'brel bar sku tshe brtan bzhugs kyi gsol 'debs bgyis pas/ de nyin rje
rang yang thugs dgyes pa'i rnam pa mdzad cing / thams cad kyis mthong snang mthun par sku'i zhal mdangs dus rgyun bas legs shing zil che ba lta bur snang bas/ re zhig zhabs
pad brtan par gsol ba thebs pa 'dra snyam pa'i thams cad blo bde ba ltar gyur par ma zad/ don la'ang bdag sogs gdul bya mgon med pa dang / skyabs med pa dang / dpung gnyen
med pa rnams la thugs brtse bar dgongs te/ rim gyis sku khams je dwangs kyi tshul bzhes te dgung grangs gya bdun du phebs pa chu khyi hor zla dang po'i nang bar spyir
sku na smin pa'i stobs kyis sku gzugs babs lci ba dang / gsol chas la dwang ga cher mi snang ba ma gtogs de las gzhan pa'i snyun gzhi che rigs ci'ang med par zhabs pad
brtan par bzhugs pa ni nges par sku tshe byin gyis brlabs par gor ma chag

la/ tshul 'di lta bu ni 'phags pa nyan thos pa rnams bcom ldan 'das kyis yul yangs pa can du sku tshe byin gyis brlab pa'i phyir 'chi bdag gi bdud btul bar 'dod pa dang tshul
mtshungs pa yin no/ /de nas kyang skyes bu dam pa 'di yun ring por mi bzhugs pa'i snga ltas su/ lcags bya hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i 'jug tu thar rtse rang gis chos srung
rnams la skong ba brgya tshar tshogs pa'i skabs kyi tshes nyer brgyad nyer dgu rnams la dus ma yin pa'i rlung chen po ldang ba dang / dpal e wa~M chos ldan gyi chos grwa
'dir sngon ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen pos dam la btags pa yin skad kyi dgon pa'i nye skor du spyang ki sogs mi 'byung zhing / gal srid byung yang ltas ngan du 'dzin pa
zhig yod pa la/ 'di lo dgon pa'i nye skor du spyang ki rgyug pa dang / thar rtse rang gi pho brang dang nye ba'i sar wa brgyal ba dang / khyad par chu khyi hor zla dang
po'i nang e wa~M pa'i lam 'bras lha khang du bzhugs pa'i ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi 'dra sku rin po che'i zhal ras kyi ngos su spyan chab bsil ba'i rjes lta bu zhig 'dug
pa thog mar grwa pa gcig gis mthong zhing / de rjes thar rtse nas lam 'bras lha khang du bla mchod cig bgyis pa'i tshe der yod pa'i grwa pa brgyad tsam gyis mthong ba dang
/ de nas rim gyis thams cad kyis mngon sum du gyur cing spyan chab kyi rjes kyang de rjes yun ring du gnas pa dang / gzhan yang snga phyi ci rigs par phal che ba'i rmi
lam du nyi zla gzas 'dzin pa sogs byung zhes gleng ba dang / khams bod kun tu dus kyi 'khrugs long mi bzad pa 'byung ba'i mgo tshugs pa sogs mi dge ba'i mtshan ma mang po
mngon sum du lhags par gyur te/ de lta bu ni gang zag dam pa 'di zhing khams gzhan du gshegs par bzhed pas nag po'i phyogs kyi bdud dang bdud kyi ris su gtogs pa rnams

mgo 'degs shing / dkar po'i phyogs kyi lha dang srung mar bcas pa mtha' dag yid mi dga' zhing mya ngan gyi chu tshan snying gi dbus nas khol ba'i ltas dang / de la brten nas
phyogs 'dir rjes su brtse ba'i skyob pa rnams kyang thugs skyo ba'i tshul bstan par mngon la/ rnam pa gcig tu na/ skyes bu dam pa 'di lta bu 'jig rten du byon pa na de'i
bsod nams kyis 'jig rten thams cad bde bar 'tsho zhing / de nyid gzhan du gshegs pa na 'jig rten 'dir mi dge ba 'byung ba chos nyid yin te/ sngon rgyal po zla 'od kyi dbu
sbyin par gtong ba'i tshe/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi thams cad kyi mgo bo'i rgyan dus gcig tu sa la lhung zhing sa g.yos pa dang / skar mda' ltung ba dang / bkra mi shis
pa sna tshogs byung zhing / mi rnams kyang tshe'i dus byas nas lha'i gnas su skyes so zhes grags pa dang / bod 'dir yang 'jam pa'i dbyangs dngos chos kyi rgyal po khri srong
lde'u btsan 'das pa na lo nyes dang / 'khrugs long byung bar grags pa sogs mdor na gang zag dam pa phal che ba zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i tshe de ltar byung ba'i tshul
mang du bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /gzhan yang bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'di dus rgyun du'ang spyir mkhyen rab kyi klong che zhing / gsung sgros sogs kyang brjid chags
zhing yid du 'bab pa zhig yod par ma zad/ lhag par lcags bya lor sku bsnyun pa'i tshul bstan pa nas bzung sngar bas kyang gsung sgros rnams brjid chags shing / mkhyen
rab kyi klong yang cher song ba lta bur snang ba dang / mngon par shes pa'ang dus rgyun dang cung mi 'dra ba'i thogs pa med par snang ste/ rje rang gi zhabs 'bring bas rin
chen ril bu zhig zhus par/ sde dge bla chen byams pa kun dga' sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi

sku dus su bsdus pa'i ril bu de'i nang nas gcig longs gsungs pa ltar len par brtsams pa'i tshe kho rang gi bsam pa la/ sde dge blo gros rgya mtsho'i sku dus su bsdus pa'i ril
bu de nas gcig byung na snyam pa sems la shar ma thag /rje rang gi zhal nas nga la khyad par spu tsam yang med cing / khyod kyis blo gros rgya mtsho'i sku dus su bsdus
pa'i ril bu de la dga' bar byed kyin 'dug pas/ de nas rdog gcig longs zhes gsungs byung bas ji ltar mkhyen pa yin snyam pa lta bu'i ngo gnong ba zhig byung zer ba dang /
yang 'ga' zhig gis lkog tu byin rten 'dra zhu phod min zer ba'i skabs kyang / rje'i zhal nas de gar byin rten 'dra dgos zer mkhan mi 'dug gam gsungs pa sogs de 'dra'i rigs
mang ba dang / lcags bya hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bco lnga bcu drug gi skor zhig tu rje'i zhal nas/ mdo khams nas mchog sprul thams cad mkhyen pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang
po phran bu'i sku khams bde min 'dra byung med dam snyam pa 'dug cing / nged kyi rmi lam du'ang mchog sprul rin po che bzhugs gdan srab mo zhig la bzhugs 'dug pa'i snang
ba zhig byung bas/ de la dmigs pa'i zhabs brtan 'dra byed dgos zhes bka' stsal pa'ang rjes sor de kho na ltar byung snang ba dang / yang hor zla gsum pa 'di dus 'khor
ba'i lugs kyi lo mgo yin gshis nged kyi khams mi bde ba 'di'ang chu khyi hor zla gnyis pa'i mjug dang gsum pa'i nang bzang thag ngan thag chod pa zhig byung 'ong 'gro'am
snyam zhing / der skyon chen rang ma byung tshe da dung zla ba kha shas mi sdod pa'i nges pa med ces gsungs pa dang / yang chab chu'i bsnyun gzhi 'dras skyon mi 'ong ngam
snyam nas de la phan pa'i gsol sman 'dra phul ba'i tshe'ang sman de mi bza'/ nged spos skrangs dang chu'i skyon

gyis 'chi bar mi 'gyur zhes bka' stsal pa'ang rjes sor de kho na ltar gyur pa sogs lkog gyur gyi chos mtha' dag tshul bzhin mkhyen pa'i gsung mang du byon pa dang / sku khams
dngos ni chu khyi hor zla dang po'i nang gsol chas la dwang ga je zhan du song ba'i rkyen gyis sku rlung shas che ba tsam las bsnyun gzhi'i rigs che ba ci'ang mi snang
ba dang / zhabs brtan gyi rigs kyang de skabs rgyun chad med par gang lcogs sgrub mu yin rung / sku khams ni de mus las lhag tu dwangs skyed du mngon pa ci yang ma mchis
shing / zla ba de'i mjug tu gus phran pas/ skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang chen po'i sku khams skyon che ba rang ma byung tshe bdag gis mtshams zla ba gcig gnyis tsam sdod rgyu
dang / gal srid sku khams babs lci bar song ba sogs byung tshe de 'phral du mtshams grol ba gzhir bzhag yin tshul zhus par/ nges par mtshams sdod rgyu byas na legs tshul
dang / nged gzugs babs lci ba sogs byung tshe de 'phral khyod la bya gtong yong tshul dang / khyod rang yang dus rgyun du tshe sgrub 'dra la nan tan byas na legs tshul
sogs bka' stsal pa dang / gzhan yang de skabs shig tu gus phran la dngos po'i gsol ras 'dra stsal te skad cha zhib par rjes sor 'byung ba yin mod/ khyod kyis e wa~M pa'i
bstan pa la phan gang thogs byed dgos tshul dang / phyogs 'dir rig gnas 'dra'ang dar ba'i thabs gang drag byed dgos tshul bka' phebs par/ spyir gus phran rang la bstan pa
la phan 'dogs nus pa'i yon tan til 'bru tsam yang med pa ma gtogs/ gzhan bstan pa rin po che'i zhabs 'degs gang 'grub zhu ba bzhir bcas dang / khyad par skyabs mgon rdo
rje 'chang chen po mchog nyid bdag sogs gdul bya rnams kyi mgon skyabs dpung gnyen dam par

gsang gsum rin po che bskal brgya'i bar du 'tsho zhing gzhes la chos kyang ston pa dang / bdag kyang skye ba dang tshe rabs thams cad du thugs rje'i skyabs 'og tu tshud par
gsol ba btab pas/ da dung lo re gnyis 'dra sdod pa'i smon lam 'debs dgos zhes bka' stsal byung yang de ni bdag gi sems 'khri ba'i phyir gsungs par gor ma chag la/ de rjes
hor zla gnyis pa'i nang du'ang res nyin lnga drug re la gsol chas la dwang ga skyon med tsam yod pa dang / res nyin lnga drug re la gsol chas la dwang ga gtan nas med pa
lta bu res 'jog gi tshul du snang zhing / khyad par zla ba de'i mjug nas bzung gsol chas la dwang ga je zhan du song zhing / sku gzugs kyang babs je lcir 'gro ba lta bur
snang bas/ hor zla gsum pa'i tshes mgor bdag kyang mtshams grol te sku mdun du bcar bas/ sku shed zhan pa'i stobs kyis gsung sgros sogs mdzad pa la 'o brgyal ba zhig 'dug
pa ma gtogs gzhan gsung sgros dang / thugs rab sogs sngar rgyun ltar mchis shing / de skabs tshe lha gsum gyi cho ga la sogs pa'i zhabs brtan kyang ci rigs par bsgrubs
mod/ rje rang ni zhabs brtan rim gro'i rigs la thugs 'dun gtan nas mi mdzad cing / zhal nas kyang / khyed rnams kyis lo snga mar rim gro gang 'grub byas pa la brten nas
nged da bar bsdad pa yin mod/ da ni rim gro byas nas kyang khyed rang rnams kyang dka' tshegs kyi rgyu kho na dang / nged kyang da na so rgas ches pas gzhan don byed pa phar
zhog /rang don du kha ton yang grul btub pa zhig mi thub pa'i lus rten 'di lta bu bsdad pa bas shi ba legs/ da lus rten 'di bor nas lus rten gsar pa 'dra

blangs na des dga' bar 'dug kho na gsungs pa dang / zla ba de'i tshes brgyad kyi nyin byis pa dpe cha shes pa 'ga' zhig la chos spyod dang bla mchod la blo gso gyis/ zla ba
'di'i tshes bcu bzhi tsam nas bla mchod 'dra 'don dgos zhes bka' stsal song ba ni bdag cag rmongs pa rnams la brda thabs zhig mdzad par mngon mod/ phyis su go ba tsam dang
/ gzhan yang de skabs rnams su thugs dam gtor ma 'di rnams brje dgos zhes yang yang gsung ba dang / khyad par tshes bcu gnyis kyi nyin dge bshes bsod nams bzang po la/
khyod kyis nga'i thugs dam gtor ma 'di rnams gsar du bzo dgos/ de'ang gnang nyin tshes bcu bzhi chos skyong gi dus chen la gtor ma rnams nges par bshams thub pa zhig dgos/
da nged nad 'di las thar bar mi 'dra na'ang / ma shi gong du gtor ma 'di rnams ma brjes pa'i thabs med ces bka' stsal song ba ltar de ma thag nas gtor ma'i rgyan rnams
bzo ba'i mgo btsugs shing / tshes bcu gnyis bcu gsum gnyis la sku khams kyang cung zad nyog tu song snang zhing / de dag gi bar bar gyi thugs rab gsal ba'i skabs rnams su/
/sbyor lam rtse mo thob pa'i rtags su lus la srin bu'i rigs med pa dang / sbyor lam bzod pa thob nas ngan song du mi 'gro bar bshad pa dang / gzhan yang sbyor lam de dag
thob pa'i rtags su ji 'dra bshad pa yod ces yang yang bka' 'dri stsal 'dug par/ bdag gis de skor gyi mngon rtogs rgyan gyi 'grel pa ldeb re gnyis 'dra gzigs rtogs phul
bas/ de la'ang zhib par gzigs pa sogs nan tan lta bur mdzad 'dug pa ni/ sbyor lam de dag gang rung zhig thob par zhal gyis

bzhes par sems la/ gzhan yang chos kyi bgro gleng 'dra'ang ci rigs par mdzad pa dang / de rjes tshes bcu gsum gyi nub mo shin tu sku bsnyel ba zhig byung song zhing / khyad
par tshes bcu bzhi'i snga dro nyi ma rtse shar tsam na sku lus la sra bzung rgyu med cing / gsung sgros stsal ba rnams kyang cher mi go ba dang / phyag rtsa'ang gtan nas
med pa lta bur snang bas/ bdag cag rnams ni ci bya gtol med du gyur te/ kye ma da ni bdag cag skal med rnams kyi bsod nams kyis mi 'chun par thag chod do snyam pa shar zhing
/ bdag gis skyabs rje rdo rje 'chang chen po da dung yang zhabs pad yun ring du brtan par gsol ba 'debs pa lags mod/ 'on kyang mjal yul dang / bsnyun gzhi sogs gang
nas brtags kyang yun ring mi bzhugs par thag chod pa lta bur snang bas/ da cha bdag cag rnams kyis rjes kyi bya ba ji ltar bgyi/ thugs dam la yun ji tsam bzhugs/ slar yang
bdag cag 'gro ba rnams kyi mgon du sprul pa'i 'dzum zhal myur du ston pa dang / bdag cag 'khor dang bcas pa rnams kyang tshe rabs kun tu rjes su 'dzin par gsol ba btab
pas/ gsung sgros gsung pa la shin tu sku bsnyel ba zhig 'dug na'ang thugs rus kyi rnam pas/ nged kyis de sngon e wa~M pa'i bstan pa 'di shin tu dar ba zhig byung na snyam
nas mchog sprul thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po e wa~M du gdan drangs pa sogs byas pa yin cing / de la brten nas bstan pa cung zhig dar bar
gyur na'ang / snyigs dus su song bas ha cang bstan pa dar zhing rgyas pa zhig mi yong 'dug /da cha e waM pa'i bstan pa 'di khyod kyi lag tu bzhag pa yin pas sgo du ma nas
dar ba'i thabs gang drag byed dgos tshul rgyu mtshan dang bcas pa dang / de sngon nged rang gi tshe la dkon mchog la mchod pa dang / dge 'dun la bsnyen bkur ba

sogs ci 'grub byas pa yin zhing / da cha des ma 'thus pa'i rjes kyi bya ba rgya chen ci'ang mi dgos pa'i tshul dang / ji ltar bya ba'i tshul rnams ni khyod rang gis babs bltas
byas pas chog tshul dang / thugs dam yang zhag bcu skor tsam dgos pa e yin snyam pa dang / phyin chad skye ba 'dra'ang len pa'i smon lam 'debs dgos tshul dang / 'on kyang
skad cha zhib par rjes sor 'byung zhing / da dung gzhan yang re gnyis dran pa byung tshe rjes su mngags dam bya dgos tshul bka' phebs par/ bdag gis deng skabs nam dus
'di'ang shin tu dro bar 'dug pas thugs dam de yun ji tsam zhig legs zhus kyang / de la bka' lan dmigs bsal ci'ang stsal ma byung zhing / de nas da lta nged rig pa shin
tu 'thibs pa zhig 'dug pas cung zad cig 'dir bsdad nas/ de nas gzim chung rnam rgyal pho brang du 'gro dgos gsungs pa la/ bdag gis cung phebs e thub ces zhus par/ nged 'chi
sa de rnam rgyal pho brang du legs par 'dug gsungs byung zhing / de nas gsung sgros kyang bka' stsal rgyu med pa lta bur da ni zhi bar gshegs sam snyam pa lta bur snang
zhing / sku 'khor ba thams cad ni mya ngan gyi gong bur gyur 'dug pa la/ bdag gis bla ma la gsol ba 'debs nus na thugs rje la nye ring med tshul 'dra gleng ba dang / de
nas gzim chung rnam rgyal pho brang du gdan drangs te bzhugs su gsol zhing / sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung zhig zhal du gsol rung ci'ang mi mkhyen pa lta bur snang la/ de
rjes yun cung zad cig nas thugs je dwangs su gyur te nyin phyed ma zin tsam na thugs rab shin tu gsal zhing / phyag rtsa'ang sor chud par gyur la/ de nas bdag la bshad ma
thag pa'i snga dro bka' stsal pa rnams yang bskyar kyi tshul du shin tu rgyas pa rgyu mtshan dang bcas pa dang / nged na sa dang

'chi sa thams cad lha khang gi nang du byas pa 'di shin tu blo 'tsher ba zhig 'dug pas de'i sgrib sbyong lta bur ltung bshags dang / gnas brtan bcu drug gi zhal thang re bzhengs
rgyu yin pa la/ de'i nang nas ltung bshags ni khar seng nas bzhengs tshar ba yin cing / da gnas bcu'i zhal thang zhig nges par bzhengs dgos pa dang / e waM pa'i gtsug
lag khang du yod pa'i gshed dmar lha lnga'i dkyil thang de shin tu bgres por song snang bas/ gshed dmar gyi dkyil thang zhig gsar du bzhengs nas sbyor 'jags bya dgos pa
dang / bde mchog lU nag dril gsum gyi mtshams tshad ldan re gzhag dgos snyam pa'i nang nas/ nag dril gnyis kyi mtshams de sngon bzhag tshar ba yin zhing / da lU hi pa'i
mtshams zhig nges par gzhag dgos tshul dang / gzhan rjes kyi bya ba rgya chen ci'ang mi dgos pa'i tshul bka' stsal byung zhing / de nas thugs dam gtor ma rnams kyang bzos
tshar nas der slebs byung ba la/ rje rang gis zhib par gzigs nas/ gtor ma'i rgyan gyi me tog la sogs pa gang ci nas shin tu legs par byung 'dug ces gsungs shing thugs mnyes
mnyes mdzad pa dang / de ring nged kyi gtor gzhi spos pa'i dga' ston yin pas mkhan rin po che rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po'i dbu byas pa'i 'dir yod thams cad la 'phar
ja dang / 'bras sil re bzos gsungs pa'ang de kho na ltar bgyis pa dang / de nas bdag la thog mar 'dir grwa pa zhig gis lam dus dang / gtor bsngo 'don pa sogs bgyis kyang
rten 'brel 'dra la'ang cung mi btub pa 'dra bas/ khyod kyis de ring nas bzung zhag bdun gyi bar la gnas khang 'dir lam dus dang gtor bsngo rnams ma chag par gyis/ de nas
grwa pa 'dra la 'don du bcug pas chog ces

bka' stsal byung ba ltar gus phran nas kyang de bzhin du bgyis pa dang / de nas sde srid sangs rgyas rgya mtshos mdzad pa'i bai dkar gyi dris lan 'khrul snang g.ya' sel zhes
sde dge'i spar ma pod gnyis yod pa de khyer shog gsungs pa ltar phul bas/ de'i nang du cig 'tshol bar mdzad kyin 'dug pa la bdag gis btsal na zhus par/ 'o na pod dang po
de'i ldeb nyis brgya bcu drug bcu bdun skor zhig tu yod snyam pas de longs gsungs pa ltar blangs pas/ de na 'byung ba rags pa thim tshul dang / phra ba snang mched thob
gsum la sogs pa'i bshad pa 'dra 'dug pas de la zhib par gzigs song ba dang / de nub kyang sku khams skyon med tsam du snang zhing / de'i phyi nyin tshes bco lngar yang sku
khams de mus su mchis pa dang / de ring tshes bco lnga yin pas sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung zhig gsol dgos tshul gsungs pa ltar phul pas thugs smon dang bcas te gsol song
ba dang / gzhan yang thog mar sku bsnyun pa'i tshul bstan pa nas bzung ste dus thams cad du thugs rig cung zad re 'thibs par gyur pa na/ de 'phral res 'ga' yi dam la gtor
ma 'bul tshul dang / res 'ga' ma rgyud pa'i lugs kyi tsham rngams sngags kyis bsrung ba'i tshul la sogs pa'i phyag rgya 'dra rtag tu mdzad 'dug pa dang / bco lnga'i nub
mo sku khams kyang je lcir song ba dang / da nged 'di ltar sdod pa yin gsungs shing zhabs skyil krung dang / sku gzugs drang por bsrangs te bzhugs song ba dang / gsol
chas kyi rigs la dwang ga gtan nas ma mchis na'ang / bdag cag rnams kyi blos mi bzod pa lta bu'i gsol ja dang bzhes 'jam 'dra bteg kyang / da nged ting nge 'dzin bsgom pa
la bsam gtan gyi zas bza' ba yin mod/ kha zas kyis dgos pa med lta bu gsal por rang

min pa zhig bka' stsal byung ba ni gsung sgros kyi tha ma yin la/ de nas bzung gsung sgros gtan nas mi mdzad par 'dug cing / de'i mtshan mo dang / phyi nyin tshes bcu drug
bcas su'ang sku gzugs drang por bzhugs 'dug pa dang / de nyin e waM pa'i lho pa khang tshan gyi grwa pa zhig phyogs gzhan zhig nas tshur 'ongs pa'i mthong snang du/ dgon
pa 'di sprin lta bu'i 'od dkar po zhig gis gtums 'dug pa'i 'ja' sne lho nub ngos su song ba zhig 'dug zer ba thos pa dang / gzhan yang de skabs rnams su chu 'dus sogs yul
phyogs gzhan du'ang 'ja' sprin mtha' yas pa ngor gyi phyogs su 'gro bar snang bas phal cher gyis ci yin nam zer zhing / rgyus yod 'dras rje 'di zhabs pad brtan min 'dra
byung ba min nam zhes phan tshun gleng ba byung zhes gzur gnas 'ga' re'i ngag las rjes su thos shing / bdag cag rnams ni mya ngan gyis non te ci bya gtol med du gyur rung
/ rje rang la gsol ba 'debs pa dang / da dung yang sku rim phran phran 'dra bsgrubs pa las gzhan pa'i thabs zad pa dang / de'i phyi nyin tshes bcu bdun gyi snga dro e waM
pa'i gtsug lag khang du dge 'dun rnams tshogs pa'i tshe/ rgyab ri'i ngos su 'ja' kha dog lnga ldan zhig zug pa grwa pa gcig gis mthong 'dug ces zer la/ de nas nyi ma rtse
shar tsam na/ rje rang gis phyag mdzub nam mkha' la bstan cing / sku 'khor ba rnams la 'dir ma sdod ces pa'i brda lta bu mdzad cing / de nas yun cung zad cig nas rlung
phyir lan gsum 'bud par mdzad pa'i rjes su ljags dbugs mi snang bas/ bdag gis da ni zhi bar gshegs pa lags pas thugs dam rigs la mi lhod par zhu zhes lan gsum tsam zhus
pas/ phran bu'i dbu gug tsam zhig mdzad/ mdor na dgung grangs gya bdun du phebs

pa chu khyi hor zla gsum pa nyis brtsegs kyi gsum pa snga ma'i tshes bcu bdun res gza' lhag pa dang / skar ma sa ri 'dzom pa'i nyi dros sbrul gyi steng du gzugs sku'i bkod
pa chos kyi dbyings su bsdus shing / nyi zla'i rlung dang byang sems kyi stobs thams cad rtsa a ba dhU ti'i nang du bsdus te rnam kun mchog ldan gyi stong pa nyid dang /
mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i bde ba chen po zung du 'jug pa'i 'od gsal phyag rgya chen po'i ngang du mnyam par bzhag pa'i tshul bstan par gyur to/ /de'i tshe nam mkha'i phyogs
bzhi nas sprin dkar po snam bu brkyangs pa lta bu bzhi nar gyis byung ste rje 'di'i gzim chung gi steng ngos kyi nam mkhar 'dus shing / de nas phyogs thams cad nas sprin
mchod pa'i gzugs brnyan can mang po nang du 'du ba zhig 'dug ces grwa pa kha cig gis zer ba dang / yang grwa pa kha shas kyis ni 'ja' kha dog lnga ldan rtsa ba gcig pa lhor
bstan cing / rtse mo mang por gyes pa byang ngos su bstan pa zhig shar song zer ba dang / yang bya bral ba kha cig gis ni 'ja' kha dog lnga ldan ring thung gsum shar song
zer zhing / bdag cag gis zur tsam mthong ba la ni sprin mchod pa'i gzugs brnyan can mang po phyogs thams cad nas nang du lhags pa zhig ni nges par 'dug cing / gang ltar
yang bdag cag rnams ni mas bu bor ba bzhin du sdug bsngal drag pos non par gyur rung / bla ma'i thugs rje la ni nye ring med pa dang / byin rlabs la 'du 'bral med pa kho
na rgyu mtshan du byas nas rang gis rang la sems gso bgyi ba dang / rje rang la gsol ba rtse gcig tu 'debs pa las gzhan pa'i thabs zad cing / de ma thag nas bzung bdag
cag dge slong bzhis thugs dam ma grol gyi bar du rje rang gis dus rgyun du gsungs pa'i yi dam gyi lha'i sgrub thabs rnams dang / gtor bsngo

dang bcas pa nyin re bzhin thun gnyis su bcad nas nyams su blangs pa dang / zhi bar gshegs pa nas bzung thugs dam ma grol gyi bar la sku'i gzi mdangs dus rgyun pas legs shing
/ sku sha dkar ba dang / zhal ras kyi ngos su gnyer ma'ang cher med pa'i gzhon sha chags par mchis shing / de nas zla ba de'i tshes bcu dgu'i nub mo bdag gi rmi lam du'ang
/ rje rang nyid bsnyun gzhi las grol ba'i snang ba za zi 'dra byung ba dang / rje 'di'i zhal slob hor nyag brag sprul sku'i mnal lam du'ang / rje 'di thugs dam las grol
te phyag na bum pa zhig bsnams te dbang bskur ba'i snang ba byung zhes gsungs shing / gang ltar yang tshes nyi shu'i nam ma langs tsam nas bzung ste de nyin nam mkha'
thams cad kha dog sna tshogs pa'i 'ja' sprin gyis gang ba dang / nyi gur phub pa sogs thams cad la mngon sum du snang bas/ dgon pa'i grwa pa phal che bas kyang de ring thugs
dam las grol ba gdon mi za zhes gleng ba byung zhing / mtshams pa kha cig gis ni 'ja' kha dog lnga ldan shin tu gsal ba ring thung gsum shar 'dug ces zer zhing / gang
ltar yang nyi ma phyed yol tsam na thugs dam las grol ba'i rtags sngar gyi zhal mdangs glo bur ba de yal ba dang / dbu mdun du cung zad gug pa dang / shangs bug g.yas nas
byang sems dmar po nar tsam zhig babs 'dug pas/ slar yang 'od gsal las zung 'jug gi skur bzhengs te/ dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa ganggA'i klung gi
bye ma snyed kyi grangs dang mnyam pa rnams kyis mchod pa'i khyad par sna tshogs pas mchod cing / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs dpag tu med pa rnams kyis
bkra shis pa'i cho ga dang bcas pa'i

sgo nas mchog gi grong khyer du gshegs te rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ye shes kyi sku mngon sum mdzad par gdon mi za'o/ /sngar tshes bcu bzhi'i nyin bdag la gnas khang 'dir lam dus
dang gtor bsngo zhag bdun gyis zhes bka' stsal pa'i zhag bdun yang tshes nyi shu'i nyin rdzogs 'gro bar snang bas/ de'ang ma 'ongs lung ston pa'i gsung du mngon no/ /de nas
sgrub thabs rin chen 'bar ba las/ rang nyid lha yi rnal 'byor las/ /bdud rtsi 'khyil ba bzlas pa yi/ /dri zhim chu yis dang por bkru/ /rnam snang mdzad du de bsams nas/
/zhes gsungs pa ltar tshes nyi shu'i nub mo dang / tshes nyer gcig gi tho rangs bcas su bdag cag kha shas kyis dpal kye rdo rje bdag gi rnal 'byor sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo
nas/ las thams cad pa'i bum pa tshul bzhin du bsgrubs shing / de nas tshes nyer gcig gi nyi ma rtse shar tsam na sku gdung rin po cher na bza' bzang po dang bcas te bzhugs
khri'i khar bzhugs su gsol nas/ dad pa can thams cad la mjal kha btang ste gsol ba dang smon lam 'debs su bcug pa dang / de nas grwa pa kha cig gis gzim chung gzhan zhig
tu dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi thig btab cing / bdag cag kha shas kyis nyi dros phyi ma tsam na 'jig rten kun gyi mchod sdong bla na med pa'i sku gdung rin po
cher gong du bsgrubs pa'i bum pa'i chus sku khrus legs par gsol zhing / de nas kyang ji skad du dpal kye rdo rje'i rtsa ba'i rgyud rgyas pa las/ sku gsung thugs kyi rig sngags
gdags/ /rang gi lha'am gzhan yang rung / /snying po snying gar gdags par bya/ /khrus kyis dag byas bdud rtsis byug /ces 'byung ngo zhes slob dpon bram ze nag po zhabs
kyi gzhung las gsungs pa ltar sku gsung thugs

kyi sa bon dang / dpal dges pa rdo rje'i rtsa sngags dang / snying po dang / nye snying rnams gog pu la bris shing dri bzang bas byugs pa rnams gnas gsum du sbyar ba dang /
dri bzang po dang / bsil sman sna tshogs pa lhan cig tu sbyar ba'i lde gus yongs su byugs shing / ras ser po mang pos legs par dkris pa dang / dbu rgyan dang / stod g.yogs
smad g.yogs la sogs pa'i lha rdzas kyi na bzas mdzes par spras te/ dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gang du bzhengs pa'i gnas kyi gzim chung du spyan drangs te/ spos mar
me zhal zas rnams re re nas brgya phrag lnga tsam dang bcas pa'i mchod pa'i bye brag mtha' yas dbus su gdung sgrom gyi bzhugs khri'i steng du bzhugs su gsol lo/ /de nas
bdag cag dge slong bcus sku gdung rin po che rnam snang dges pa rdo rjer yan lag bzhi rdzogs su bskyed de bzlas pa bya ba sogs rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i kye rdor dus
tha'i cho ga gzhan phan bdud rtsi sogs nas ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bgyis so/ /de'i tshe'ang gdung khrus dang por gsol ba dang mnyam du nam mkhar sprin gyi phung po glo
bur du 'dus te/ /gnam lo 'dir de sngon 'brug skad grag pa gtan nas ma thos pas/ de nyin 'brug skad thog ma'i tshul du shin tu gsal ba lan gnyis bsgrags shing / me tog gi
dbyibs lta bu yod pa'i gangs zim bu sa gzhi mdog 'gyur tsam du babs pa dang / de nas sku gdung rin po cher chas 'bul grub la nye ba na/ nyi ma shin tu dro zhing nyi gur
phub pa dang / 'ja' sprin thar thor 'dra' bshar bas skye bo thams cad ngo mtshar ba'i gnas la bkod par gyur to/ /de nub bdag cag dge slong bcus dpal kye rdo rje sta gon gyi
cho ga bgyis pa nas bzung / zhag zhe dgu'i bar du dge slong bcus dpal kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te sgrub cing

mchod pa dang / bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba la sogs pa nyin rer cho ga tshar re ma chag par bgyis pa dang / rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i dus tha'i cho ga gzhan phan
bdud rtsi las/ bdun phrag re re song ba dang dkyil 'khor gyi lha la gsol ba gdab cing dngos grub blangs te gshegs su gsol lo/ /rdul tshon phyags te chu bor dor ba la
sogs pa 'jug gi bya ba rdzogs par bya'o/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa ltar bdun phrag re re rdzogs pa'i mthar rdul chen gyi dkyil 'khor gshegs su gsol zhing / slar thig btab ste
sta gon bya ba sogs tshul bzhin du bgyis pa dang / dus tha'i cho ga dngos ni sngon gyi bla ma gong ma rnams kyis gang zag mchog la ji ltar bya ba'i tshul mang du bshad snang
bas/ de ltar byas kyang phun sum tshogs pa'i yan lag tu 'gyur ram snyam nas thog mar bdun phrag gnyis kyi bar la sku gdung rin po che rnam par snang mdzad kye rdo rjer
bskyed cing / ye shes pa gzhug pa sogs bgyis pa dang / dbang bskur ba ni rje btsun rin po che'i gzhan phan bdud rtsi las/ bla ma'am gang zag mchog la byed na/ dbang la
sogs pa len mkhan ni gang zag mchog de yin la/ dbang skur mkhan ni dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo la sogs pa sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs rnams yin zhing / bdag
gis bla ma'i zhabs tog byed par dmigs na bsod nams mchog tu 'gyur gyis/ gzhan du na bdag slob dpon lta bur bsgoms na ni bdag nyid la nyes par 'gyur ro/ /des na bdag g.yog
gam/ zhabs tog byed par bsam pa gal che'o/ /zhes bka' stsal pa ltar/ dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bos dbang rnams phul bar bsams te/ dbang tshig rnams bdag gis brjod pa dang /
maNDal 'bul ba dang / dbang rdzas 'bul ba sogs

las kyi rdo rje'i bya ba thams cad bdag gis bgyis te/ mdor na bdun phrag gnyis kyi bar la/ dus tha'i cho ga dbang dang bcas pa'i zhabs tog bgyis pa dang / bdun gsum pa man
chad la dus tha'i cho ga dang / dbang sogs kyi spros pa ci'ang ma byas par bla ma dang dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo dbyer med du dmigs te/ bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba kho
na bgyis pa yin la/ bdun phrag bdun pa'i dkyil 'khor gshegs gsol gyi nyin dpa' bo'i ston mo'am tshogs 'khor du grags pa dang / rdul tshon chu bor spyan 'dren pa dang /
gtor 'bul la sogs pa cho ga mtha' rgyas kyi tshul du bgyis pa dang / de'ang bdun phrag gnyis la bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nges pa don gyi rdo rje 'chang mkhan
rin po che rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po tshogs kyi rdo rje slob dpon chen por phebs shing / de 'phros thams cad la bdag gis rdo rje slob dpon gyi khul bgyis pa dang / de
thams cad la'ang nyin re bzhin dge slong re la phyag 'gyed dngul zho re phul ba sogs bsnyen bkur zhabs tog zab par bgyis pa dang / gzhan yang thog mar thugs dam grol ba
nas bzung / sku gdung rin po cher zhugs ma phul gyi bar du nyin re bzhin spos mar me zhal zas rnams re re nas brgya phrag gnyis gsum re ma chag par phul ba dang / de nas
kyang dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor la nyin re bzhin rnam gsum brgya mchod re ma chad par phul ba dang / yang zhi bar gshegs pa'i phyi nyin tshes bco brgyad nas bzung ste/
dgung zhag zhe dgu ma rdzogs kyi bar zhag lnga bcu nga gsum la nyin re bzhin dge slong bcus snga dro bdag bskyed bsnyen rgyas dang 'brel pa'i dpal kun tu rig pa'i ras
bris kyi dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i cho ga dang / phyi dro bdag bskyed

rdo rje sems dpa' dang 'brel ba'i kun rig gi cho ga re ste tshar gnyis gnyis ma chad par bgyis pa dang / de'ang bla ma dang dkyila'akhor gyi gtso bo dbyer med du dmigs te bdag
nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba kho na bgyis pa yin la/ khyad par bdun tshigs re re rdzogs nyin dge tshogs byang chub tu bsngo ba'i phyir/ tshogs kyi rdo rje slob dpon
du bla ma re re gdan zhus dang 'brel bar dge slong nyi shu res kun rig gi cho ga tshar gnyis re bgyis pa dang / de thams cad la'ang nyin re bzhin mchod pa shin tu rgyas pa
dang / grwa pa re la nyin rer phyag 'gyed dngul zho re phul ba sogs bsnyen bkur zab pa dang / yang bdun tshigs re re'i mtshams su dge slong bzhi res rje btsun rdo rje rnal
'byor ma'i siddhu ra'i dkyil 'khor bzhengs te sgrub cing mchod pa dang / bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba sogs bgyis pa dang / yang e waM pa'i lam 'bras lha khang sogs
dang / rje rang gi gzim chung khag bcas su re mos kyis nyin re bzhin brgya mchod re dang bcas te dge slong bcu skor res snga phyir bla ma mchod pa nyin nyi shu skor bgyis
pa dang / de dag so sor grwa pa re la nyin rer yon 'bul dngul zho re dang bcas pa'i bsnyen bkur zab pa dang / thugs dam grol ba nas bzung rim gyis e waM bla brang gzhung
du mkhan rin po che khri thog pa ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi mdun du skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi dgongs pa chos dbyings su rdzogs pa'i ljags bsngo
thugs smon zhu mtshon lha gos/ rdor dril/ gos chen gyi stod rtse spus legs/ chung ja 'khor drug gcig bcas phul ba dang / de bzhin du klu ldings zhabs drung rin po che
byams pa tshul khrims phun tshogs pa dang / khang gsar zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang blo gros snying po bcas so so'i mdun du'ang ljags bsngo zhu mtshon gyi 'bul ba gong
mtshungs

re phul ba dang / bla brang phan bde khang gsar du mkhan rin po che dang zhabs drung gnyis ka de skabs khams su phebs nas bzhugs med kyang / de dag gi 'bul skal dang mchod
thebs kyi zhabs 'debs bcas su ston pa'i gser sku/ rdo dril dang / rgya rol cha/ dngul ting bdun tshar/ ras lhwam/ chung ja 'khor gnyis bcas phul ba dang / bdun tshigs dang
po rdzogs nyin kun rig gi rdo rje slob dpon du klu ldings zhabs drung rin po che byams pa tshul khrims phun tshogs pa gdan zhus kyi 'bul bar gser zangs kyi sgrol dkar/
zangs bum dngul kham kha rgyan dang bcas pa cha gcig /rgya rol cha/ dngul gyi ting phor bdun tshar/ gos chen gyi stod 'bogs/ sku ber/ zhabs lhwam 'ja' chen/ phying khra/
ljon ja 'khor drug gcig /'bras do sogs phul ba dang / bdun tshigs gnyis pa rdzogs nyin khang sar zhabs drung rin po che ngag dbang blo gros snying po gdan zhus kyi 'bul bar
gser zangs kyi jo bo/ ting shags dngul thag can/ rgya rol cha/ dngul gyi ting phor bdun tshar/ dngul gyi mchod kong / zangs bum dngul kham kha rgyan dang bcas pa cha/
gos chen gyi stod 'bogs/ gos sgrim gser gyi mtha' lcags can gyi sku gzan/ gos chen gyi zhabs lhwam 'ja' chen/ sa gdan/ ljon ja 'khor drug gcig /'bras ltang bcas phul ba dang
/ bdun tshigs gsum pa dang / bzhi pa dang / lnga pa rnams su khang ser dpon slob rin po che dang / dpon slob las thog pa dang / phu mgo sprul sku bcas gdan zhus kyis
so sor rdor dril dang / phrug gzan dang / ljon ja 'khor re re bcas phul ba dang / bdun drug par lung rig smra ba sprul sku shes rab rgya mtsho bar yang 'bul ba gang 'os dang
/ bdun tshigs bdun pa rdzogs nyin gyi tshogs

dbur mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po phebs te dge tshogs byang chub tu bsngo ba sogs cho ga mtha' rgyas su mdzad pa dang / e waM pa'i gtsug lag khang
du'ang nyin re bzhin brgya mchod re dang bcas te dge 'dun gang yod kyis kun rig gi cho ga nyin bdun dang / bla mchod nyin gnyis bcas tshogs pa'i thog mar/ nyin bzhi la
dge slong re la nyin re bzhin phyag 'gyed dngul Tam phyed re phul ba dang / de rjes nyin lnga la nyin re bzhin grwa pa nyi shu la phyag 'gyed ljon ja brgyad pa sbag re phul
ba dang / de dag gi dge rtsa thams cad byang chub snying por bsngo ba'i slad du mkhan rin po che khri thog pa tshogs bsngo lan gnyis gdan zhus kyi 'bul bar ljon ja 'khor
drug gsum/ gos chen bcas phul ba dang / dpon slob las thog par yang tshogs bsngo zhu rten snga phyir lan gsum tsam phul ba dang / de rjes sa ga zla ba'i nang e waM pa'i
gtsug lag khang du dge 'dun gang yod kyis ngor lugs dkyil 'khor lnga'i sgrub mchod tshogs pa'i skabs kyang / 'phar ma nyin gcig gtsugs te/ de'ang rten gyi drung du brgya
mchod gnyis dang / dkyil 'khor so sor mchod pa dang / dge 'dun rnams la mang ja'i bsnyen bkur ba sogs zab pa dang / snga tshogs su grwa pa bcu re la phyag 'gyed ljon ja
brgyad pa sbag re dang / phyi tshogs su grwa pa re la phyag 'gyed dngul Tam re dang / dar gyi tshab ra bcas phul ba dang / de nyin mkhan rin po che khri thog pa tshogs kyi
rdo rje slob dpon du phebs pa'i 'bul ba dar ras gos chen mgo snam la sogs pa'i tshan grangs mang po/ ljon ja 'khor drug gnyis/ shing thog /'bras dos sogs zab par phul
ba dang / dpon slob dang / zur bzhi slob dpon bzhi dang / chos khrims sogs su rnam gzhag gang zab bcas phul ba dang / tshur yang snga phyir e waM pa'i bla brang khag rnams
dang / thar rtse rang gi grwa tshang dang / ltos rigs

rnams nas gdung 'bul byung ba thams cad kyang gong 'og gi dge tshogs rnams su smin nges zhus pa dang / gzhan yang bkras lhun du paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i mchog sprul rin
po che'i mdun ljags bsngo zhu rten dang / chibs pa sga 'byar spus legs dang / ljon ja 'khor drug gnyis dang / dngul Tam srang bco lnga bcas phul ba dang / dgon de'i lha
khang khag thams cad la mchod 'bul shin tu zab pa dang / yongs 'dzin rin po che/ sngags chen/ zur bzhi bcas kyi bla ma so sor ljags bsngo zhu mtshon gyi 'bul ba dang /
tshogs chen la mang ja dang / de'i nang gses khron sbug mi tshan la mang ja bcas zab pa dang / khyad par bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal sa skya'i chos grwa chen por khri chen
thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang bkra shis rin chen gyi spyan sngar ljags bsngo zhu mtshon gyi 'bul bar/ dar gos chen la sogs pa'i tshan grangs/ gser zangs las grub pa'i sangs
rgyas mar me mdzad/ rdo dril/ dngul gyi bum pa kha rgyan bcas pa/ dngul Tam srang bco lnga/ ljon ja 'khor gnyis bcas dang / 'jam mgon dngos grub dpal 'bar/ ngag dbang
rdo rje rin chen/ gdung sras kun dga' bsod nams bcas so so'i mdun du gser zangs las grub pa'i sku 'dra re dang / rdo dril/ sil snyan/ dngul Tam srang lnga re/ ja brgyad
pa 'khor drug re re bcas phul ba dang / gdung sras sku chung ba gnyis so sor rdo dril/ bzang ja spag gnyis re/ dngul Tam srang gsum re bcas phul ba dang / rje btsun ma bgres
gzhon yod do cog dang / lha khang mkhan rin po che bcas su bsngo zhus kyi 'bul ba dang / chos grwa chen po der bzhugs pa'i rten gsum ngo mtshar can so so'i mdun du brgya
mchod dang / mgon khang khag rnams su sa lam gyi bar chad zhi zhing thugs bzhed lhun gyis grub pa'i phyir chos srung rnams la skong phrin dang / dge 'dun 'dus pa rgya

mtshor mang ja'i bsnyen bkur bcas bsgrubs pa dang / zhwa lu ri sbug mchog sprul rdo rje 'chang chen po'i spyan sngar ljags bsngo zhu mtshon dngul Tam srang lnga dang / ljon
ja 'khor drug gcig bcas dang / zhwa lu ri mthil gyi slob dpon rnams su bsngo zhus dang / dgon par mang ja'i bsnyen bkur/ gzhan yang rgyal rtse dpal 'khor chos sde dang /
de'i nang gses gur pa gra tshang pa/ nyang stong skyid sbug gi sgrub sde/ theg mchog gling / dga' ba gdong / snar thang / byang chen sgrub ste/ gangs can chos sde/ gnas
chos sde/ khro phu/ gnas phur mo chos rdzong gi sgrub sde khag /lhun po rtse/ rab brtan chos lung gi sgrub ste/ byang chub gling gi sgrub sde stod smad/ 'dar chos 'khor yang
rtse/ rgyang 'bum mo che/ lha rtse chos sde/ rtag brtan phun tshogs gling / ri khrod jo nang / snying ri'i sgrub sde khag /rta nag thub bstan/ bzhad thub bstan yangs
pa can/ rta nag sgrol ma phug /shangs rgya tsho chos sde/ dben dgon ri khrod/ srad brgyud pa/ srad dgon khra/ srad mkhar chen gyi sgrub ste/ srad chos 'khor gling rnams kyi
rten gsum rnams la mchod 'bul dang / bla ma mtshan snyan che ba phal che bar bsngo zhus dang / dgon pa rnams la mang ja'i bsnyen bkur ba bcas bsgrubs shing / de dag gi
dus kyi tshe'ang / thog mar bdun phrag gnyis tsam gyi bar la nyin re bzhin me tog gi dbyibs lta bu yod pa'i gangs zim bu cung zad re babs pa dang / khyad par bdun tshigs
re re rdzogs mtshams kyi dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gshegs gsol gyi nyin snga phyi thams cad du nyi gur phub cing kha dog lnga ldan gyi 'ja' shar ba dang / bdun tshigs
gnyis pa'i kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gshegs gsol tshar rjes bdag cag 'ga' zhig gis sku gdung rin po che'i mdun lam zab bla ma mchod pa'i sgo nas dbang bzhi blang ba sogs
bgyis pa'i tshe'ang glo bur du kha dog lnga ldan gyi 'ja' sprin 'dra shar song zhes phyi rol na yod

pa kun gyis zer zhing / gang ltar yang bdun tshigs gnyis pa rdzogs pa'i rjes su/ spyir khang steng la sogs pa'i sa dul ba rnams su sa chog ma byas kyang chog mod/ 'on kyang
byas pa nyid phun sum tshogs pa'i yan lag tu 'gyur bar sems nas/ sa chog mdor bsdus tsam sngon du btang nas gdung khang brtsigs shing / de'ang bu ston gyis mdzad pa'i mi
'khrugs pa'i gshin po rjes 'dzin sogs nas bsreg khang brtsig tshul mi 'dra ba 'ga' re gsungs pa bzhin gang byas kyang rung mod/ 'on kyang thar paN gyi kye rdor dus tha'i
cho gar myang 'das mchod rten gyi dbyibs su brtsigs par bshad pa bzhin/ gdung khang myang 'das mchod rten gyi dbyibs su brtsigs pa dang / sbyin sreg kyang kha cig gis 'jig
rten pa'i gtam dpe la khungs su bcol nas sbyin sreg gcig kho na las mang po mi 'dod pa yod mod/ rang gzhan gyi grub mtha' mang po'i sngon gyi phyag len la/ 'byor pas lcogs
na sbyin sreg gsum bzhi tsam yang bya ba'i srol byung 'dug pa ltar/ de ltar byas pa la 'gal ba ci'ang yod par mi sems te/ rang rang gis lha de dang der bsgoms nas bsreg
rdzas 'bul ba yin pas blo gu dogs pa de 'dra mi dgos pa'i phyir ro/ /de'i phyir na kye rdor dang kun rig gnyis kyi sgo nas sbyin sreg 'bul bar brtsams shing / thab kyi
thig tshon yang rgyud sde gong 'og gi babs dang bstun te 'og tu kun rig dang / de'i steng rgya lcogs lta bu'i steng du kye rdo rje'i sbyin sreg gi dkyil 'khor bris pa dang
/ sngar kye rdo rje'i sgo nas sku gdung rin po cher gnas yig gdags pa dang / rnam snang dges pa rdo rjer bskyed pa sogs grub zin pa yin na'ang / kun rig gi sngon 'gro'i
rdo rje sems dpa' bskyed pa dang / gnas yig gdags pa sogs bgyis kyang mi 'gal bar sems nas hor zla gsum pa phyi ma'i tshes drug gi nyin/ kun rig gi rnal 'byor pa

rnams kyis sku gdung rin po che rdo rje sems dpar bskyed pa dang / gnas yig gdags pa sogs bgyis pa dang / de nub mchod pa'i bye brag 'ga' zhig dang bcas te sku gdung rin po
che gdung khang du spyan drangs pa dang / de'i phyi nyin tshe bdun gyi snga dro mkhas dang grub pa'i gtsug rgyan khang gsar mkhan rin po che ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan
pa tshogs kyi rdo rje slob dpon chen por gdan drangs shing / bsnyen pa song ba'i dge slong bcu phrag gcig dang bcas pas dpal kye rdo rje'i sgo nas sku gdung rin po
cher zhugs 'bul ba dang / lung rigs smra ba sprul sku shes rab rgya mtshos dbu byas pa'i dge slong kha shas kyis bcom ldan 'das kun tu rig pa'i sgo nas sku gdung rin po cher
zhugs 'bul ba'i zhabs togs rgyud sde nas ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin du bsgrubs shing / de'i tshe'ang thog mar sbyin sreg gi mgo tshugs pa nas bzung ste/ de nyin nam mkha'
thams cad kha dog sna tshogs pa'i sprin gyis gang ba dang / kha dog lnga ldan gyi 'ja' ring thung gsum tsam shar ba dang / dgon gsham gyi grong pa rnams kyis yar bltas
pa'i tshe gdung khang gi steng du 'ja' kha dog lnga ldan gnyis zug 'dug ces gleng ba dang / me tog gi dbyibs lta bu yod pa'i gangs thar thor 'dra'ang skabs skabs su babs
pa dang / thog mar zhugs 'bul ba'i tshe me rang 'bar lta bu'i shin tu 'bar sla ba dang / de'i dus kyi dud pa ni thog mar gdung khang gi steng du 'khyil ba snyam byed cing
/ de ma thag nas dud pa rnams dgon pa'i shar ngos kyi bskor lam gyi steng gi nam mkhar song zhing / de nas dgon pa la g.yas skor lan cig byas nas/ mthar nam mkha'i 'ja'
sprin rnams dang dbyer med du 'dres pa'i tshul gyis yal bar gyur pa dang / me lce rnams kyang kha dog dkar gsal 'od dang ldan zhing / gzhan du 'khyag 'khyog med par rtse
mo rnams rtsa ljang gshibs pa ltar gyen kho nar 'bar ba'i ya mtshan pa dang /

skabs skabs su bkra shis pa'i ri mo'i dbyibs lta bur 'bar ba dang / khyad par dri bzang pos dgon pa'i gling thams cad la khyab pas skye bo mtha' dag ngo mtshar ba'i gnas la
bkod par gyur to/ /de nyin mkhan rin po che khri thog pa'i mdun du gser zangs las grub pa'i ston pa'i sku dang / phyag ting dngul thag can/ rgya rol che legs cha/ zangs
bum dngul kham kha rgyan dang bcas pa/ dngul gyi ting phor bdun tshar/ gos chen ser po gser Tam can gyi sku stod/ gos chen gser Tam gyis mtha' lcags byas pa'i sku gzan/ mgo
snam gyi zhabs chags 'ja' chen/ phying khra/ ljon ja 'khor drug gnyis/ 'bras dkar ltang bcas phul ba dang / de byings thams cad la'ang rnam gzhag dang / yon 'bul la sogs
pa'i bsnyen bkur zab par bgyis so/ /de nas mchod pa dang bcas te zhag bdun song ba'i mthar gdung khang zhal phye ba na gdung rus ni phal che ba zla ba ltar dkar ba dang
/ mthing shun ltar sngo ba'ang re gnyis tsam snang la/ gang ltar yang gdung rus nyung tsam zhig las mi snang bas thams cad yid mi ches pa lta bur byung pa ni/ ring bsrel
dang bcas pa'i gdung ngo mtshar ba rnams bdag cag skal ba dman pa rnams kyi bsod nams kyis mi 'chun par mthong nas dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis spyan drangs par
gdon mi za'o/ /gang ltar yang rgyud sde rnams nas ji ltar bshad pa bzhin gyis gdung rus rnams btus te/ dpal kye rdo rje'i sgo nas bsgrubs pa'i bum chu dang / dge slong
brgyad tsam gyi kun rig gi sgo nas bum pa tshul bzhin du bsgrubs pa'i chus yang dang yang du sku khrus gsol zhing / slar gdung rus zhib par 'dur te rin po che'i phye ma dang
/ dri zhim pos sprus pa'i

'jim pa gtsang ma dang lhan cig tu bsres te/ 'jim pa byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas bla ma yi dam sangs rgyas byang sems chos srung nor lha dang bcas pa'i sku 'dra mang
du spar btab cing / de rnams la'ang rab tu gnas pa brgya tshar 'gro nges bgyis pa dang / yang gdung thal rnams la'ang gdung rus shin tu zhib pa phran bu 'dres snang bas/
de dag kyang shin tu zhib par 'dur te/ dri zhim po'i chus sprus pa'i 'jim pa dang bsres te/ 'jim pa byin rlabs sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas/ rigs lnga'i sa bon dang / gtsug
tor dri med kyi gzungs dang / rten 'brel snying po bcas kyi gzungs gzhug dang ldan pa'i sAtstsha 'bum ther cung med tsam bzhengs shing / de thams cad la'ang rab tu gnas
pa bgyis pa dang / khyad par lo de'i hor zla dgu pa'i nang phyi rten khang bu brtsegs pa'i mchod rten bzhengs par/ thog mar sa chog mdor bsdus dang / sa bdag lto 'phye'i
thig dang / gter bum 'jug pa sogs sngon du 'gro ba'i mchod rten gyi phyags tshad rnams ngor chen rdo rje 'chang yab sras kyi bzhed pa ji lta ba bzhin du bgyis pa dang
/ de'i nang du'ang mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i srog shing la ji skad bshad pa ltar gyi gzungs 'jug pa dang / 'bri ba sogs dang / khyad par bla ma brgyud pa'i mtshan 'bum
nas bzung / chos srung nor lha dang bkra shis kyi bar thams cad go rim ma 'phyugs pa gong ma'i phyag len ji lta ba bzhin dang / 'og tu gnod sbyin 'khor lo dang nor lha'i
gter bum bcas dang / khyad par sAtstsha rnams kyang yongs su rdzogs par bzhugs su gsol zhing / de dag kyang sa rdo spungs pa lta bu ma yin par re re nas pad spungs mchod
rten shar du bstan te bsgrigs pa dang / star re bsgrigs tshar ba'i rjes su sAtstsha rab gnas mdor bsdus

re'ang bgyis pa dang / de dag gi bar thams cad kyang bsang dang shugs phye kho nas bkang ba sogs mdor na tshul ldan bzhin du bzhengs pa'i mchod rten la/ lung rig smra ba sprul
sku shes rab rgya mtsho sogs dge slong bcu gsum gyis tshe dpag tu med pa la brten pa'i rab tu gnas pa bgyis pa dang / yang hor zla gsum pa phyi ma'i yar tshes nas bzung
ste rta nag lha bris pa bos te/ gtsug lag khang du bsham rgyu'i dus thang rin po che che legs shin tu sgros gtsang bar bzhengs te gong gsham zhal khebs thams cad kyang
phun sum tshogs par bgyis pa la/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po dbur bzhugs pa'i bdag cag dge slong kha shas dang bcas pas tshe dpag med la brten
pa'i rab tu gnas pa bgyis te/ hor zla lnga pa'i tshes bcu bdun gyi nyin e waM pa'i gtsug lag khang du spyan drangs/ de nyin bdag gis gtsug lag khang der mchod pa'i phreng
ba brgya phrag dang bcas shing / dge 'dun gang yod kyis bla ma mchod pa tshogs pa la/ dge slong re re la phyag 'gyed dngul Tam re dang bcas pa'i bsnyen bskur phun sum
tshogs pa dang / mkhan rin po che khri thog pa'ang tshogs bsngor gdan zhus kyi 'bul ba gang zab bcas bsgrubs pa dang / zhal chems su yod pa'i gnas bcu'i zhal thang dang /
gshed dmar dkyil thang rnams kyang shin tu sgros gtsang bar bzhengs pa dang / yang hor zla lnga pa'i nang rtse gdong nas zangs rdung mkhas pa mi bzhi bos te/ nang rten 'dra
sku rin po che gser zangs las grub pa sku dngos mda' tshad tsam khri rgyab dang bcas pa dang / mdzod mkhyen rab bzang po dang gnyer sher seng gnyis nas rin chen gnyis
pa 'degs srang brgyad cu las grub pa'i lha babs mchod rten mda' tshad tsam pa la rin po che du ma'i phras mdzes

par spud pa bcas kyang zla ba gsum gyi khongs su shin tu sgros gtsang bar bzhengs grub pa la/ yungs 'bru lta bu'i ring bsrel dang / sku 'dra li ma dang / byin rten khyad par
du 'phags pa 'ga' zhig dang / srog shing mtshan nyid dang ldan pa dang / bla ma brgyud pa'i mtshan 'bum nas bzung ste/ bkra shis kyi bar rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i
gzungs bsam las 'das pa dang / sku gdung yid bzhin nor bu'i cha shas las grub pa'i sku 'dra rnams kyis phyur bur bkang ste/ tshul bzhin du bsgrubs pa'i nor lha'i gter bum
dang / gnod sbyin 'khor los zhabs bsdams pa'i bar rje btsun gong ma'i phyag len ji lta ba bzhin bgyis pa la/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang rnal 'byor 'jam dpal bzang po tshogs
kyi rdo rje slob dpon chen por phebs te bdag cag dge slong bcu phrag gcig dang bcas pas dpal kye rdo rje la brten pa'i rab gnas nyin gang ma zhig mdzad de byin rlabs kyi
gzi 'od 'bar bar mdzad pa dang / slar yang bdag cag dge slong bcu gsum gyis dpal kye rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te sgrub mchod dang 'brel bar rab gnas
shin tu rgyas pa nyin lnga pa zhig kyang bgyis pa yin no/ /de dag gi tshe bzo bo thams cad la'ang skabs skabs su ston mo dang / rgyun gyi bza' btung sogs shin tu zab pa
dang / yon dang gnang sbyin la sogs pas shin tu yid tshim par byas so/ de dag gi skabs su'ang gegs kyi rnam pa cung zad tsam yang med cing / mthun rkyen rnams kyang 'bad
rtsol med par rang shugs kyis 'grigs pa sogs mdor na tshogs chung dus bde blag tu grub pa'ang rje nyid kyi thugs rje kho nas yin par gdon mi za'o/ /gzhan yang ldan ma mtshams
pa dpal ldan don grub par zla ba drug gi mtshams brgyags phul te/ sngar zhal chems su stsal ba'i 'khor

lo bde mchog lU hi pa'i bsnyen tshad mthar phyin par bgyis pa dang / yang gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos dbyings su bsdus pa'i tshul bstan pa nas bzung deng sang gi bar phal che
bar zla re bzhin dus chen dang bstun te dge slong kha shes kyis bla ma mchod pa ma chag pa dang / chu phag hor zla gsum par lo dus kyi dus chen dang bstun te bdag cag dge
slong bcus dpal kun tu rig pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs te sgrub cing mchod pa dang / bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba dang bcas nyin lnga pa zhig bgyis pa
dang / khyad par zla de'i tshes bcu bdun gyi nyin dge slong nyung bsdus kyi ser sbreng dang bcas te 'dra sku rin po che lam 'bras lha khang du gdan drangs te gos chen gyi
sku ber la sogs pa'i na bzas bklubs te bzhugs su gsol zhing / de'i sku mdun du rin chen gnyis pa 'degs srang bdun dang zho bdun las grub pa'i phud kong / dngul srang bdun
dang zho bzhi las grub pa'i spyi blugs/ dngul srung bcu bzhi las grub pa'i kar 'dzin gyi steng zhal kar yu ring zas snas bkang ba/ dngul srang dgu dang zho do las grub
pa'i bzed zhal/ rdo dril gser mgo can/ Da ma ru dngul dkris can/ phyag ting dngul thag can/ dngul las grub pa'i nang mchod ka pA la/ dngul srang nyer gcig las grub pa'i bum
pa cha la kha rgyan bum gos dang bcas pa/ dngul srang drug dang zho brgyad las grub pa'i 'bru spar rnams kyang sbyor 'jags zhus pa dang / de nyin nas bzung nyin gsum la
rnam lnga brgya mchod dang bcas te dge slong bcus bla ma mchod pa bgyis par bsnyen bkur phun sum tshogs pa bsgrubs pa dang / yang tshes bcu bdun gyi nyin e waM pa'i gtsug
lag khang du dge 'dun gang yod kyi bla ma mchod pa tshogs par brgya mchod dang / mang ja dang gral 'gyed la

sogs pa'i bsnyen bkur shin tu bzang bar bgyis pa yin no/ /gzhan phyogs tha dad nas kyang mgon po gang gi thugs sras rnams kyis thugs kyi dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i slad
du rnam par dkar ba'i sgo 'phar yangs por phyes pa'i tshul rnams ni re re nas smos kyis mi lang ngo / /mdor na bka' drin gyi cha shas phra mo tsam yang 'di nas byang chub
bar du gzhal dka' ba'i bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa yon tan rin po che'i phung por gyur pa 'di'i phyogs su bdag cag rnams kyis lus longs spyod dus gsum du bsags
pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang bcas pa thams cad bskal pa'am bskal pa las lhag par nyin re bzhin 'bum phrag du mar btang yang chung ba'i skyon kho na las ma mchis mod/ re zhig
bdag cag rnams kyi nus pa ni de tsam du zad do/ /de ltar bdag cag gi dpal ldan bla ma dam pa 'di ni don dam par bskal pa dpag tu med pa'i sngon rol nas skye 'chi'i spros
pa thams cad yongs su spangs kyang / kun rdzob tu bdag lta bu'i gdul bya rtag 'dzin can rnams 'dul ba'i slad du/ gzugs sku'i bkod pa chos dbyings su bsdus pa'i tshul bstan
par gyur mod/ 'on kyang 'khor ba ji srid gnas pa de srid du sprul pa sna tshogs pa'i sgo nas sems can gyi don rgyun chad med par 'bad med lhun grub kyi tshul du mdzad
pa yin te/ spyod 'jug las/ yid bzhin nor bu dpag bsam shing / /ji ltar re ba yongs skong ba/ /de bzhin gdul byar smon lam gyi/ /dbang gis rgyal ba'i skur snang ngo / /zhes
dang / rdo rje gur las/ gdul ba'i 'jig rten mthong nas ni/ /'di yi gzugs ni du mar byed/ /sangs rgyas sems can skyabs bzhed pas/ /sangs rgyas gar ni rol par mdzad/ /ces
gsungs pa ltar ro/ /nyin byed nub rir nye ba na/ /grib ma'i tshogs rnams 'ong ba bzhin/ /mgon khyod zhing gzhan gshegs bzhed tshe/ /ltas rnams

bos pa bzhin du lhags/ /kye ma srid pa'i phun tshogs kun/ /mgon khyod thugs rje las byung na/ /de nyid zhi bar mngon phyogs tshe/ /mi dge'i mtshan ma cis mi 'byung / /gzod
nas bdud bzhi bcom pa'i tshul/ /slar yang gsal bar ston pa'i slad/ /re zhig sku tshe byin brlabs pas/ /'chi bdag bdud kyang pham par byas/ /'on kyang gdul bya'i chu gter
ni/ /rin chen gling du bsgyur zin pas/ /gzhan pa'i gdul bya la brtse ba'i/ /gzigs pa dus las yol ma gyur/ /de tshe ye shes sems dpa' nyid/ /mngon sum bzhugs pa'i rten rnams
kyang / /skyo ba'i ngal ba rab 'dzin na/ /tha mal gzhan rnams smos mi dgos/ /de nas sdug bsngal du ma'i gter/ /'gro 'di'i bden 'dzin gzhom pa'i slad/ /rdo rje'i sku yang
mi rtag pa'i/ /dus ngan mun pa de 'dra shar/ /kye ma sdom gsum rtsa ba brtan/ /byams brtse'i yal ga rab brkyangs nas/ /phan bde'i 'bras bu kun stsol ba'i/ /dpag bsam shing
de gang du song / /kyi hud dam chos gzi 'od kyis/ /'khor ba'i chu gter skems byed cing / /thar pa'i lam bzang gsal mdzad pa'i/ /smra ba'i nyi ma gang du bzhud/ /kye
ma ma la 'di lta bu/ /mngon sum mig gis ma mthong bar/ /'chi ba'i go skabs ma rnyed pa'i/ /bdag cag las ngan ci zhig bsags/ /ltas dang ngo mtshar mtha' yas pas/ /sa gzhi
nam mkha' kun bkang yang / /bdag cag khyod dang bral ba yi/ /snying la mi bzod dug tu byas/ /gzod nas sems can thams cad la/ /phan pa sgrub par zhal 'ches na/ /bdag cag mgon
gyis phongs pa yi/ /khur 'di khyod kyis bzod lags sam/ /'on kyang snying nas gsol btab na/ /mgon khyod thugs rje byin rlabs la/ /gzhar yang nye ring med pa 'dis/ /sems
la ngal bso cung zad thob/ /'di lta'i gnas skabs mthong gyur kyang / /da dung rtag 'dzin ma zhig pa'i/ /bdag 'dra'i

mi gzugs dud 'gro rnams/ /srid pa'i mtsho las bsgral du gsol/ /srid gsum mchod pa'i zhing mchog tu/ /bzhag pa'i sku gdung rin po cher/ /rgyud nas ji skad gsungs pa ltar/ /sri
zhu'i bya ba rdzogs par bsgrubs/ /khyad par bla ma yi dam gnyis/ /dbyer med gcig tu bskyed byas nas/ /sgrub cing mchod pa la sogs pa'i/ /bsod nams sgo 'phar ci yang phyes/
/dbus gtsang dag pa'i mkhar shar ba'i/ /bla ma lha dang dge 'dun la/ /rnyed dang bkur sti stob pa sogs/ /bsod nams ji ltar nus bzhin bsags/ /dad pa'i chu yis snying
brlan pa'i/ /skal bzang bsod nams zhing mchog tu/ /chos sku'i rten dang gzugs kyi sku/ /bris dang 'bur du bcas pa bzhengs/ /de sogs rjes kyi bya ba kun/ /'bad med lhun gyis
grub pa dang / /ngo mtshar ltas kyang mang snang bas/ /mgon des rjes su bzung snyam byed/ /dkar po'i las kyis dbul ba yi/ /bdag cag ngan 'gror lhung dogs nas/ /bsod nams
cung zhig gsog pa'i slad/ /'di 'dra'i gnas skabs bstan nam snyam/ /ji srid 'khor ba ma stongs par/ /de srid gang 'dul skur bstan nas/ /'gro ba'i re 'dod skong ba ni/ /yid
bzhin nor bus mtshon ma yin/ /ngan song lta bur mgon med pa'i/ /bdag cag gdung ba sel ba'i slad/ /sprul pa'i nyin byed myur shar te/ /phan bde'i padmo rgyas par gsol/
/bdag kyang byang chub ma thob par/ /khyod las skyabs gzhan yod min pas/ /de phyir thugs rje'i lcags kyu yis/ /'bral med rjes su gzung du gsol/ /de ltar dzambu'i rkang 'thung
gis nye bar mtshan pa'i ljongs 'dir/ 'gro ba rnams kyi ma rig pa'i mun pa mtha' dag sel ba dang / lung dang rtogs pa'i 'dab stong rnam par rgyas pa'i slad du bsam bzhin
du sku'i skye ba bzhes pa 'dren mchog

smra ba'i nyi ma mtshan brjod par dka' ba don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po'i zhal snga nas kyi rnam par thar pa so skye'i blo'i spyod yul du gyur pa rnams re zhig bkod zin to/ /slar smras pa/ mkhas pas mkhas pa'i bdud rtsi'i zer gyis lung
rtogs chu gter 'phel bgyid cing / /grub pas grub pa'i gtsug na rab 'dzegs mchog thun dngos grub sbyin mkhas pa/ /dran pas dran pa tsam gyi mod la srid zhi'i mun pa kun
sel ba/ /bla ma'i bla ma thams cad gzigs der slar yang gus pas phyag bgyi'o/ /gang de'i gsang gsum me long gcig nyid du/ /sras bcas rgyal kun tshud pa'i ngo mtshar gtam/
/mtha' dag brjod la 'jam dpal dpa' bo yis/ /dbyangs can grogs su sbran yang zad pa med/ /'on kyang dngos grub rtsa ba bla ma ru/ /shes pa'i blo yis cha tsam bsnyad pa 'dis/
/mdzub mos nam mkha' bstan pa ji bzhin du/ /yon tan bsam mi khyab tsam rtogs par byed/ /grogs dag las nyon rab rib cher rgyas pa'i/ /mun pa'i khang bu dag las phyir thon
te/ /rnam par thar pa 'di la ltos shig dang / /srid pas byas pa'i 'jigs pa 'jil bar byed/ /'dir 'bad dge ba nyin mor byed pa'i gzis/ /'gro ba'i las nyon mun pa kun bsal
te/ /yang dag snang ba dam pas 'jig rten na/ /phan bde'i dga' ston ci yang 'jo bar shog /dpal ldan bla ma dam pa gsum gyi rtogs pa brjod pa ngo mtshar me tog g.yo ba'i
'khri shing byin rlabs 'dod dgu'i 'byung gnas las/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin bkra shis grags pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas
kyi rtogs pa brjod pa'i yal 'dab ste gnyis pa'o// //
